# DeepSeek V4 AMD Pretrain

Status: direct TorchTitan DeepSeek-V4-Flash canaries now train on both `4xMI350` and `8xMI350` without Primus. The active 4xMI350 target for this thread remains `S=4096`, `GBS=128`, MBS tunable, and `~12.2k` tok/GPU/s (`~48.8k` node tok/s on 4 GPUs). The promoted 4-layer canary baseline still clears that gate at `12,570.33` tok/GPU/s steps 4-6, but the current work is the harder `flash_12layer_ceiling_probe`. The fair current-stack hot-helper count gate rejects reducing standard-EP helper execute from top-8 to top-6/top-4 at `MBS=8`, so the MoE/EP path should keep top-8 and make the hot/cold/helper row layout cheaper instead of shrinking the helper set.

Cross-model retained hot-helper evidence is tracked in [`changesets/balanced_moe_cross_model_retained_perf_gates_20260612.md`](changesets/balanced_moe_cross_model_retained_perf_gates_20260612.md), summarized for automation in [`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_cross_model_retained_perf_status_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_cross_model_retained_perf_status_20260612.json), and guarded by the model-surface audit [`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_model_surface_status_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_model_surface_status_20260612.json). The current clean apples-to-apples backend table is [`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_backend_table_cleanrerun_20260613_fresh4.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_backend_table_cleanrerun_20260613_fresh4.json). It supersedes the older mixed-row comparison table for DeepSeek/Qwen baseline decisions. The next corrected baseline table must split DeepSeek into two explicit model surfaces: MTP1 and no-MTP historical control. The DeepSeek helper-MBS8 row was rechecked three more times in [`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_recheck2_20260613_rep1.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_recheck2_20260613_rep1.json), [`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_recheck2_20260613_rep2.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_recheck2_20260613_rep2.json), and [`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_recheck2_20260613_rep3.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_recheck2_20260613_rep3.json). Fresh4 plus those three repeats cluster at `7,381.92` tok/GPU/s steps 2-20 and `7,508.65` tok/GPU/s steps 13-20; same-host recheck on the old `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu` host was blocked by the strict clean-node guard because a non-GPU `nexus-titan-lighthouse` container was running ([`run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_dosonle_recheck_20260613.json`](run_artifacts/balanced_moe_deepseek_helper8_mbs8_dosonle_recheck_20260613.json)). Source/log audit explains the mismatch: the 20260608 `~8.5k` row built an `81,244,314,368` parameter model, while current source defaults DeepSeek MTP to one module and fresh4 built `87,079,924,032` parameters with `dsv4_num_mtp_modules=default`. That is `+5,835,609,664` parameters (`+7.18%`) and about `+19.4 GiB` peak memory. Treat the old `~8.5k` row as historical no-MTP evidence; reproduce it only with the explicit `deepseek_nomtp` table surface. The corrected table surface uses `deepseek_mtp1`.

| Model surface | Reduced topology | Retained standard-EP top-8 helper result | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| DeepSeek-V4 Flash | 12 layers, 256 experts, top-k 6, first-12 compress ratios `[1,1,4,128,4,128,4,128,4,128,4,128]` | Fresh4 helper uplifts at MBS1/2/4 are `+8.38%`, `+25.66%`, `+34.41%`; MBS8 no-helper fails before metric, while helper reaches `7,347.98` tok/GPU/s full-window and `7,529.00` late-window (`~7.38k`/`~7.51k` across fresh4 plus three repeats) | clean table + rechecked MBS8 |
| Qwen3.5-397B-A17B | 8 layers, 512 routed experts, top-k 10 + 1 shared, `hidden=4096`, GQA `32Q/2KV`, `head_dim=256` | Fresh4 helper is `-0.76%`, `+11.95%`, `+20.74%`, `+17.86%` vs plain at MBS1/2/4/8; Primus raw top-k is faster than helper across the clean table | clean table evidence |
| Kimi-K2.6 | 6 layers, 384 routed experts, top-k 8 + 1 shared, `moe_inter=2048`, MLA, native `hidden=7168` | MBS1/MBS2 top-8 helper uplifts `+5.48%`/`+7.70%`; raw Primus-Turbo no-helper reaches `4,836.63`/`5,704.93` tok/GPU/s; MBS4 does not fit for raw TurboEP or top-8 helper | retained Kimi MBS1/MBS2 gate |

Kimi now has a real native-hidden-7168 TorchTitan training surface and retained MBS1/MBS2 gates. The first MBS4 raw Primus-Turbo no-helper fit check fails before the first metric with HSA out-of-resources in backward ([`run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_primus_turbo_nohelper_mbs4_failure_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_primus_turbo_nohelper_mbs4_failure_20260612.json)), and the matched MBS4 standard-EP top-8 helper check also fails before the first metric with a 16 GiB backward OOM ([`run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_standard_ep_top8_helper_mbs4_failure_20260613.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_standard_ep_top8_helper_mbs4_failure_20260613.json)). Backend-native MORI or Primus-Turbo speedup claims across all three model families should distinguish "Kimi MBS1/MBS2 covered" from a full Kimi MBS ladder.

Primus-Turbo raw-top-k no-helper baseline check: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_primus_turbo_nohelper_cross_model_mbs1_mbs8_20step_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_primus_turbo_nohelper_cross_model_mbs1_mbs8_20step_20260612.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_primus_deepep_nohelper_mbs4_mbs8_20step_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_primus_deepep_nohelper_mbs4_mbs8_20step_20260612.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_qwen397b_a17b_primus_deepep_nohelper_mbs4_mbs8_20step_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_qwen397b_a17b_primus_deepep_nohelper_mbs4_mbs8_20step_20260612.json), corrected Qwen MBS4 rerun/profile [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_qwen397b_primus_turbo_mbs2_mbs4_rerun_profile_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_qwen397b_primus_turbo_mbs2_mbs4_rerun_profile_20260612.json), corrected Qwen MBS8 rerun [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_qwen397b_primus_turbo_mbs8_cleanrerun_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_qwen397b_primus_turbo_mbs8_cleanrerun_20260612.json), and Kimi rows [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_standard_ep_hothelper_primus_turbo_mbs1_20step_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_standard_ep_hothelper_primus_turbo_mbs1_20step_20260612.json) / [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_standard_ep_hothelper_primus_turbo_mbs1_mbs2_20step_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_kimi_k2_6_standard_ep_hothelper_primus_turbo_mbs1_mbs2_20step_20260612.json) confirm the retained no-helper rows above were plain standard EP, not DeepEP/TurboEP. The Primus-Turbo no-helper runs use `TORCHTITAN_STANDARD_EP_BACKEND_NORMAL_TOPK_DISPATCH_PERMUTE=1` and `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_PLAN_BACKEND=primus_turbo`, which hand the normal token-major `[tokens, top_k]` EP edge to Primus-Turbo. Source and runtime smoke identify the active lower backend as the in-tree `TurboEPBackend`: `PRIMUS_TURBO_MOE_DISPATCH_COMBINE_BACKEND` is unset, default selection is `TURBO`, `TurboEPBackend` is available, and optional external `DeepEPBackend` is unavailable because standalone `deep_ep`/`deepep` is absent. A fresh external-DeepEP availability check is recorded in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_primus_external_deepep_backend_availability_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_primus_external_deepep_backend_availability_20260612.json): the active TorchTitan and Primus images expose `primus_turbo`, but not `deep_ep`, `deepep`, `uccl`, or `rocshmem`, and Primus-Turbo's experimental DeepEP README documents MI300/gfx942-only support while the current nodes are MI350/gfx950. External `DeepEPBackend` therefore remains a dependency-blocked, not-yet-measured column, not part of the retained table. Qwen MBS4 raw TurboEP now has a clean corrected 20-step row at `15,745.63` tok/GPU/s steps 2-20, superseding the old `11,799.62` row. Qwen MBS8 raw TurboEP now has a corrected current-source 20-step row at `16,702.90` tok/GPU/s steps 2-20 and `17,275.64` steps 13-20, superseding the old allocator-contaminated `11,650.90` row. Kimi MBS1/MBS2 raw TurboEP reaches `4,836.63`/`5,704.93` tok/GPU/s steps 2-20, beating both plain standard EP and top-8 helper at those low-MBS points; Kimi MBS4 raw TurboEP and standard-EP top-8 helper both fail before first metric. Qwen MBS8 still runs close to the memory cliff (`277.34 GiB`, `24` allocator-retry warning lines), so raw TurboEP is a corrected baseline column, not proof that raw top-k EP replaces native hot-helper partitioning.

The fully rerun fresh4 table below uses one harness, one node, helper SDMA, common expandable allocator, and 20-step windows for all DeepSeek/Qwen rows. It supersedes earlier non-reproducible Qwen rows and the older DeepSeek helper-MBS8 table value; those older artifacts remain useful historical evidence but should not be mixed into this backend comparison without a config-diff audit.

| Model surface | MBS | Plain no-helper standard EP | Primus-Turbo `TurboEPBackend` no-helper raw top-k EP | Standard-EP top-8 hot-helper | Primus vs plain | Primus vs helper |
| --- | ---: | ---: | ---: | ---: | ---: | ---: |

| DeepSeek-V4 Flash 12-layer | 2 | `4,812.99` tok/GPU/s | `6,060.80` tok/GPU/s | `6,047.89` tok/GPU/s | `+25.93%` | `+0.21%` |
| DeepSeek-V4 Flash 12-layer | 4 | `5,187.05` tok/GPU/s | `6,784.80` tok/GPU/s | `6,971.76` tok/GPU/s | `+30.80%` | `-2.68%` |
| DeepSeek-V4 Flash 12-layer | 8 | fails before metric | `7,049.86` tok/GPU/s | `7,347.98` tok/GPU/s | changes fit boundary | `-4.06%` |
| Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 8-layer | 1 | `8,897.24` tok/GPU/s | `10,559.85` tok/GPU/s | `8,829.57` tok/GPU/s | `+18.69%` | `+19.60%` |
| Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 8-layer | 2 | `10,497.52` tok/GPU/s | `13,195.61` tok/GPU/s | `11,752.39` tok/GPU/s | `+25.70%` | `+12.28%` |
| Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 8-layer | 4 | `11,835.55` tok/GPU/s | `15,708.61` tok/GPU/s | `14,290.69` tok/GPU/s | `+32.72%` | `+9.92%` |
| Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 8-layer | 8 | `13,582.17` tok/GPU/s | `16,657.03` tok/GPU/s | `16,008.45` tok/GPU/s | `+22.64%` | `+4.05%` |

| Kimi-K2.6 6-layer | 2 | `5,059.56` tok/GPU/s | `5,704.93` tok/GPU/s | `5,449.39` tok/GPU/s | `+12.76%` | `+4.69%` |
| Kimi-K2.6 6-layer | 4 | not retained | fails before first metric, HSA OOR with `258 MB` free | fails before first metric, 16 GiB backward OOM | n/a | n/a |

Read: Primus-Turbo `TurboEPBackend` is a real raw-top-k/no-helper EP baseline. In the clean fresh4 table it helps DeepSeek across MBS1/2/4, changes the DeepSeek MBS8 fit boundary, and wins Qwen MBS1/2/4/8 outright. Standard-EP top-8 helper still wins DeepSeek MBS4/MBS8 and is the only no-helper-to-helper mechanism that changes the DeepSeek no-helper fit cliff into a robust pass, but its current-source MBS8 level is `~7.4k` tok/GPU/s, not the older `~8.5k` historical row. Kimi remains covered only at MBS1/MBS2; MBS4 is a fit failure for both raw TurboEP and top-8 helper on the native-hidden surface. The first mixed wrapper gate that preserved standard-EP top-8 hot-helper but delegated the normal/cold raw top-k dispatch+permute edge to Primus-Turbo also rejects promotion: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_primus_turbo_hothelper_mbs8_20step_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_primus_turbo_hothelper_mbs8_20step_20260612.json) completes 20 steps at `6,434.89` tok/GPU/s and `318.57 TFLOPs/GPU` over steps 2-20, trailing both fresh4 raw Turbo no-helper and helper. The matching profile [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_primus_turbo_hothelper_mbs8_profile_steps2_20260612.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_primus_turbo_hothelper_mbs8_profile_steps2_20260612.json) shows why: the mixed path still pays standard count exchange/hot-mask planning and the existing helper-hot graph, while adding visible Turbo dispatch+permute (`162.458 ms` rank-max) and Turbo unpermute/combine (`201.249 ms`). The optimization target remains preserving the hot/cold/helper owner-compact partition and making MORI/Primus-Turbo native to that layout; simply swapping the raw normal top-k EP edge is not enough.

Historical 20260608 note: a separate 12-layer 8xMI350 standard-EP hot-expert helper-execute top-8 run with MORI/SDMA hot-weight transport, attention-only selective activation checkpointing, and the Triton backward weighted-scatter backend reported higher throughput in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json): steps 2-20 averaged `8,518.84` tok/GPU/s, `68,150.74` node tok/s, `431.31 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `251.97 GiB` peak logged memory; steps 13-20 averaged `8,630.66` tok/GPU/s and `436.97 TFLOPs/GPU`. Fresh4 plus three same-surface helper-MBS8 repeats on `do-vunguyen-mi350-gpu` did not reproduce this level and instead averaged `7,381.92`/`7,508.65` tok/GPU/s for steps 2-20/13-20 with `~271.27 GiB` peak. The current-source same-host check on `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu` was blocked by the clean-node guard because a `nexus-titan-lighthouse` Docker container was already running with 0% GPU/VRAM. Do not use the 20260608 row in the backend comparison table until a same-host clean rerun or a config/source/env diff explains it. The matched sparse profile [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_currentbest_sparse_profile_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_currentbest_sparse_profile_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json) remains useful diagnostic evidence: backward `5.959 s`, forward `2.047 s`, loss `0.409 s`, optimizer `0.0465 s`, Sparse SharedKV backward `1.701 s` (`C4` `1.230 s`, mostly query-recompute), dense attention backward `0.819 s`, dense linear backward `0.708 s` with `attention.wo` `0.426 s`, standard-EP combine `0.316 s`, and hot-helper backward `0.311 s`. The same-scope pp_vis traces close the coarse-bubble suspicion: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_currentbest_ppvis_fbscope_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_currentbest_ppvis_fbscope_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json) reports a `6.073 ms` rank-max residual, and the current-best hot-VJP detail trace [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_currentbest_mbs8_hotvjp_detail_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_currentbest_mbs8_hotvjp_detail_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json) reports `5.830 ms` rank-max residual inside an `8228.561 ms` forward/backward call (`0.0708%`). So the earlier `5.70%` pp_vis read was step-scope loss/bookkeeping accounting, not pipeline idle. The lower-memory reference is still the owner-compact hot-row materialization branch: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_ownercompact_materialized_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_ownercompact_materialized_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json), `MBS=4`, no AC, steps 2-6 `8,051.75` tok/GPU/s, `407.6725 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `194.90 GiB`. Fresh native-MORI/source-scatter MBS4 follow-up [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_source_scatter_mbs4_ab_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_source_scatter_mbs4_ab_20260611.json) proves the header-aware native path is stable at lower MBS, but rejects promotion: the first two native runs are attention-only selective-AC fit checks, and the true no-AC SDMA-matched native run reaches steps 2-6 `7,235.0` tok/GPU/s and `366.31 TFLOPs/GPU`, trailing the owner-compact no-AC control by `10.14%` over steps 2-6 and `9.45%` over steps 4-6 with about `+0.95 GiB` peak memory. Read: scoped attention recompute, not expert-Muon or current native compact, is the material MBS8 fit/perf lever; native compact remains a profiling surface for output/staging/final receive-layout overhead. The matched Muon + `triton_bwd` branch saves real memory at the same MBS8 attention-only shape ([`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json), `234.38 GiB`, `-17.59 GiB` versus AdamW + `triton_bwd`) and improves over old Muon by `+0.94%` steps 2-20, but it remains `1.99-2.42%` slower than AdamW + `triton_bwd`; MBS16 and no-AC retries still fail on activation/backward headroom. The dense-attention-only recompute gate is also rejected ([`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_mbs8_dense_attention_ac_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_mbs8_dense_attention_ac_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json)): it aborts in step-1 backward with `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` and only `170 MB` free, so Muon's saved optimizer state does not let us leave sparse MLA/LI activations uncheckpointed at `MBS=8`. The next MoE/EP scaling target is to keep the standard-EP hot/cold/helper row layout while building a first-class compact-row dispatcher/helper VJP; C4 sparse-MLA compressed-dKV/query-recompute remains the parallel attention-kernel track. Raw logs, checkpoints, and traces stay outside the repo under `/scratch/sonle5/dsv4_pretrain_canary_20260527/`, and compact JSON summaries are mirrored into `run_artifacts/`.

Corrected mHC/node-check note: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mhc_nodecheck_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mhc_nodecheck_20260610.json) confirms `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu` is healthy for the retained `MBS=8`, `GA=2`, `GBS=128`, `S4096` control: no-mHC completes six steps at steps 2-6 `8,228.0` tok/GPU/s and `416.594 TFLOPs/GPU`, with peak logged memory `245.99 GiB`. The same shape with `CANARY_USE_HYPER_CONNECTIONS=true` and attention-only checkpointing fails before the first completed metric step in backward with `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` and `Available Free mem : 0 MB`. Full activation checkpointing makes mHC fit at the same MBS8 shape, completing six steps at steps 2-6 `5,545.4` tok/GPU/s and `281.088 TFLOPs/GPU`, with peak logged memory `142.51 GiB`. A new narrower `attention_and_hyper_connections` scope keeps attention-only checkpointing and checkpoints only mHC helper calls; at MBS8 it reaches one finite metric step at loss `12.26306`, grad norm `19.125`, rank-max logged memory `252.63 GiB`, and `1474-1477` tok/GPU/s, then OORs in the next backward with `0 MB` free. Lowering to `MBS=4`, `GA=4` with the same corrected mHC scope completes six steps and is the best corrected mHC fit point so far: steps 2-6 `6,021.6` tok/GPU/s, `48,172.8` node tok/s, `305.224 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak `187.39 GiB`; steps 4-6 reach `6,060.3333` tok/GPU/s and `307.1833 TFLOPs/GPU`. The matched diagnostic profile [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mhc_mbs4_attention_hc_profile_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mhc_mbs4_attention_hc_profile_20260610.json) reaches step 2 at `5,687` tok/GPU/s and decomposes rank-max wall into model forward `3.030s`, loss `0.375s`, backward `7.999s`, Sparse SharedKV `1.705s`, attention module `4.208s`, MoE module `1.980s`, and standard-EP dispatch/combine `0.375/0.309s`; SharedKV is essentially flat versus the no-mHC MBS8 profile, so the mHC hit is not a new sparse-kernel regression. The existing middle-ground `selective/transformer_block` scope is not a fit datapoint yet: it fails before the first metric step in checkpoint recompute at the standard-EP hot-helper `weighted_scatter_add` boundary with a CPU/GPU tensor-device mismatch; a transient forced score-copy diagnostic was rejected with `Autograd not support dtype: Byte` and was not retained in source. Read: the old retained no-mHC baseline is node-valid, but it is not the corrected mHC baseline; MBS4 attention+mHC selective checkpointing now supersedes full-AC MBS8 as the corrected mHC throughput baseline, while the next mHC optimization should target memory lifetime/headroom to recover MBS8 without full-block recompute.

Fresh no-mHC current-node recheck: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_nomhc_current_nodecheck_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_nomhc_current_nodecheck_20260611.json) reruns the retained no-mHC `MBS=8`, `GA=2`, `GBS=128`, `FSDP8/EP8`, attention-only AC control on the same node after the mHC out-of-resources suspicion. It completes six steps cleanly with steps 2-6 `8,365.8` tok/GPU/s, `423.562 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak logged memory `256.87 GiB`, and post-run ROCm SMI returns to 0% allocated VRAM. Read: the node is healthy for the retained no-mHC shape; the corrected mHC failure remains an mHC memory/lifetime fit issue.

Current-source standard-EP scatter isolation: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_weightedscatter_scoretorch_nodecheck_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_weightedscatter_scoretorch_nodecheck_20260611.json) closes the separate same-source fault that made the node look suspicious. The unguarded current-source `MBS=4`, `GA=4`, no-AC standard-EP gate still fails in the normal-combine `weighted_scatter_add` backward with an HSA memory access fault when Triton owns both `grad_src` and `grad_scores`. Keeping `triton_bwd` for normal and hot scatter but setting `TORCHTITAN_WEIGHTED_SCATTER_BWD_SCORE_MODE=torch` makes Triton compute only `grad_src` and computes `grad_scores` with Torch gather/sum; that six-step no-mHC gate completes at steps 2-6 `8,066.4` tok/GPU/s, `408.404 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak `195.31 GiB`, with steps 4-6 `8,145.6667` tok/GPU/s and `412.4233 TFLOPs/GPU`. A post-fault one-step smoke with the same scoretorch split also passes cleanly after the experimental `triton_split` reducer faults, logging finite loss/grad and then returning ROCm SMI to idle ([`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_scoretorch_postfault_smoke_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_scoretorch_postfault_smoke_20260611.json)). The follow-up row-owned Triton reducer is faster in the isolated production-like weighted-scatter probe (`8.372 ms` fwd+bwd versus `12.051 ms` for scoretorch), but the integrated 8xMI350 training gate still faults in backward even after an empty-shape guard; a fresh post-row-fault scoretorch smoke passes one step with finite loss `12.35699`, grad norm `19.75`, `142.80-144.91 GiB` rank memory, and the node returns to idle after teardown ([`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_weightedscatter_scorerow_rejection_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_weightedscatter_scorerow_rejection_20260611.json)). Read: the fresh failure is isolated to the normal-combine Triton weighted-scatter score-gradient reduction at production scale, not the MI350 node, not mHC, and not the hot-helper scatter path. The next source target is an integrated-safe score-gradient reduction rather than a global fallback to `torch_custom`.

Weighted-scatter production-shape follow-up: the passing scoretorch profile run `torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_scoretorch_shapes_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260611` records the real standard-EP combine contract as `x=[16384,4096]`, `top_k=6`, and routed rows `56,441-102,799` (median `85,828`). `weighted_scatter_add` is still the largest combine substage in that trace (`2925.12 ms` summed over 384 combine records). A score-zero integrated diagnostic completes one full step when only `grad_scores` is disabled, while keeping Triton `grad_src` active. Exact-shape row-owned probes at `rows=102799`, `tokens=16384`, `hidden=4096` pass in both single-GPU and eight-rank isolated mode; eight-rank row-mode fwd+bwd medians are `3.7767-3.8204 ms` versus `5.9244-5.9640 ms` for Torch. Forcing the hot-helper scatter caller to `torch_custom` while keeping normal combine on row-score mode still faults before a metric step, so the hot-helper scatter path is not the integrated-only culprit. Batching four score rows per Triton program with `row_bm4` still faults, so this is not simple one-row program launch pressure. Read: the node and the standalone row reducer are healthy; the remaining row-mode crash is an integrated autograd/training-context issue around normal-combine score-gradient production.

Native-MORI/source-scatter profile follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_vs_native_mbs4_noac_profile_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_vs_native_mbs4_noac_profile_20260611.json) and generated step-2 parser output [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_vs_native_mbs4_noac_profile_step2_summary_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_vs_native_mbs4_noac_profile_step2_summary_20260611.json) run a matched no-AC `MBS=4`, `GA=4`, `GBS=128`, `FSDP8/EP8` profile after the node check. The standard owner-compact control reaches step-2 `6,253` tok/GPU/s and `316.61` TFLOPs/GPU; native MORI source-scatter reaches `5,476` tok/GPU/s and `277.25` TFLOPs/GPU, a `-12.43%` regression with flat memory. The loss is EP/MoE native compact, not sparse attention or optimizer: native dispatch/combines add `+455.754/+205.976 ms` rank-max and MoE backward layer sum adds `+648.029 ms`, while attention backward layer sum changes only `+31.083 ms`. Native buys dispatch permute (`100.117 -> 16.505 ms`) and combine weighted scatter (`140.395 -> 97.245 ms`), but pays steady native compact launch/body cost (`521.425 ms` dispatch launch and `382.871 ms` combine launch). Step-2 dispatch init is only `21.985 ms`, and capacity is mostly stable at `16384` peer rows, so this is not primarily handle-cache churn. Full-run MORI profiler faulted before metrics, so keep profiler use stage-isolated and use low-intrusion timing hooks for apples-to-apples full runs. Next source target remains final expert-major/compact-return ABI collapse, not route-mask or selected-order adapters.

Native-MORI count-aware combine follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_countcombine_smoke_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_countcombine_smoke_20260611.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_countcombine_mbs4_noac_6step_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_countcombine_mbs4_noac_6step_20260611.json), and [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_countaware_combine_rebuild_20260611.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_countaware_combine_rebuild_20260611.md) close the remote-source ABI trap and then run the rebuilt path for six steps. The 8xMI350 `MBS4/GA4`, no-AC native count-aware run completes six steps with finite loss/grad; steps 2-6 log `7,360.8` tok/GPU/s, `58,886.4` node tok/s, `372.684` TFLOPs/GPU, and `195.29 GiB` peak. A same-source standard-control rerun failed before metrics with HSA memory-access faults; post-failure ROCm SMI returned to idle, so that run is invalid as a control and needs separate isolation.

Native MORI compact-row status: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_compactonly_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_compactonly_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_genbarrier_noprereset_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_genbarrier_noprereset_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_directexpert_selfbypass_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_directexpert_selfbypass_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_bucketed_compact_capacity_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_bucketed_compact_capacity_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_zero_safe_cachedebug_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_zero_safe_cachedebug_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_prereset_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_prereset_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_denseguard_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_denseguard_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json), and [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_mori_native_compact_bucketed_capacity.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_mori_native_compact_bucketed_capacity.md) move the cold/normal compact collective from an adapter idea into MORI source and close the misleading `6.8k` regression read, but do not yet produce a stable promoted sparse candidate. Compact-only handle allocation fixes the prior static-heap failure and 4-rank parity passes. The first production 8x gate was rejected at step-2 `1,903` tok/GPU/s because single-CTA native compact dispatch/combine medians were `240.637/285.780 ms`; multiblock plus generation-barrier recovered to about `6.85k` tok/GPU/s, and the corrected cache-debug run showed the remaining collapse was a native compact capacity-cache bug, not an inherent native MORI slowdown. Before the fix, exact capacities above the `65536` floor created separate multi-GiB handles (`71201`, `67073`, `69231`, `125223`) and exhausted the `48G` MORI heap. The bucketed source policy now uses `max(next_power_of_two(required_rows), fixed_floor)`, and compatible larger-handle reuse avoids recreating smaller same-prefix handles. A no-checkpoint 8x diagnostic completes only 3 steps at step 2 `8,213` tok/GPU/s / `415.86 TFLOPs/GPU` and step 3 `8,453` tok/GPU/s / `428.00 TFLOPs/GPU`; this is useful evidence but not a stability claim. After adding a zero-row-safe vendored MORI Python wrapper, the next 6-step gate logs step 4 at `8,520` tok/GPU/s / `431.36-431.37 TFLOPs/GPU`, then fails after step 4 / in the next backward with a GPU memory access fault in sparse MLA sink-gradient backward. A pre-reset isolation run fails earlier after step 2 with the same sparse sink-gradient stack, so reset/sync/barrier is rejected as a stability path. A dense-guard isolation with `CANARY_SPARSE_MLA_MAX_SEQ_LEN=512` completes 6 steps (`6,618.30` tok/GPU/s and `336.70 TFLOPs/GPU` steps 2-6, diagnostic only), so native compact does not fail universally when compressed sparse MLA is removed from the failure surface. Read: native compact is still not promoted over the retained 20-step standard-EP baseline (`8,518.84` tok/GPU/s steps 2-20, `431.31 TFLOPs/GPU`; `8,630.66` tok/GPU/s steps 13-20), but the next stability target is now the native compact plus sparse SharedKV/sink-gradient interaction, output-order/dependency risk, or sparse-path memory corruption. The MORI profiler autoload path is now fixed in [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_compact_profiler_slots_20260610.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_compact_profiler_slots_20260610.md): C++ now prefers the profiler JIT cache when `ENABLE_PROFILER` is set, and a sliced 4x smoke exported real compact dispatch/combine traces before failing OOR. That smoke is profile-plumbing evidence only; the next gate must still be apples-to-apples on a clean 8x node, then followed by a non-profiled 6-step sparse stability pass before any 20-step throughput replacement. The remaining source target is collapsing the output/staging ABI so compact rows land directly in a MORI-owned or final expert-major receive layout consumable by AITER/helper grouped MLP, instead of symmetric staging plus peer pull into ordinary `torch.empty` outputs.

Clean 8x native-MORI profiler update: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_profiler_clean8x_stageisolated_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_profiler_clean8x_stageisolated_20260610.json) supersedes the earlier sliced smoke and mixed-stage combine read. Native-MORI profiler harness correction: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_profiler_harness_importfix_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_profiler_harness_importfix_20260611.json) and [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_profiler_sampling_import_mode_20260611.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_profiler_sampling_import_mode_20260611.md) close the profiler-source mismatch from the next retained-shape attempt. Native MORI integrated profile update: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_gradcontig_profile_mbs8_steps2_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_gradcontig_profile_mbs8_steps2_20260611.json) profiles the native compact path at the retained `MBS=8`, `GA=2`, `GBS=128`, `FSDP8/EP8`, attention-only AC shape after adding a narrow grad-contiguity probe. Native source-position scatter follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_source_position_scatter_flat_triton_20260611.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_source_position_scatter_flat_triton_20260611.md), [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_jit_dispatch_header_cache_key_20260611.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_jit_dispatch_header_cache_key_20260611.md), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_source_position_scatter_flat_triton_probe_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_source_position_scatter_flat_triton_probe_20260611.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_jit_headerhash_source_scatter_recheck_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_jit_headerhash_source_scatter_recheck_20260611.json) add an opt-in `weighted_scatter_add_from_flat_positions(...)` path for native-MORI combine. The unset default is intentionally `materialize`, preserving old behavior; `TORCHTITAN_STANDARD_EP_SOURCE_SCATTER_BACKEND=triton_flat` enables the new source-position Triton kernel. MI350 smoke validates exact default behavior and matching gradients for the opt-in path, while a production-shaped scatter slice improves `2.433 -> 2.253 ms` median. The first 8x e2e gate failed at a native compact staging-stride assert; the follow-up pins that to stale MORI JIT cache keying because `ep_intranode` did not hash `src/ops/dispatch_combine/intranode.hpp`. The header-aware cache compiles fresh hash `b948f452e255` and removes the stale assert, but the `MBS=8` native-MORI + `triton_flat` branch still only reaches one finite step (`~1,964-1,970` tok/GPU/s, `220.27-223.01 GiB`) before next-backward HSA out-of-resources with `2 MB` free. Read: keep the cache-key fix and keep `triton_flat` opt-in; this is still a scoped source-position adapter cleanup, not an e2e throughput promotion. The main native-MORI target remains final receive-layout collapse, compact helper VJP/return, and lower native compact memory/output residency.

Native MORI role-handle follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_role_handles_20260610.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_role_handles_20260610.md), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_rolehandles_fixedcap6_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_rolehandles_fixedcap6_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_refcount_release_fixedcap3_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_refcount_release_fixedcap3_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_keepreleased_default_kernelmodule_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_keepreleased_default_kernelmodule_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_rolehandles_cap65536_smoke3_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_rolehandles_cap65536_smoke3_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json) split compact handle allocation by role and make shared-forward-handle autograd ownership reference-counted. Dispatch-only handles allocate dispatch staging, combine-only handles allocate combine staging, and TorchTitan retains one logical handle reference per inverse autograd consumer, releasing it after that inverse collective runs. This is intentionally a handle-lifetime/memory fix only: no route-mask wrapper, row materialization, token collective, per-row Python work, per-token refcount, or default forced Python GC on release. `KEEP_RELEASED_HANDLES` now defaults to true for perf because physically destroying a MORI op calls the C++ handle destructor and synchronizes the device; set it false only for memory-pressure release diagnostics. The remote MORI rebuild and pybind smoke pass. The first 8x fixed-cap MBS8 gate reaches finite step 1 with logged memory `190.32-198.53 GiB`, then fails in the next backward with `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` at `0-44 MB` free. The refcount-release follow-up lowers max logged step-1 memory to `196.28 GiB`, but still fails at the same next-backward boundary with `60 MB` free. The keep-released default rerun fixes the sparse-MLA backend-module env and confirms the same next-backward failure with step-1 memory `190.37-195.05 GiB` and `0 MB` reported free, so this is not a module-import issue. A `65536` cap smoke is also rejected: it reaches finite step 1 at `191.58-194.86 GiB` but fails in the next backward with a GPU memory access fault, so a smaller fixed cap is not the fix. Read: the patch is worth keeping as a lower-residency/autograd-correct native-MORI primitive, but the next native compact fix must reduce active compact capacity/staging-output residency or collapse the MORI staging/output ABI, not add row-path adapters, cap knobs, or destructor-synchronized release to the perf path.

Native MORI role-handle heap32 follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_rolesplit_reusefwd_heap32_steps6_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_rolesplit_reusefwd_heap32_steps6_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json) updates the role-handle read. With role split, forward-handle reuse, keep-released handles, and `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=32G`, the autograd-correct native compact path completes six sparse `S4096` steps. Steps 2-6 average `7,788.2` tok/GPU/s and `394.324 TFLOPs/GPU`; steps 4-6 average `8,166.667` tok/GPU/s and `413.497 TFLOPs/GPU`; peak logged memory is `235.59 GiB`. It is not promoted over the retained 20-step standard-EP baseline, but it replaces the earlier role-handle conclusion that the path was still blocked at step 1. The heap A/B is now clear: `16G` is too small for handle construction, `48G` over-reserves and starves FSDP reduce headroom, and `32G` is the validated six-step default for native compact. The launcher now defaults to role split plus `32G` heap only when `CANARY_STANDARD_EP_COMPACT_COLLECTIVE_BACKEND=mori_native`, so the fix stays on handle lifetime/heap sizing and does not add row-path latency.

Native MORI role-handle 20-step correction: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_autocap_heap32_kernelmodule_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_autocap_heap32_kernelmodule_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_default_fixedcap_heap48_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_default_fixedcap_heap48_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260610.json) reject turning this into a hidden default promotion. With the sparse backend module explicitly pinned, auto-cap plus heap32 reaches step 4, then exhausts the MORI heap while requesting another aligned `16 GiB` handle/buffer. Fixed `131072` peer rows plus heap48 avoids that capacity churn but fails after step 1 with `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` on `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu`. Read: the role-handle/refcount invariant is still the right autograd-correctness fix, but the native compact perf path still needs lower active capacity/staging-output residency or reserved-capacity/active-row decoupling before it can replace the retained standard-EP baseline.

Native MORI remote-staging capacity follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_remote_staging_capacity_20260611.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_native_remote_staging_capacity_20260611.md), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_remote_staging_autocap_smoke2d_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_remote_staging_autocap_smoke2d_20260611.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_remote_staging_heap16_smoke3_20260611.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_remote_staging_heap16_smoke3_20260611.json) fix the self-row capacity accounting and prove the source is active: native compact now selects the `32768` row bucket for remote-staged rows instead of the old fixed `131072`. Heap32 reaches one step at `1130-1131` tok/GPU/s with `224.65 GiB` peak then fails in step-2 backward with `24 MB` free; heap16 also constructs and reaches one step at `1109` tok/GPU/s with `235.15 GiB` peak, then fails in the next backward. Read: lower capacity/heap helps residency but still does not materialize stability; the next native-MORI source target is active handle/output residency and final receive-layout collapse, not more heap/capacity knobs.

Native MORI compact source-position follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_sourcepos_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_sourcepos_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json) fixes the most plausible output-order ABI risk in the native combine path. The prior TorchTitan wrapper discarded MORI's returned `source_rank_flat_positions` and then scattered with the old expert-sorted token/score vectors. The source-position patch threads the returned flat positions into final combine, decodes the rank-strided local `(token, topk-slot)` key, and gathers the source-order top-k scores for `weighted_scatter_add`; non-native standard EP combine remains unchanged. The first `do-vunguyen` attempt failed before training because that node did not have the patched vendored MORI binary and imported the stock image extension. After copying the patched 2026-06-09 MORI tree under `/scratch/sonle5/dsv4_pretrain_canary_20260527/sources/references/mori` and verifying the four native compact pybind symbols in-container, the sparse `S4096` native compact gate completed all 6 steps. Metrics: steps 2-6 average `8,160.20` tok/GPU/s and `413.166 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak `226.89 GiB`; steps 2-5 average `8,481.25` tok/GPU/s and `429.4175 TFLOPs/GPU`; steps 3-5 average `8,702.33` tok/GPU/s and `440.61 TFLOPs/GPU`. Step 6 dipped to `6,876` tok/GPU/s, so this is not promoted over the retained 20-step standard-EP baseline. Read: native compact plus sparse SharedKV now passes the previous step-4 sparse sink-gradient failure surface, but promotion needs the same source-position path to pass a 20-step non-profiled run, ideally with native compact debug-cache logging disabled after confirming no capacity churn.

Native MORI compact chunked-sink 20-step gate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_sourcepos_chunkedsink_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_native_sourcepos_chunkedsink_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260609.json) supersedes the 6-step stability question. The pre-patch 20-step source-position gate failed after step 4 in sparse SharedKV sink-gradient backward while allocating the full `(grad_output.float() * output.float())` product slab. The sparse backend now computes that dot in last-dimension chunks (`TORCHTITAN_DSV4_SPARSE_MLA_SHAREDKV_SINK_DOT_CHUNK=32` in the gate), preserving the math while avoiding the 4 GiB transient. Two non-profiled 20-step repeats completed on `do-vunguyen-mi350-gpu`. Run 1 averaged steps 2-20 `8,450.37` tok/GPU/s and `427.86 TFLOPs/GPU`, steps 13-20 `9,055.50` tok/GPU/s and `458.50 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak `228.04 GiB`. Repeat 2 averaged steps 2-20 `8,429.42` tok/GPU/s and `426.80 TFLOPs/GPU`, steps 13-20 `8,896.13` tok/GPU/s and `450.43 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak `228.72 GiB`. Read: native source-position compact is now stable enough to keep as a lower-memory candidate, and the late window is promising (`~4.0%` above the retained baseline on average with `~23 GiB` lower peak memory), but it is not promoted over the retained full-window baseline because the combined steps 2-20 mean is `8,439.89` tok/GPU/s / `427.33 TFLOPs/GPU`, about `0.93%` below the retained `8,518.84` / `431.31`. The next native-MORI action is a short MORI-profiler/isolation pass on this stable candidate to explain the mid-run steps 6-12 dips before attempting another retained-baseline replacement.

Current-best helper-tail lower-level gate: [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_currentbest_tailrows_1xmi350_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_currentbest_tailrows_1xmi350_20260609.json) and [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_currentbest_tailrows.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_currentbest_tailrows.md) rerun the 1xMI350 helper owner-VJP probe at the actual retained MBS8 late-window helper row sizes: median `69,635`, p95 `128,284`, and max `147,159` remote rows. Compact grouped-MM-only remains useful (`16.521/24.105/30.591 ms` full fwd+bwd), but the scatter-inclusive grouped-MM boundary is `26.791/30.088/37.499 ms`; at the max tail it is effectively tied with padded full VJP (`37.450 ms`). Read: the next MoE/EP implementation gate is not another isolated grouped-MM slice. It needs the compact-row helper VJP/dispatcher return contract to keep `dX`, `dTopK`, and weighted scatter in the compact layout.

Compact-return helper probe: [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_compact_return_probe_1xmi350_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_compact_return_probe_1xmi350_20260609.json) and [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_compact_return_probe.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_compact_return_probe.md) add and measure `--grouped-mm-compact-return`, a lower-bound helper contract that returns `dx_compact` and `dTopK_compact` without dense token/top-k scatter. The 512-row smoke passes after densifying only for correctness. At retained MBS8 tail sizes, compact return is `17.240/27.120/33.175 ms` for median/p95/max rows, versus scatter-inclusive `17.854/28.248/34.950 ms` and padded `17.539/31.638/36.422 ms`. Read: compact return recovers `~1.1-1.8 ms` at p95/max, but still leaves the max-tail path `5.49 ms` above grouped-MM-only (`27.687 ms`). The next MoE/EP implementation remains fused/batched compact helper VJP plus compact dispatcher return; delaying dense scatter alone is not enough.

Selected hot-weight alignment cache: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_align_hotweight_cache_4x_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_align_hotweight_cache_4x_20260609.json) and [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_align_hot_weight_cache.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_align_hot_weight_cache.md) cache the selected-order hot-weight `compact_to_hot` index once per hot-split call and time W1/W2/W3 reindex into owner-compact row-group order. A 4x sliced diagnostic on GPUs `1,2,3,4` with torch hot-weight transport completes two steps; step 2 is `5,160` tok/GPU/s, `261.27 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `223.45 GiB`. After caching, the selected-weight alignment stages total about `648.61 ms` across all ranks and both steps, or `~81 ms/rank/step`; build-index itself is only `0.055 ms/call`. Decision: keep the cache/instrumentation, but do not chase selected-hot-weight alignment as the lead MoE target. Hot-weight movement, helper VJP, combine wait/scatter, and dispatch/count exchange are larger in the same diagnostic.

4x MBS4 torch-transport fit: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_attention_ac_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_attention_ac_20260609.json) and [`changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_fit.md`](changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_fit.md) supersede the old 4x MBS2 stable reference. On `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu` GPUs `1,2,3,4`, the `FSDP4/EP4`, `MBS=4`, `GA=8`, `S4096`, `GBS128`, attention-only AC shape completes six steps when hot-weight forward/reduce uses torch instead of MORI/SDMA. Steps 2-6 average `6,977.6` tok/GPU/s, `27,910.4` node tok/s, `353.30 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `259.98 GiB` peak; steps 4-6 average `7,087.67` tok/GPU/s. The matched diagnostic profile [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_profile_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_profile_20260609.json) and [`changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_profile.md`](changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs4_torchtransport_profile.md) record step-2 additive timing: backward `15.621 s`, forward `5.335 s`, loss `0.814 s`, optimizer `0.089 s`, and same-scope fwd/bwd residual only `22.0 ms` (`0.101%`). Profile sidecars name C4 SharedKV `2.449 s`, all SharedKV `3.305 s`, dense attention inner backward `1.840 s`, hot-split backward `1.438 s`, standard-EP combine `0.808 s`, and dispatch `0.662 s`. Read: the old 4x MBS4 fault was not intrinsic to MBS4 and is likely tied to the sliced SDMA hot-weight path. This is now the better 4x reference, but it is still only `57.2%` of the `12.2k` tok/GPU/s target and trails the retained 8x MBS8 branch; the 4x wall is GA8 plus per-microbatch C4 SharedKV and MoE/EP helper work, not optimizer or PP bubble.

4x MBS8 expert-Muon fit gate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs8_expertmuon_fit_failures_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs8_expertmuon_fit_failures_20260609.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs8_expertmuon_nomaterialize_ce256_fit_failure_20260609.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_4x_mbs8_expertmuon_nomaterialize_ce256_fit_failure_20260609.json), [`changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs8_expert_muon_fit.md`](changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs8_expert_muon_fit.md), and [`changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs8_ce256_fit.md`](changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_mbs8_ce256_fit.md) reject the next 4x batch rung. On `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu` GPUs `2,3,4,5`, `FSDP4/EP4`, `MBS=8`, `GA=4`, expert-Muon `NS=1` prealloc, attention-only AC, torch hot-weight forward/reduce, owner-compact hot rows, and `triton_bwd` weighted scatter reach one metric step, but every fit attempt fails on the next step with ROCm out-of-resources. Default CE8 fails in `cross_entropy_loss` with `4 MB` free after `266.53 GiB` logged peak; CE32 fails in loss lm-head linear with `0 MB` free after `267.21 GiB`; CE128 fails in next-step MoE hot-weight alignment with `0 MB` free after `265.08 GiB`; disabling materialized hot rows plus CE128 fails in FSDP `foreach_reduce` while requesting `6.00 GiB` with `5.86 GiB` free; raising that to CE256 fails in step-2 `chunk_loss.backward()` with `0 MB` free after `266.50 GiB`. Read: expert-Muon optimizer-state savings and CE chunking do not buy 4x `MBS=8/GA=4`; closing the 4x target needs lower activation/MoE hot-helper lifetime or a split/chunked expert-bank FSDP reduce allocation, not just optimizer state.

C4-only recompute gate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_mbs8_c4_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_mbs8_c4_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json) completes six steps at the same Muon + `triton_bwd` MBS8 shape, with steps 2-6 `8,372.8` tok/GPU/s and `423.922 TFLOPs/GPU`, but peak memory rises to `269.67 GiB`. The longer overflow-node 20-step gate [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_c4_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_overflownode_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_c4_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_overflownode_20260608.json) confirms the speed/memory trade: steps 2-20 `8,553.45` tok/GPU/s and `433.072 TFLOPs/GPU`, steps 13-20 `8,603.17` tok/GPU/s and `435.5925 TFLOPs/GPU`, with `269.63 GiB` peak memory. Read: C4-only recompute can match or slightly beat the AdamW current best in broad windows, but it gives back `17.66 GiB` versus AdamW attention-only and `35.25 GiB` versus Muon attention-only, so it does not preserve the memory headroom needed for MBS16/no-AC tuning. Decision: useful high-memory evidence, not a retained baseline promotion. Attention-only selective recompute remains the retained memory-saving scope.

4x SDMA-hotweight historical gate: [`changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_standard_ep_materialization.md`](changesets/torchtitan_flash12_4x_standard_ep_materialization.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_sdma_hotweight_4x_materialization_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_sdma_hotweight_4x_materialization_20260608.json) close the matching `FSDP4/EP4` standard-EP top-8 + MORI/SDMA hot-weight gate on `do-sonle5-mi350-gpu`. `MBS=4`, `GA=8`, `GBS=128` logs one step at `~3.23k` tok/GPU/s and `~163.6 TFLOPs/GPU`, then fails on the next forward with a GPU memory access fault in `_standard_ep_hot_split_forward` after `244.72 GiB` peak logged memory. `MBS=2`, `GA=16` completes six steps, but is not competitive: steps 2-6 average `4,986.6` tok/GPU/s, `19,946.4` node tok/s, `252.472 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `261.08 GiB` peak logged memory. This is now superseded by the torch-hotweight MBS4 run above; the useful read is that the old failure was tied to the sliced SDMA hot-weight path rather than the `MBS=4` batch shape itself.

Expert-Muon follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_rootcause.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_rootcause.md), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_batched_chunk4_followup_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_batched_chunk4_followup_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_batched_ns1_followup_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_batched_ns1_followup_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_mbs8_selective_attention_ac_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_mbs8_selective_attention_ac_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_mbs8_attention_ac_additive_profile_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_mbs8_attention_ac_additive_profile_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/muon_batched_chunk_sweep_ns1_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/muon_batched_chunk_sweep_ns1_1xmi350_20260608.json), and the AdamW control above explain the optimizer-memory surprise. Muon does halve persistent expert optimizer state, but native/per-expert Muon created large transient rank-2 update/orthogonalization state and slow Newton-Schulz work. Batched expert-Muon fixes that isolated optimizer regression (`MBS=4` peak drops to `176.29 GiB` and native-Muon step-3 throughput improves to `7,417` tok/GPU/s), and `NS=1` cuts the 12-layer expert optimizer slice from `637.8 ms` to `213.2 ms`, but no-AC `MBS=8` still fails after step 1 at `255.35 GiB`. The root-cause fit fix is scoped activation recompute: whole-block selective AC re-enters MoE hot-helper collectives and fails, while `CANARY_ACTIVATION_CHECKPOINT_SCOPE=attention_only` completes six `MBS=8`, `GA=2` steps. The corrected apples-to-apples read is that Muon is not higher-memory than AdamW at the same `MBS=8` attention-only shape (`243.22` vs `260.04 GiB`), but it is slower (`8,049.2` vs `8,151.0` tok/GPU/s); the additive profile names the residual optimizer wall at `228.5 ms` for Muon versus `46.8 ms` for AdamW. The runtime `torch.optim.Muon` has no foreach/fused path, and the batched-Muon chunk sweep keeps `chunk4` as the best speed/memory point (`212.14 ms`, `54.32 GiB` on the 12-layer expert-bank slice). A follow-up PyTorch-level Newton-Schulz workspace reshuffle is rejected in [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_ns_workspace_probe.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_ns_workspace_probe.md): `NS=1` chunk4 regresses to `212.79 ms`, while `NS=5` improves only `0.18%`. The concrete chunk/fuse follow-up is now [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_prealloc_workspace.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_prealloc_workspace.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json): preallocated chunk workspace improves the 12-layer expert-bank slice from `223.57` to `219.02 ms`, then materializes as `8,151.2` tok/GPU/s and `412.71 TFLOPs/GPU` over steps 2-6 with `240.31 GiB` peak. Correctness follow-up [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_correctness_validation.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_correctness_validation.md), [`run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_correctness_cpu_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_correctness_cpu_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_correctness_mi350_bf16_abs5e4_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_correctness_mi350_bf16_abs5e4_20260608.json) show the preallocated workspace implementation matches the older batched path tightly in FP32 and stays within a `5e-4` absolute MI350-BF16 envelope for matching `NS=1/2/5`; strict BF16 relative parity fails near zero. The PyTorch 2.9 MI350 optimizer-slice perf check [`run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_perf_mi350_12layer_ns1_20260608.jsonl`](run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_perf_mi350_12layer_ns1_20260608.jsonl) shows `prealloc` improves the 12-layer expert-bank `NS=1` step-2 slice from `692.88` to `580.88 ms` (`+16.16%`) with a slight peak-memory drop, but the follow-up [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_gram_trace_norm.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_gram_trace_norm.md) rejects a norm-only Gram-trace optimization for the retained Nexus image (`210.20 ms` vector norm vs `210.58 ms` Gram trace). The MBS16 fit follow-up [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_mbs16_fit_failures_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_mbs16_fit_failures_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json) rejects the next batch jump: default weighted scatter faults in first-forward MoE combine, and exact `torch_chunked` scatter passes parity at the MBS16 combine shape but then fails in LightningIndexer forward with an `8.00 GiB` allocation when only `6.64 GiB` is free. The no-AC MBS8 retry with Muon prealloc is also rejected in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_mbs8_noac_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_mbs8_noac_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json): it logs one step at `1,628-1,631` tok/GPU/s and `250.86-258.43 GiB`, then aborts in the next backward with `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` and `0 MB` free. The remaining risk is optimizer semantics and quality because `NS=1` differs from `NS=5` as expected. Decision: keep this as the best lower-memory MBS8 Muon branch, but keep AdamW attention-only AC as the quality-safe throughput baseline; larger MBS or no-AC now needs sparse-attention/LI activation-memory reduction, not optimizer-state savings alone.

Muon `NS=1` quality-smoke follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json) extends the best Muon MBS8 branch to 20 steps on the tiny re-looped `c4_test` data. It completes cleanly with steps 2-20 averaging `8,271.84` tok/GPU/s and `418.82 TFLOPs/GPU`, steps 13-20 averaging `8,321.09` tok/GPU/s, peak logged memory `240.49 GiB`, loss `12.28050 -> 3.27528`, and grad norm `104.5 -> 3.8438` from step 2 to 20. The matched AdamW comparator [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json) also completes cleanly and is faster at the same shape: steps 2-20 `8,431.87` tok/GPU/s and `426.92 TFLOPs/GPU`, steps 13-20 `8,514.63` tok/GPU/s and `431.11 TFLOPs/GPU`, peak `259.82 GiB`, loss `12.26053 -> 3.47305`, and grad norm `51.0 -> 5.1875` from step 2 to 20. The matched `triton_bwd` rerun [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_ns1_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json) improves Muon to steps 2-20 `8,349.67` tok/GPU/s and `422.76 TFLOPs/GPU`, steps 13-20 `8,421.73` tok/GPU/s and `426.41 TFLOPs/GPU`, with peak `234.38 GiB`; this is `+0.94-1.21%` versus old Muon and `-6.11 GiB` peak, but still `1.99-2.42%` slower than AdamW + `triton_bwd` while saving `17.59 GiB`. Read: `NS=1` Muon is a useful lower-memory health-pass branch, not a promotion over AdamW as the quality-safe throughput baseline.

Steady-window Muon overhead follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_steady_window_overhead.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_steady_window_overhead.md), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_muon_steady_window_overhead_read_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_muon_steady_window_overhead_read_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/muon_ns1_prealloc_phase_current_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/muon_ns1_prealloc_phase_current_1xmi350_20260608.json) make the promotion rule explicit. Six steps are acceptable for fit/smoke, but they understate steady throughput: AdamW rises from `8,227.1` tok/GPU/s over steps 2-6 to `8,514.625` over steps 13-20, while Muon rises from `8,111.8` to `8,321.094`. The longer window therefore strengthens the AdamW decision: Muon falls from `-1.40%` behind over steps 2-6 to `-2.27%` behind over steps 13-20. The existing additive profile explains the e2e gap: Muon's optimizer step is `228.529 ms` versus AdamW's `46.79 ms`. The corrected current-source `NS=1` phase split shows why a lower-level Muon kernel can help but must fuse more than raw matmul: the retained expert-bank slice is `211.738 ms`, with an intrusive phase split of `132.026 ms` Newton-Schulz work and `96.840 ms` non-NS update/plumbing. The NS BMM stages contain about `98.95 TFLOP` and measure around `999 TFLOPs/s` on one MI350, but source update, param add, and chunked epilogues still prevent e2e promotion. Both 8x MI350 nodes were busy with a two-node TorchTitan job at the original follow-up check, so a fresh 8x late-window profile should only be rerun after a new Muon implementation.

Muon Triton-elementwise follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_triton_elementwise.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_triton_elementwise.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_triton_elementwise_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_expert_muon_prealloc_triton_elementwise_mbs8_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json) test the obvious next rung from that phase split: Triton kernels for the Nesterov source update and final parameter add around the existing preallocated Newton-Schulz workspace. The isolated 1xMI350 12-layer expert-bank slice improves from `219.619` to `212.465 ms` on the warm step (`+3.26%`), but the real 8x e2e gate does not materialize: `MBS=8`, `GA=2`, attention-only selective AC, standard-EP top-8 helper, and MORI/SDMA hot-weight transport complete six steps at only `8,039.0` tok/GPU/s, `407.026 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `240.69 GiB` peak over steps 2-6. That is `-1.38%` tok/GPU/s versus the same Muon prealloc baseline (`8,151.2` tok/GPU/s) and still well behind the 20-step AdamW baseline. Decision: keep `TORCHTITAN_OPTIMIZER_MUON_ELEMENTWISE_BACKEND=triton` as an opt-in diagnostic only. Also note the selector trap: expert-Muon is selected with `CANARY_DSV4_EXPERTS_ON_MUON=1`; `CANARY_OPTIMIZER_IMPLEMENTATION=muon_adamw` is invalid because TorchTitan's `optimizer.implementation` is an enum.

Swap-offload MBS8 follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_swapopt_torchparam_mbs8_fit_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_swapopt_torchparam_mbs8_fit_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps2_20260608.json) tested the adjacent memory-relief branch that keeps AdamW semantics: `optimizer.implementation=swap_opt_states_cpu`, `TORCHTITAN_OPTIMIZER_SWAP_UPDATE_MODE=torch_param`, CPU-resident BF16/param moments, same retained standard-EP top-8 + MORI/SDMA hot-weight shape, `MBS=8`, `GA=2`, no AC. It does complete two steps where plain AdamW and batched expert-Muon MBS8 failed after step 1, but it is not a promotion: step 2 is only `1,203-1,208` tok/GPU/s and `60.91-61.14` TFLOPs/GPU, while rank-max logged memory still reaches `260.52 GiB`. Decision: Python-level optimizer-state swap is a fit/debug mechanism, not the path to target throughput. Larger-MBS work needs activation/backward-memory reduction or a real HIP/C++ fused and pipelined swap-update/mapped-memory optimizer implementation; otherwise keep optimizing the retained MBS4 MoE/EP and sparse-MLA tracks.

Muon FP32/NS5 gate: [`changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_fp32_prealloc_gate.md`](changesets/torchtitan_expert_muon_fp32_prealloc_gate.md) and [`run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_fp32_ns5_gate_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/muon_prealloc_fp32_ns5_gate_20260608.json) tested whether preallocated workspace can make the quality-safer `NS=5`, FP32-compute Muon path viable. The implementation now preserves old BF16 blend rounding and passes MI350 prealloc-vs-none parity exactly for `NS=1/2/5`, but the 12-layer expert-bank slice regresses slightly (`4138.644 -> 4171.202 ms`) and adds `3.5 GiB` resident workspace. Decision: reject for perf; keep `NS=1` BF16 prealloc as the lower-memory Muon branch and AdamW as the quality-safe throughput baseline.

Standard-EP SDMA timing follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_sdma_hotweight_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_sdma_hotweight_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260607.json) shows why this is a retained edge but not the next large lever. In the approximate step-2 timing window, SDMA improves backward hot-dW all-reduce by `8.62 ms` rank-max versus the torch hot-weight reference, but forward hot-weight all-reduce regresses by `4.91 ms`, leaving only about `3 ms` net hot-weight microstage improvement. Raw SDMA timing also includes a one-time `~4.93s` first-use setup/JIT/handle tax in `w2.forward.all_reduce_hot_weight`. Decision: keep SDMA hot-weight transport, but push the next MoE/EP work toward first-class MORI compact-row dispatcher layout, batched helper grouped VJP, and overlap, not more hot-weight all-reduce tuning.

Standard-EP stage timing follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_stage_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_stage_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260607.json) adds intrusive per-stage timing around the same top-8 helper branch. Step 2 completes at `7,655` tok/GPU/s and `387.59` TFLOPs/GPU, so this is attribution evidence only. The late-window read says ordinary token all-to-all is not the next big edge: dispatch all-to-all is `~8.0 ms` rank-max and combine all-to-all is `~7.4 ms`, while combine score application is `~233.6 ms`, combine scatter is `~50.5 ms`, the hot-weight/helper movement bucket is `~165-170 ms`, dispatch count exchange is `~86.5 ms`, and permute/unpermute are `~74.8/51.9 ms`. Decision: preserve the standard-EP hot/cold/helper row layout and target fused weighted combine/scatter plus batched/overlapped helper grouped VJP before trying to replace the whole standard-EP all-to-all path with current MORI dispatch/combine.

Standard-EP hot-split backward timing follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hot_split_backward_timing.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hot_split_backward_timing.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_hot_split_bwd_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_hot_split_bwd_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json) add opt-in autograd spans for the retained standard-EP helper backward path. Step 2 reaches `7,547` tok/GPU/s and `382.12` TFLOPs/GPU, so this is attribution evidence only. The step-2-ish window (`call_id > 576`) names `standard_ep.hot_split.backward.helper_mlp_vjp_to_sorted_x` at `334.019 ms` rank-max and `standard_ep.hot_split.backward.scatter_to_remote_y` at `105.546 ms`, while the forward helper grouped W1/W2/W3 buckets are only `45.400/45.830/42.408 ms`. Decision: the next standard-EP MoE/EP target is batched or fused helper grouped training VJP plus weighted scatter/combine, not another hot-weight transport-only swap.

Standard-EP manual helper-VJP follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hot_split_manual_tgmm.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hot_split_manual_tgmm.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_hot_split_manual_tgmm_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_hot_split_manual_tgmm_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json) test the obvious adapter-level fix: custom autograd helper MLP VJP with explicit SwiGLU backward, xgrad, and AITER `ptgmm` wgrads. The clean 8x smoke reaches step-2 `7,603` tok/GPU/s and `384.95` TFLOPs/GPU, `-5.31%` versus retained; the timing run reaches only `7,358` tok/GPU/s and shows helper VJP rank-max grows to `440.009 ms`, with manual wgrad at `192.505 ms`. Decision: reject `manual_tgmm`; the next MoE/EP branch should make compact hot/cold/helper rows and batched helper VJP first-class rather than wrapping the old helper path in explicit TGMM.

Standard-EP manual compact-return split: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_vjp.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_vjp.md), [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_topscore_grad_path.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_topscore_grad_path.md), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_split_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_split_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_split_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_split_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json) refine the rejected manual-return branch. At the 28k mean-row shape, dense `dTopK` scatter is only `0.674 ms` and dense `dX` scatter is `0.531 ms`; at the 54.4k tail shape, dense `dTopK` scatter grows to `3.601 ms` and dense `dX` scatter to `1.472 ms`. The source audit corrects the interpretation: production `weighted_scatter_add` backward already returns compact per-helper-row `grad_scores`, so the explicit dense `dTopK` scatter is a useful tail diagnostic rather than the exact production helper-kernel boundary. The full manual-return path still loses at the tail (`21.556 ms` versus `17.193 ms` Triton scatter-autograd), so the next MoE/EP implementation should go below the wrapper level: fused/batched compact-row helper backward with weighted `dX`, compact-score return, delayed/fused router scatter, and hot `dW` overlap.

Hot-weight collective-shape probe: [`run_artifacts/mori_hotweight_collectives_8x_s4096_top8_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/mori_hotweight_collectives_8x_s4096_top8_20260607.json) and [`run_artifacts/mori_hotweight_collectives_8x_s4096_top8_w13_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/mori_hotweight_collectives_8x_s4096_top8_w13_20260607.json) explain the forward SDMA regression more directly. On `do-vunguyen-mi350-gpu`, all 8 GPUs report uniform one-hop XGMI, so the issue is not an obvious fabric fallback. For top-8 hot weights, torch/RCCL owner-sharded all-gather is faster than full all-reduce (`0.350 ms` vs `0.682 ms` at `128 MiB`, `0.638 ms` vs `1.323 ms` at `256 MiB`). MORI SDMA all-gather is also faster than MORI SDMA all-reduce, but slower than torch/RCCL all-gather on the measured shape. Decision: make forward hot-weight movement an owner-sharded gather/broadcast backend, while keeping backward hot `dW` movement on a true reduce primitive.

Owner-gather materialization follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_standard_ep_hotweight_owner_gather_rootcause_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_standard_ep_hotweight_owner_gather_rootcause_20260607.json) closes the first implementation attempt as a drop-in backend. Correctness passes, but the clean 8xMI350 S4096/GBS128/MBS4 six-step A/B is slightly slower than retained MORI SDMA forward transport: candidate steps 2-6 average `7,974.6` tok/GPU/s and `403.768` TFLOPs/GPU versus retained `8,029.0` and `406.522`. The reason is the current dense selected-hot-weight ABI. Successful owner-gather calls all have pad factor `2.0`, about half the calls fall back at pad factor `3.0-4.0`, and the pack/allgather/unpack adapter costs `~0.20-0.26 ms` per successful hot-weight call versus `~0.07-0.10 ms` for retained MORI SDMA. Decision: do not promote `torch_allgather` as a drop-in backend. The next staged EP/MORI work should make owner-sharded hot-weight buffers first-class in the hot/cold/helper dispatcher layout so helper grouped MLP can consume them without reconstructing dense selected-order `hot_weight`.

Owner-sharded helper-layout follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_owner_sharded_hot_helper.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_owner_sharded_hot_helper.md) implements the first ABI/layout step toward that target behind `TORCHTITAN_STANDARD_EP_HOT_SPLIT_WEIGHT_LAYOUT=owner_sharded`. The dispatcher now saves owner-shard and compact-owner row offsets, and the helper grouped-MLP path can sort/count rows by compact owner-shard offset so it consumes compact owner-sharded gathered weights directly. The extended 8-rank parity probe passes in both balanced and skewed owner cases: [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_owner_sharded_hot_helper_parity_8x_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_owner_sharded_hot_helper_parity_8x_20260607.json). The timing A/B [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_owner_sharded_hothelper_timing_ab_dosonle5_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_owner_sharded_hothelper_timing_ab_dosonle5_20260607.json) closes this as correct but not promoted: selected-order W13 logs step-2 `6,371` tok/GPU/s and `322.56` TFLOPs/GPU with `765.0 ms` rank-max hot path; default owner-sharded logs `6,380` and `323.02` with `779.7 ms` hot path while still falling back on `288/432` hot-weight calls; forced pad8 owner-sharded logs `6,319` and `319.94` with `917.4 ms` hot path. Decision: do not tune pad factors further. The next MoE/EP branch should move only per-rank needed hot weights or make compact owner-sharded rows a first-class dispatcher input, avoiding all-rank padded gather and dense selected-order reconstruction.

Needed-set and compact-presort follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_needed_hotweight_presort.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_needed_hotweight_presort.md) closes both immediate branches from the owner-sharded helper-layout result. The clean probe artifact [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_needed_hotweight_and_presort_decision_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_needed_hotweight_and_presort_decision_20260607.json) shows explicit per-rank-needed hot-weight all-to-all is not viable for normal top-8: mixed W13 selected dense all-reduce is `1.2665 ms`, while needed-set forward is `3.1729 ms` and needed backward reduce is `2.9490 ms`; even skewed W13 loses unless each helper needs only a small artificial subset. Compact dispatcher presort is correct and opt-in via `TORCHTITAN_STANDARD_EP_HOT_SPLIT_PRESORT_MODE`, and it cuts late-window helper `sort_offsets` from `27.38` to `15.24 ms`, but the profiled 8x step-2 e2e only moves `7,563 -> 7,578` tok/GPU/s. Decision: do not promote either branch. The next useful MoE/EP path is a true compact-row dispatcher/helper grouped-VJP ABI that makes hot/cold/helper rows the layout from the start, not another wrapper around dense selected-order hot weights.

Owner-compact materialization follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_ownercompact_materialized.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_ownercompact_materialized.md), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_ownercompact_materialized_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_ownercompact_materialized_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_ownercompact_stage_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_ownercompact_stage_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json) close the next compact-row ABI branch. The six-step 8xMI350 `MBS=4` run completes at steps 2-6 `8,051.75` tok/GPU/s, `407.6725 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `194.90 GiB`, a small `+0.28%` uplift over the previous lower-memory MBS4 reference. The profile proves the contract is active (`owner_compact` materialized rows and presort on all 288 step-2 hot-split records, no selected fallback), but step-2 attribution still shows helper backward VJP `329.4 ms` rank-max, hot-weight movement `260.8 ms`, combine wait `149.0 ms`, and weighted scatter `69.0 ms`. Decision: promote as the lower-memory MBS4 reference only. The next MoE/EP work needs first-class compact-row helper VJP/overlap, not more dense hot-weight ABI transforms.

Standard-EP helper Triton-SwiGLU follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hot_split_triton_swiglu.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hot_split_triton_swiglu.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_ownercompact_triton_swiglu_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_ownercompact_triton_swiglu_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json) reject a tempting single-variable vector-fusion gate. The same owner-compact top-8 MBS4 shape completes six steps with `CANARY_STANDARD_EP_HOT_SPLIT_SWIGLU_BACKEND=triton`, but steps 2-6 fall to `5,658.0` tok/GPU/s and `286.472` TFLOPs/GPU, about `-29.7%` versus the torch-SwiGLU owner-compact reference, while peak memory only drops to `192.44 GiB`. Decision: do not tune helper SwiGLU-only fusion further; the MoE/EP branch should stay on batched/fused helper grouped VJP and dX return overlap.

Standard-EP helper grouped-MM autograd slice: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_autograd_probe.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_autograd_probe.md), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_autograd_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_autograd_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_autograd_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_autograd_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json) isolate the actual `torch._grouped_mm` autograd helper surface. At mean/max owner-compact hot rows (`28,000`/`54,400` rows), saved-graph backward is `4.373`/`8.251 ms` and full forward+backward is `6.082`/`11.327 ms`, faster than padded full VJP (`7.014`/`13.520 ms`) but not enough to explain the full e2e helper wall.
