Read: the next MoE/EP implementation should make compact-row helper VJP plus weighted scatter/dX return first-class while preserving the standard-EP hot/cold/helper layout; more padded or activation-only wrapper toggles are the wrong hill.

Scatter-inclusive helper VJP boundary: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_boundary.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_boundary.md), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_autograd_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_autograd_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_autograd_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_autograd_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_triton_bwd_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_triton_bwd_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_triton_bwd_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_triton_bwd_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_triton_bwd_e2e_gate_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_scatter_triton_bwd_e2e_gate_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_ownercompact_triton_hotscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_ownercompact_triton_hotscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_ownercompact_triton_hotscatter_dynrows_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_ownercompact_triton_hotscatter_dynrows_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_ownercompact_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_retry_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_ownercompact_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_retry_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_quality20_mbs8_attention_ac_triton_bwdscatter_8x_s4096_gbs128_20260608.json) close the next drop-in question. Once the weighted `dX` return/scatter is included, retained torch mean/max full boundary is `7.766`/`14.543 ms`, versus grouped-MM-only `6.124`/`11.293 ms` and same-run padded full VJP `6.986`/`13.482 ms`. A new Triton scatter backward kernel fixes the old Triton-forward-only path and improves the local boundary from `7.816`/`14.867 ms` to `7.228`/`13.655 ms`; a small BF16 duplicate-index smoke matches torch exactly for both backward tensors. The first current-source 8x materialization gate with `CANARY_STANDARD_EP_HOT_SPLIT_WEIGHTED_SCATTER_BACKEND=triton` measured only `5,374.89` tok/GPU/s at step 2. Making Triton weighted-scatter `n_rows`/`dim` runtime values improves the two-step gate to `6,433` tok/GPU/s and `325.70 TFLOPs/GPU`, but it remains about `20.47%` slower than the retained MBS4 owner-compact branch. The scoped `triton_bwd` MBS4 retry completes six full 8x steps at `8,055.0` tok/GPU/s and `405.822` TFLOPs/GPU over steps 2-6, near-neutral versus the MBS4 owner-compact reference. The same backend does promote at the retained MBS8 attention-only selective-AC shape: 20 steps average `8,518.84` tok/GPU/s and `431.31 TFLOPs/GPU` over steps 2-20, `+1.03%` versus the previous AdamW MBS8 baseline and `-7.85 GiB` peak memory. Decision: keep `triton_bwd` in the retained MBS8 baseline, while the larger MoE/EP target remains a single first-class compact-row helper VJP plus weighted `dX`/`dTopK` return contract and overlap with hot `dW` reduction.

Manual compact-return helper VJP follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_vjp.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_hothelper_manual_return_vjp.md), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_manual_return_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_manual_return_meanrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_manual_return_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_manual_return_maxrows_1xmi350_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_manual_return_correctness_smoke_1xmi350_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_hothelper_groupedmm_manual_return_correctness_smoke_1xmi350_20260608.json) close the immediate "make the return path first-class in Python/autograd" idea. The manual path is correct against the padded BF16 baseline, but slower than the current Triton scatter-autograd boundary: mean rows `7.576 ms` versus `7.209 ms`, max rows `13.770 ms` versus `13.184 ms`. The explicit compact grad plus full token `dX`/`dTopK` return slice costs `1.064/2.004 ms`. Decision: do not promote another wrapper-level helper VJP. The next MoE/EP branch needs lower-level fused/batched compact-row helper backward plus overlapped hot `dW` reduction, not another `_grouped_mm` autograd island.

Owner-compact torch-prof follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_ownercompact_torchprof_hotvjp.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_ownercompact_torchprof_hotvjp.md), [`run_artifacts/standard_ep_ownercompact_hot_split_torchprof_sidecar_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps3_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/standard_ep_ownercompact_hot_split_torchprof_sidecar_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps3_20260608.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_ownercompact_torchprof_hotvjp_pf2_summary_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps3_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_ownercompact_torchprof_hotvjp_pf2_summary_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps3_20260608.json) add a less hand-wavy profile of the same MoE branch. The diagnostic step-2 window is slower (`6,145` tok/GPU/s, `311.11` TFLOPs/GPU) because profiling is active, but the mechanism read is useful: all `672` filtered hot-split records use owner-compact materialization/presort, and the lead MoE wall is helper training VJP at `719.664 ms` rank-max, corroborated by `GroupedMmBackward0` at `790.861 ms` rank-max kernel-context total. Secondary walls are combine all-to-all wait `289.472 ms`, hot-weight movement `272.417 ms`, W3 hot `dW` reduce `211.070 ms`, and weighted scatter `145.723 ms`. Decision: push first-class batched/fused helper grouped VJP and dX-return overlap; do not spend the next rung on another hot-weight transport-only swap.

Deferred hot-reorder follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_defer_hot_reorder.md`](changesets/torchtitan_standard_ep_defer_hot_reorder.md) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_standard_ep_defer_hot_reorder_decision_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_standard_ep_defer_hot_reorder_decision_20260608.json) test the adjacent idea of computing only expert counts before hot-plan selection, then materializing the final hot/cold row layout once. The flag works mechanically: late-window timing shows `standard_ep.dispatch.local_count=0.827 ms`, `standard_ep.dispatch.local_reorder=0.000 ms`, and `standard_ep.dispatch.hot_local_reorder=25.372 ms`. But the matched 8xMI350 MBS4 A/B is not a promotion: flag-on steps 2-4 average `7,846.33` tok/GPU/s and `397.273 TFLOPs/GPU` at `194.97 GiB`, while the flag-off current-code control averages `7,859.67` tok/GPU/s and `397.953 TFLOPs/GPU` at `194.65 GiB`; the then-retained baseline was `8,029.0` tok/GPU/s and `406.522 TFLOPs/GPU` at `193.80 GiB`. Decision: keep `CANARY_STANDARD_EP_DEFER_HOT_REORDER` opt-in only. The saved duplicate reorder is too small versus weighted combine/scatter, hot-weight movement, count exchange, and helper grouped-MLP work.

Rejected MORI/AITER balance rung: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_top2_smoke_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_top2_smoke_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260606.json) proves the first dummy-zero-gate attempt is the wrong shape: it activates hot-expert planning, but leaves remote-hot rows in the normal MORI/AITER owner path as fake local assignments, makes AITER see a 33-expert local shape, hits `grad_norm=nan`, then OOMs in stage1 VJP. The rejected dummy implementation is now opt-in only; the MORI/AITER `execute` implementation default is `off` until a no-expansion hot-row filter is implemented.

Rejected compact-dispatch follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_compact_dispatch_smoke_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs1_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_compact_dispatch_smoke_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs1_20260607.json) shows that the first compact-dispatch MORI/AITER port is also not materializable. The default heap attempt fails before step 1 in MORI static-heap setup; with `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=96G`, the run reaches step-1 `fwd_bwd_start` but produces no step metric after about `284s` of active 8-GPU compute and is stopped. Read: flattening normal routed assignments into a separate top-k=1 MORI/AITER dispatch avoids the dummy-zero-gate correctness issue, but duplicates token rows for normal expert slots and creates too much forward/backward work even at `MBS=1`. The next MORI/AITER helper-execute target is a no-expansion route filter inside MORI dispatch/permute, or a fused owner path that can skip remote-hot rows while preserving the original top-k token layout.

Route-mask MORI/AITER follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_routemask_cpuplan_heap80_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_routemask_cpuplan_heap80_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json) implements the no-expansion route filter and completes a 6-step `8xMI350`, `MBS=2`, `GBS=128`, no-AC run with steps 2-6 averaging `4,053.2` tok/GPU/s, `204.414 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `156.87 GiB` peak logged memory. The thresholded follow-up [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_routemask_minhelper512_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_execute_routemask_minhelper512_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json) adds `CANARY_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_MIN_HELPER_ROWS=512` and reaches `4,120.4` tok/GPU/s, `208.548 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `155.50 GiB`, only `+1.66%` tok/GPU/s over unthresholded route-mask. The recompute helper-backward follow-up [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_split_recompute_minhelper512_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_split_recompute_minhelper512_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json) completes the same shape with `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_HOT_SPLIT_BACKWARD=recompute`, but drops to `4,005.2` tok/GPU/s and `202.78 TFLOPs/GPU`, so it is rejected. These runs do not use `moe_force_load_balance`; learned top-k routing stays intact and only remote-hot rows are masked out of the owner-side MORI dispatch. Decision: not promoted. Route-mask improves over the old 8x MBS2 dense-dTopK MORI baseline, but is far below the retained MBS4 MORI/AITER anchor and standard-EP helper-execute best. The useful read is that route-mask is fit-safe at MBS2, while MBS4 still OOMs after step 1 and logs show many tiny helper AITER fused-MoE calls (`estimated_m_per_expert` near `0-23`) from the 33-local-expert helper branch. Recompute alone does not fix that. Next MoE/EP work should fuse/batch helper-side hot-row VJP, not tune route-mask dispatch filtering or saved-intermediate policy alone. Source change summaries: [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_aiter_route_mask_hot_execute.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_aiter_route_mask_hot_execute.md) and [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_aiter_hot_split_recompute.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_aiter_hot_split_recompute.md).

Top-8 MORI/AITER route-mask plus SDMA smoke: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_routemask_top8_sdma_smoke_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_routemask_top8_sdma_smoke_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps2_20260607.json) completes 2 steps at the same `MBS=2`, `GBS=128`, `FSDP8/EP8` MORI/AITER route-mask shape with `CANARY_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_HOT_EXPERTS=8`, SDMA forward hot-weight movement, and SDMA hot dW reduction. Step 2 reaches `4,330` tok/GPU/s and `219.25 TFLOPs/GPU`, with `159.20 GiB` peak logged memory. This is about `+5.09%` over the top-2 route-mask/min-helper steps-2-to-6 average, but still `-45.71%` versus the standard-EP top-8 best. Decision: not promoted; larger hot-expert count alone helps the sidecar branch but does not reproduce the Ascend/MindSpeed first-class balanced dispatcher/overlap mechanism.

Overlap-hot-forward MORI/AITER follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_routemask_top8_sdma_overlap_hotfwd_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_routemask_top8_sdma_overlap_hotfwd_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps6_20260607.json) adds `CANARY_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_OVERLAP_HOT_SPLIT_FORWARD=1`, putting helper hot-weight movement and helper grouped rows on a side stream before joining at `normal_out + hot_split_out`. It completes 6 steps at the same `MBS=2`, `GBS=128`, route-mask top-8 SDMA shape. Steps 2-6 average `4,468.6` tok/GPU/s, `35,748.8` node tok/s, `226.264 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `166.55 GiB` peak logged memory. Decision: not promoted. The overlap hook is stable and mildly positive versus route-mask/min-helper, but still `-43.97%` versus standard-EP top-8 helper execution and `-38.03%` versus the retained MBS4 MORI/AITER anchor. Logs still show tiny helper AITER calls (`estimated_m_per_expert` down to `0-23`), so the next MORI/AITER target is first-class hot/cold/helper dispatcher layout plus fused/batched helper/owner VJP, not more side-stream wrapping.

The matching timing sidecar [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_routemask_top8_sdma_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_routemask_top8_sdma_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_steps2_20260607.json) keeps step 2 at `4,306` tok/GPU/s and shows the root cause more clearly: top-8 reduces modeled owner-load skew, but the sidecar still spends `~728 ms` rank-max in listed steady helper-forward stages and `~2.13 s` rank-max in owner local VJP. Sampled SDMA hot dW reduce is already present (`w13` `10.68 ms`, `w2` `3.17 ms` rank-max over four sampled calls/rank, owner scatter sub-ms), so the missing mechanism is not partial-gradient reduction; it is batching/overlapping hot-row helper execution as a first-class MORI/AITER dispatcher graph.

Hot-helper timing follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_helper_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_helper_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json) runs the same route-mask/min-helper fused MORI/AITER shape for two steps with `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_TIMING_PATH` enabled. Step 2 lands at `4,069` tok/GPU/s and `206.00 TFLOPs/GPU`, so it is timing evidence only. The new split shows the all-call plan total is dominated by first-use/layer-0 warmup; the steadier last-half proxy is more useful. Over that proxy, rank-max helper-forward time across 96 hot-execute calls per rank is: plan `123.8 ms`, helper grouped rows `91.0 ms`, hot-weight broadcasts `64.1 ms` combined, remote mask `38.8 ms`, sort/counts `21.1 ms`, and scatter back to source tokens `15.2 ms`. Read: the helper branch is not primarily slow inside the helper grouped expert math; it is repeatedly paying planning, mask, broadcast, and sort overhead around modest hot-row compute. Next MORI/AITER helper work should cache/batch the hot plan and merge helper hot-row execution into the normal fused path rather than keep adding route-mask knobs.

Hot-plan GPU-count follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_plan_gpucounts_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_plan_gpucounts_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json) keeps the same fused MORI/AITER route-mask/min-helper timing shape but sets `CANARY_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_PLAN_BACKEND=gpu_counts`, replacing the local CPU `topk_ids` count copy with device-side `torch.bincount`. It validates and step 2 reaches `4,146` tok/GPU/s, `209.92 TFLOPs/GPU`, but the steady plan stage is unchanged: `124.19 ms` rank-max versus `123.80 ms` for the CPU-topk timing run. Remote-mask improves slightly (`38.84 -> 32.83 ms`), helper grouped rows regresses slightly (`90.99 -> 96.10 ms`), and broad timing remains dominated by `local_vjp` plus `combine_dx`. Decision: reject as a material speed path; the next MORI/AITER helper lever is caching/batching/removing the synchronized plan boundary and folding helper execution into the fused path, not just moving local route counts to GPU.

Hot-plan cache follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_plan_cachedcpu_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_plan_cachedcpu_timing_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json) tests `CANARY_MORI_AITER_BALANCED_MOE_PLAN_BACKEND=cached_cpu_topk`. It removes the steady planning stage (`0.507 ms` rank-max on all cache hits) but is rejected because the cached hot expert IDs become stale for learned routing: step-2 last-half helper rows collapse to median `0`, grouped helper work drops to `3.21 ms`, hot-weight broadcasts still cost `82.70 ms`, and step 2 is only `3,958` tok/GPU/s. A local empty-helper skip follow-up is also invalid and reverted: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_plan_cachedcpu_skipempty_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mori_aiter_hot_plan_cachedcpu_skipempty_failure_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260607.json) shows it hangs because hot-weight broadcasts are all-rank collectives. Next MORI/AITER helper work needs a bounded replan cadence or all-rank `active_any` skip protocol, not a forever-cache or per-rank skip.

Current `flash_12layer_ceiling_probe` throughput candidate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_mbs8_selective_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_adamw_mbs8_selective_attention_ac_8x_s4096_gbs128_steps6_20260608.json) completes 6 non-profiled steps at `MBS=8`, `GA=2`, checkpoint-free, standard EP, AdamW, attention-only selective AC, `CANARY_MOE_BALANCED_MOE_MODE=execute`, `CANARY_MOE_BALANCED_MOE_HOT_EXPERTS=8`, `CANARY_STANDARD_EP_HOT_WEIGHT_FORWARD_BACKEND=mori_sdma`, `CANARY_STANDARD_EP_HOT_WEIGHT_REDUCE_BACKEND=mori_sdma`, `CANARY_DEBUG_MOE_FORCE_LOAD_BALANCE=false`, `CANARY_SPARSE_MLA_COMPRESS_RATIO_ALLOWLIST=4,128`, `CANARY_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_H=64`, `CANARY_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_N=64`, `CANARY_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_D=128`, `shared_kv` query-recompute backward, and Triton LI/KL. Steps 2-6 average `8,151.0` tok/GPU/s, `65,208.0` node tok/s, and `413.292 TFLOPs/GPU`; peak logged memory is `260.04 GiB`, about `0.668x` of the `12.2k` tok/GPU/s target. The lower-memory MBS4 AdamW reference is now [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_ownercompact_materialized_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_ownercompact_materialized_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps6_20260608.json) at `8,051.75` tok/GPU/s, `407.6725 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `194.90 GiB`.

Top-4 profile follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_hot_execute_top4_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_hot_execute_top4_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_steps2_20260607.json) completes a two-step additive/module profile of the current standard-EP helper branch. The hooks are intrusive (`6,362` tok/GPU/s on profiled step 2 versus `7,774.2` clean), so use it for ranking only. Step-2 additive timing has `8.78s` step GPU time, `8.67s` fwd/bwd, `2.27s` model forward, `0.39s` loss, `6.01s` backward, and only `10.5 ms` fwd/bwd residual. Module timing shows the branch has shifted: summed backward attention is now about `3.55s` rank-max across the four microbatches, MoE about `2.13s`, and sparse shared-KV backward about `1.64s`. Read: standard EP helper execution reduces the MoE/EP skew wall enough that C4 shared-KV backward is again a first-class e2e target, while MORI/AITER still needs helper execution ported into its fused path.

Top-8 attention-detail follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_attention_detail_sparseon_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_standard_ep_top8_attention_detail_sparseon_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_20260607.json) records the matching sparse-on profile for the top-8 helper-execute branch before the SDMA hot-weight transport swap. It is intrusive (`6,256` tok/GPU/s on profiled step 2 versus the clean top-8 SDMA retained `8,029.0` tok/GPU/s), so use it for attribution only. Step-2 additive timing is `8.88s` train-step, `8.78s` fwd/bwd, `2.23s` forward, `0.42s` loss, and `6.16s` backward. Nested module timing ranks attention above MoE again: attention `3.69s`, MoE `2.14s`, SharedKV `1.63s`, dense attention layers 0/1 `0.82s`, visible attention/indexer linears `~0.56s` with `attention.wo` at `0.43s`. Read: top-8 remains the clean e2e best, but the profile does not show MoE as the only wall; C4 SharedKV and non-SharedKV attention work are now first-class optimization targets alongside staged MORI transport swaps and, eventually, a compact-row dispatcher.

Attention backend follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_attention_backend_gap_and_hipkittens_b4_sharedkv.md`](changesets/torchtitan_attention_backend_gap_and_hipkittens_b4_sharedkv.md) records the current source/runtime answer for dense attention and B4 SharedKV. Dense attention is still PyTorch SDPA in TorchTitan, and the active DSv4 dense MLA contract is `D=512`; stock AITER is faster for a D128 control (`12.38 ms` versus PyTorch `16.86 ms`) but not for D512 (`249-350 ms` AITER Triton versus PyTorch `100.56 ms`; AITER CK rejects D512 with a head-dim limit). C4/C128 use the same SharedKV query-recompute backend, but at production `B=4` C4 measures `263.40 ms` full boundary fwd+bwd with `235.56 ms` SharedKV and `12.70 ms` `wo`; C128 measures `101.09 ms` full boundary with `76.75 ms` SharedKV and `12.81 ms` `wo`. This reconciles the older B1 `~11 ms` isolated C4 gate with the profile's `~60.6 ms` C4 per-call figure: the production profile is B4, and `235.56 / 4 = 58.89 ms`.

SharedKV scaling follow-up: [`changesets/torchtitan_sharedkv_batch_scaling_and_hipkittens_next.md`](changesets/torchtitan_sharedkv_batch_scaling_and_hipkittens_next.md) adds the corrected H64/N64/D128 component split. The standalone probe now records active backend envs; an initial no-H64 env-spelling pass is superseded. Corrected C4 B4 SharedKV is `72.44 ms` fwd+bwd and `64.47 ms` backward-only, aligning with the standard-EP profile's `~60.6 ms` C4 SharedKV backward call; C128 B4 is `27.91 ms` fwd+bwd and `24.14 ms` backward-only. The old `~11.02 ms` C4 number remains a raw isolated backend-kernel gate, while the real autograd component boundary is `16.39 ms` at B1 C4. The current HipKittens full-output attempts are demoted: the per-head route-keyed dQ owner is `70.48 ms` before `dOriKV/dCmpKV/dSinks`, and the token-owned split-output HIP owner is `288.01 ms` for C4/B4. The retained HipKittens direction is to fork dense GQA backward at the resident-KV dK/dV epilogue and replace dense stores with DSv4 `dOriKV` plus route-aware `dCmpKV`, not to tune those rejected owners.

HipKittens SharedKV follow-up: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_cmp_route_scan_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_cmp_route_scan_gate_20260607.json) shows compressed-group owner metadata is cheap: C4 B4/S4096 route scan is `0.089 ms` with exact count parity after the earlier bitset pack gate. The next gate [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_cmp_owned_active_tiles_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_cmp_owned_active_tiles_gate_20260607.json) rejects the raw HipKittens KV-owned latent backward schedule as the C4 replacement: timing only the 16 active C4 compressed-group tiles is still `16.92 ms` for one D128 chunk, versus the current Triton C4 D512 source boundary at `11.02 ms`. The query-chunked follow-up [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_query_chunk_sweep_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_query_chunk_sweep_20260607.json) fixes that specific serial-sweep wall: `ATTN_QUERY_CHUNKS=8` drops the active C4 D128 kernel to `4.40 ms`, while 16 chunks is `4.49 ms` and 32 chunks is `4.65 ms`; the recheck pins the ramp as q1 `17.01 ms`, q2 `8.68 ms`, q4 `4.49 ms`, then plateau. A C128-style active-1 check is still `4.33-4.37 ms`, so the remaining wall is the dense query sweep/dQ producer, not compressed output tile count. The route-sidecar gate [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_route_sidecar_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_route_sidecar_gate_20260607.json) keeps the new ABI at `4.47 ms` with sidecar disabled, rejects the giant per-query-step sidecar (`[4,4096,64,1]`) because it crashes with `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_MEMORY_APERTURE_VIOLATION`, and validates compact block/tile metadata (`[4,16,1,4]`) at `4.63 ms`, only `+0.16 ms` or `+3.6%` over sidecar-off. The epilogue-cull follow-up [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_route_cull_epilogue_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_route_cull_epilogue_gate_20260607.json) rejects late route-aware store gating as the main lever: with `ATTN_QUERY_CHUNKS=8`, gating from 16 resident compressed tiles down to 8 tiles gives `4.45 ms`, and down to 1 tile gives `4.37 ms`; gating dQ atomics too gives `4.42 ms` for 8 tiles and `4.37 ms` for 1 tile. All-inactive early return is only `0.045 ms`, so the gate works, but any remaining active resident tile still pays the long query-sweep body. Increasing query chunks for the sparse case also loses (`16` chunks/1 tile `4.40 ms`, `32` chunks/1 tile `4.47 ms`). Read: HipKittens is alive as a producer template, but late dQ/dCmpKV epilogue/store reduction is not enough. The next gate must move route masking into the producer math before QK/P/dP/dQ and dCmpKV accumulation, or use a new source-boundary owner whose compressed-group route is part of the score/prob tile; promotion still requires beating the current `11.02 ms` C4 SharedKV D512 boundary before any 4x/8x TFLOPs run.

HipKittens C4-shaped Q/KV split follow-up: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_c4_qkvlen_decoupled_latent_epilogue_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_c4_qkvlen_decoupled_latent_epilogue_gate_20260607.json) fixes the latent-epilogue fork's shape contract from one `ATTN_N` to `ATTN_Q_N=4096` and `ATTN_KV_N=1024`, matching C4 compressed groups. This materially improves the D128 SharedKV slice: q1 is `16.97 ms`, q4 `4.33 ms`, q8 `2.43 ms`, q16 `1.90 ms`, q32 `2.03 ms`, and q64 `2.34 ms`; the q16 build has `105` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, no spills. The sink-gradient follow-up [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_c4_qkvlen_sink_grad_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_c4_qkvlen_sink_grad_gate_20260607.json) includes the production zero-value attention sink in O/LSE and times `dAttnSink` as the separate vectorized row-term reduction: q16 kernel `1.865 ms`, `dAttnSink` `0.806 ms`, serialized total `2.671 ms`, all finite. Decision: keep HipKittens alive as a C4 SharedKV backward substrate, but do not promote yet. This still omits D512 fusion, exact row-ragged LI routing, and TorchTitan e2e materialization; the next gate remains a full `SparseAttnSharedkvGrad` boundary versus the current Triton C4 `~11.02 ms` latency.

HipKittens q-chunk D512 row-term gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_qchunk_d512_rowterms_score_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_qchunk_d512_rowterms_score_gate_20260607.json) keeps the C4 q-chunk/shared-KV ownership shape (`Q=4096`, `KV=1024`, `H64/HKV1`) but extends the row-term producer to the real D512 latent dimension. It builds cleanly on MI350 (`106` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, no spills), yet the producer alone is `10.770 ms` median before production `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, or `dSinks` are emitted. The same-shape B4 rerun [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_qchunk_d512_rowterms_score_b4_c4_scale1e3_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_qchunk_d512_rowterms_score_b4_c4_scale1e3_20260607.json) is finite at `10.724 ms` median with smaller input scale; the default-scale timing is `11.117 ms` but produces nonfinite scratch sentinels. Decision: diagnostic, not promoted. The D128 q16 slice does not extrapolate cleanly to D512; the next HipKittens/HIP branch needs a different full-D schedule that reduces D512 row-term replay or changes producer ownership before adding production output epilogues.

HipKittens token-major follow-up: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_qm_h16n256_d512_score_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_qm_h16n256_d512_score_gate_20260607.json) tests a more query-major C4 schedule: one token, one H16 head slice, one selected N256 window, with four N64 warp subtiles and H-major `Q/dO` layout so HipKittens can load a head tile at a fixed token. It compiles cleanly on MI350 (`70` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, no spills) and runs finite, but the producer/scratch gate is `13.036 ms` before exact LI selected-slot gather, production `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, or `dSinks`. Decision: reject as a promotion path; it is slower than the q-chunk D512 producer and would require a source-layout change. The next material SharedKV branch should preserve Triton's H64/N64 source layout or integrate selected-slot epilogue into Triton rather than require H-major conversion.

HipKittens producer-mask gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_producer_mask_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_producer_mask_gate_20260607.json) adds `ATTN_ROUTE_MASK_MODE=6`, which carries compact block/tile route metadata into the P/dP tile boundary and zeros inactive `P_ij`/`dP_ij` tiles before dV/dK accumulation while also gating final dQ/dKV writes. It builds cleanly on MI350 (`105` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, no spills), but is rejected as a speed path: active-8 is `4.62 ms`, active-1 is `4.52 ms`, both slower than the previous mode-5 store/dQ gate (`4.42/4.37 ms`), while all-inactive remains cheap at `0.038 ms`. Read: value-culling after P/dP production is still too late for this four-warp CTA; the next HipKittens candidate must make compressed-route ownership part of the producer decomposition itself, for example one-warp/tile CTAs or a source-boundary owner whose score/prob tile is keyed by active compressed groups before QK/P/dP/dQ accumulation.

HipKittens one-warp/tile compile gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_onewarp_tile_compile_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_onewarp_tile_compile_gate_20260607.json) adds an explicit `ATTN_NUM_WARPS`/`--num-warps` contract and tries the mechanical `ATTN_NUM_WARPS=1` retile. It fails at compile time because the current owner is structurally a 256-row resident KV tile schedule: `subtile_inplace<256,32>` cannot consume the resulting 64-row `K_j_smem`, and the `dP_ij_bf16_col_T` register tile remains `256x16` while the shared tile becomes `64x16`. The default `ATTN_NUM_WARPS=4` control still builds cleanly with the same no-spill resource report. Decision: reject macro-only one-warp retile; a real route-keyed producer needs redesigned K/V shared tiles, dP transpose storage/load, and dQ/dK/dV register tile shapes.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row contract: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_contract_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_contract_gate_20260607.json) adds that structural target rather than another macro knob. It builds on MI350 with `30` SGPRs, `26` VGPRs, `8` AGPRs, no scratch/spills, and `8` waves/SIMD occupancy. The B4/S4096 one-KV-head active-tile sweep is stable in the `0.028-0.033 ms` median range for this tiny contract. Decision: promote as a structural gate only. It proves HipKittens can run a 64-row route-keyed resident tile without the old 256-row dQ page, but it is not a full SharedKV backward kernel yet. The next implementation must retile the real C4 producer around this shape and emit `dQ`, `dOriKV`, `dSinks`, and route-aware `dCmpKV` before comparing to the current `11.02 ms` Triton source-boundary gate.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row score/dQ gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_score_dq_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_score_dq_gate_20260607.json) moves the structural tile to a real source producer slice: `Q/K/V/dO -> QK -> P -> dP -> dQ` for one 64-row route-keyed D128 tile. The first generic dP transpose/store fork compiled but produced nonfinite dQ for any nonzero input; the retained fix mirrors the HipKittens reference ART register contract for Q/K/V/dO, P, dP, and the transposed bf16 dP page. The MI350 build has `86` SGPRs, `94` VGPRs, `128` AGPRs, no scratch/spills, and `2` waves/SIMD occupancy. The B4/S4096/HKV1 active-tile sweep is finite at every tested point, with median `0.0321 ms` inactive, `0.0332 ms` active-1, `0.0347 ms` active-8, `0.0346 ms` active-16, and `0.0340 ms` active-64. Decision: gate passed, not promoted. This still does not emit full-D `dQ`, `dOriKV`, `dCmpKV`, or `dSinks`; the next HipKittens step is to graft those outputs onto this valid query-major score producer and keep route-keyed compressed-group ownership in the `dCmpKV` epilogue before comparing to the current `11.02 ms` Triton C4 SharedKV source-boundary gate.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row score/dQ+dK/dV gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_score_dq_dkv_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_score_dq_dkv_gate_20260607.json) adds local `dK = dP^T Q` and `dV = P^T dO` scratch writes to the same valid score producer. The MI350 build is finite and has no spills, but the resource report jumps to `95` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, and only `1` wave/SIMD occupancy. Active-16 median is `0.0521 ms`; active-64 median is `0.0470 ms`, with finite dQ/dK/dV scratch outputs. Decision: slice gate passed, not promoted. The result proves dK/dV can be attached without breaking the query-major score page, but full `SparseAttnSharedkvGrad` cannot simply keep all outputs live in one CTA. The next branch should stage or split full-D `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, and true `dSinks` while preserving the route-keyed score producer.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row row-term dQ+dK/dV gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_rowterms_dq_dkv_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_rowterms_dq_dkv_gate_20260607.json) adds the production backward row terms to the same slice: `P = exp(QK / sqrt(D) - LSE)` and `dS = P * (dO V^T - softmax_dot)`. The first generic row-subtraction fork failed because generic `sub_row` expects RT tiles; the retained version mirrors the HipKittens dense backward ART/scalar-register contract. The MI350 build has `94` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, no scratch/spills, and `1` wave/SIMD occupancy. Active-16 median is `0.04574 ms`; active-64 median is `0.04832 ms`, with finite dQ/dK/dV/sink scratch outputs. Decision: slice gate passed, not promoted. The useful read is that production `LSE`/`softmax_dot` row terms are not the new wall; the next branch must preserve this route-keyed producer while staging/splitting full-D `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, and true `dSinks` before comparing to the current `11.02 ms` Triton C4 SharedKV source-boundary gate.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row D512 row-term gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_score_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_score_gate_20260607.json) extends the row-term producer check across the full latent D512 dimension before consuming `P/dS` through one D128 dK/dV scratch epilogue. The MI350 build passes with no spills, but is resource-heavy (`80` SGPRs, `256` VGPRs, `256` AGPRs, `1` wave/SIMD). The first active-63/64 run faulted because the D512 loop passed element offsets as HipKittens tile coordinates; fixing the loads to pass tile coordinates (`0..3`) makes production-sized S4096 source tensors run without padding. Corrected active-64 median is `0.04756 ms`, with finite dK/dV scratch. Decision: slice gate passed, not promoted. This is still not full `SparseAttnSharedkvGrad`; the next step is full-D `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, and `dSinks` before full-boundary C4 latency comparison.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row D512 row-term dQ gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_dq_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_dq_gate_20260607.json) adds a full-D dQ scratch consumer on top of the corrected D512 row-term producer. The build remains resource-healthy (`83` SGPRs, `94` VGPRs, `128` AGPRs, no spills, `2` waves/SIMD), and active-64 timing is fast at `0.04614 ms` median, but the output is invalid: active-1 still has `64` nonfinite dQ values and active-64 has absurd finite magnitude (`abs_max ~= 2.34e34`) for the synthetic input scale. Decision: rejected. The producer is not the failing piece; the dQ consumer must move to the ART-style HipKittens dense-backward register/load/MMA contract before this path can add production `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, and `dSinks`.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row D512 row-term ART dQ gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_dq_art_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_dq_art_gate_20260607.json) replaces the rejected RT dQ shortcut with the ART-style HipKittens dense-backward register/load/MMA contract and packed BF16 atomic-add output helper. The MI350 build is still spill-free (`90` SGPRs, `152` VGPRs, `128` AGPRs, `1` wave/SIMD). Debug splits isolate row terms (`0.05268 ms` active-1), ART loads without MMA/store (`0.04204 ms`), and ART MMA without store (`0.06356 ms`). The full active-64 gate is finite at `0.04758 ms` median with `2,097,152` nonzero dQ scratch values and `abs_max=4.34e-05`. Decision: slice gate passed, not promoted. This fixes the dQ validity failure but still does not emit full production `dQ`, `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, or true `dSinks`; the next comparison target remains the full C4 SharedKV boundary versus the current Triton `~11.02 ms` source-boundary gate.

HipKittens route-keyed 64-row D512 row-term full-sequence dQ gate: [`run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_dq_fullseq_gate_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/hipkittens_sharedkv_routekeyed_64row_d512_rowterms_dq_fullseq_gate_20260607.json) changes the finite ART dQ slice from scratch output to production-shaped `[B,H,S,D]` dQ over every `q_tile x kv_tile` pair. The build remains spill-free (`89` SGPRs, `152` VGPRs, `128` AGPRs, `1` wave/SIMD). H1/B4/S4096 active-64 is finite at `1.405 ms`, but the H64 C4 scale gate is `70.476 ms` before `dOriKV`, route-aware `dCmpKV`, or production `dSinks` are attached. Decision: rejected as a full-boundary direction. The ART output contract is valid, but this per-head full-sequence owner does not mirror the retained Triton H64/N64 query-major source-boundary schedule; the next HipKittens/HIP rewrite should use the Triton schedule as the spec, with true shared-KV source layout and route-aware compressed `dCmpKV` epilogue.

HipKittens/HIP Triton-schedule H64/N64 gate: [`run_artifacts/sparse_mla_source_boundary_triton_qm_h64n64_rocwmma_dqdkv_s4096_layer2_20260607.json`](run_artifacts/sparse_mla_source_boundary_triton_qm_h64n64_rocwmma_dqdkv_s4096_layer2_20260607.json) tests the opposite correction: keep one query token plus full H64 head block, process selected slots as N64 windows, and emit `dQ+dKV+d_sinks` from the same source-boundary HIP/CK producer. It is also rejected. The full C4 layer-2 boundary is `57.038 ms` event median versus the retained Triton gate around `11.13 ms`. The split artifacts show the wall is not final compressed-dKV writes: score/dQ plus d_sinks with `TRITON_QM_DKV_MODE=0` is already [`35.803 ms`](run_artifacts/sparse_mla_source_boundary_triton_qm_h64n64_rocwmma_dqdkv_mode0_s4096_layer2_20260607.json), contribution math/checksum with mode 1 is [`53.925 ms`](run_artifacts/sparse_mla_source_boundary_triton_qm_h64n64_rocwmma_dqdkv_mode1_s4096_layer2_20260607.json), and final dKV writes add only about `3.11 ms`. Decision: do not keep tuning this raw D16 HIP/CK replay owner. The next SharedKV rewrite must either preserve the real Triton producer more faithfully than this transcription, or return to the valid HipKittens route-keyed score producer and avoid per-head/full-sequence replay while adding route-aware `dCmpKV`.

4-layer to 12-layer scaling read: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash4_to_flash12_scaling_decomposition_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash4_to_flash12_scaling_decomposition_20260606.json) shows that the tok/GPU/s drop is mostly real work growth rather than a TFLOP accounting error. The retained 4-layer anchor is `12,570.33` tok/GPU/s at `237.19 TFLOPs/GPU`, or `18.87 GFLOP/token`; the current best 12-layer candidate is the standard-EP top-4 helper-execute run at `7,774.2` tok/GPU/s and `393.62 TFLOPs/GPU`, with the same active 12-layer `50.71 GFLOP/token` accounting. So FLOP/token rises `2.69x` while achieved TFLOPs/GPU rises `65.95%`. At the active 12-layer FLOP/token, the `12.2k` tok/GPU/s target requires about `619 TFLOPs/GPU`, and the current run is `0.637x` of the tok/GPU/s target. The current standard-EP profile now ranks attention above MoE, but the retained MORI/AITER path still exposes MoE/EP owner-rank VJP plus `combine_dx` wait/skew. Sparse C4 compressed-dKV remains the parallel attention-kernel track, while the MORI/AITER scaling mechanism remains helper execution plus fused compact expert backward efficiency.

Layer-owner scaling profile: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_layerowner_scaling_profile_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_layerowner_scaling_profile_20260606.json) validates the new MORI timing metadata from [`changesets/torchtitan_mori_expert_loop_detail_timing.md`](changesets/torchtitan_mori_expert_loop_detail_timing.md): `layer_idx`, `expert_start`, and `expert_end` are now present, so owner local VJP and `combine_dx` wait can be grouped by layer and owner expert range. The diagnostic runs are not throughput baselines: the full DSv4 profile path timed out in final `all_gather_object`, and the lighter MORI/additive-only path failed after step 1 at `mori_aiter_moe.py:2060` (`torch.nonzero(local_mask)`) with HSA out-of-resources. The useful read is mechanism-level: 12-layer MBS4 executes `48` routed owner-backward calls per step, hot owner rows show `~15x` compact padding multipliers, and the critical owner VJP stack is `wgrad -> forward recompute -> xgrad/reduce -> W2 dgrad+SwiGLU -> dTopK/gather`, while lighter ranks show the same skew as `combine_dx` wait. Next MoE/EP scaling work should remove the allocation-heavy route-pack/padded expert-loop path and fuse compact owner-rank training backward before more MBS or MORI tuple sweeps.

Current 4x comparison candidate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_dtopk_dense_allreduce_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_dtopk_dense_allreduce_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) completes 6 non-profiled steps at `MBS=2`, `GA=16`, `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=40G`, no AC, checkpoint-free, with dense dTopK return. Steps 2-6 average `4,327` tok/GPU/s, `17,308` node tok/s, and `219.08 TFLOPs/GPU`; peak logged memory is `214.42 GiB`. It remains the best same-node 4x comparison point, but is no longer the best per-GPU 12-layer materialized candidate.

Previous all-compressed H64/N64/D128 candidate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) completes 6 non-profiled steps at `MBS=2`, `GA=16`, `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=40G`, no AC, checkpoint-free, with `CANARY_SPARSE_MLA_COMPRESS_RATIO_ALLOWLIST=4,128`, `CANARY_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_H=64`, `CANARY_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_N=64`, `CANARY_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_D=128`, `shared_kv` query-recompute backward, Triton LI/KL, compact `ptgmm` expert wgrads, grouped xgrad, and `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_COMPACT_RECOMPUTE_MODE=expert_loop`. Steps 2-6 average `4,034.4` tok/GPU/s, `16,137.6` node tok/s, and `204.27 TFLOPs/GPU`; peak logged memory is `223.20 GiB`, about `0.331x` of the `12.2k` tok/GPU/s target. This superseded the previous C128-only compact `ptgmm` candidate (`3,925.6` tok/GPU/s, `198.74 TFLOPs/GPU`, `220.66 GiB`) by `+2.77%` tok/s and `+2.78%` TFLOPs/GPU at `+2.54 GiB` peak memory. Read: the H64/N64/D128 block shape materialized a small but real e2e uplift and made both C4 and C128 sparse layers viable in the 12-layer canary; C4 compressed dKV accumulation remains the leading sparse-attention kernel rewrite target because the isolated C4 boundary remains `11.018 ms` with an `8.179 ms` dKV accumulation wall.

8x dense dTopK-return scaling check: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_dtopk_dense_allreduce_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_heap96_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_dtopk_dense_allreduce_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_heap96_20260606.json) runs the same all-compressed 12-layer MBS2 shape at `FSDP8/EP8`, `GBS=128`, `GA=8`, heap96, no AC, checkpoint-free, and `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_DTOPK_RETURN_MODE=dense_allreduce`. Steps 2-6 average `3,358.4` tok/GPU/s, `26,867.2` node tok/s, and `170.05 TFLOPs/GPU`, with `141.86 GiB` peak logged memory. This is `+17.52%` tok/GPU/s versus the previous 8x all-compressed MBS2 anchor (`2,857.8` tok/GPU/s, `144.69 TFLOPs/GPU`) and proves the dense dTopK-return branch survives EP8. It still trails the current 4x dense-return candidate by `22.39%` per-GPU tok/s, so EP8 scaling remains a MoE/EP owner-VJP and dX-return skew problem, not solved by the dTopK return rung alone. Harness note: the first EP8 attempt used the base image and failed before metrics with `ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'mori'`; the completed run used the MORI overlay image.

8x forward-x-op reuse + Triton SwiGLU MBS4 materialization: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_reuse_forward_xop_triton_swiglu_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_heap96_steps6_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_reuse_forward_xop_triton_swiglu_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_heap96_steps6_20260606.json) reruns the EP8 MBS4 hypothesis after reusing the saved forward x dispatch op for backward and selecting Triton SwiGLU inside the compact owner VJP. It completes all 6 steps on `do-vunguyen-mi350-gpu`: steps 2-6 average `4,896` tok/GPU/s, `39,168` node tok/s, and `248.28 TFLOPs/GPU`; steps 4-6 average `4,883.67` tok/GPU/s and `247.93 TFLOPs/GPU`; peak logged memory is `167.67 GiB`. This is `+45.79%` tok/GPU/s over the previous 8x MBS2 dense-dTopK anchor and `+13.08%` over the best 4x dense-dTopK per-GPU candidate. A 2-step timing sidecar confirms `reused_forward_x_op=true` and `backward.reuse_forward_dispatch`; the paired Torch-SwiGLU 6-step run fails before step 3 on the transient `dgate = dh_f * up_f * silu_grad` allocation. Read: the user hypothesis is correct once the hidden MORI workspace/op lifetime and local VJP transient are controlled, but this row is now historical and superseded by the `stage1_recompute_cached12` MORI/AITER anchor and the standard-EP helper-execute branch. Follow-up profile [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_reuse_forward_xop_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_heap96_steps2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_reuse_forward_xop_profile_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs4_heap96_steps2_20260606.json) reaches step 2 at `4,778` tok/GPU/s and `241.94 TFLOPs/GPU` with `160.67 GiB` peak memory; additive timing shows step wall `12.15s`, forward `2.54s`, loss `0.35s`, backward `7.67s`, and fwd/bwd residual `1.11s`. MORI detail shows EP8's memory payoff is real but partial: rank 7 spends `2.08s` in owner local VJP while rank 6 spends `1.75s` in `combine_dx` wait, so the next MoE/EP scaling target is fused compact owner-rank VJP plus dX-return skew/overlap reduction, not just raising MBS.

8x dense dTopK-return MBS4/no-AC ladder before forward-x-op reuse: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_dtopk_dense_allreduce_8x_mbs4_noac_heap_ladder_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_dtopk_dense_allreduce_8x_mbs4_noac_heap_ladder_20260606.json) tested whether EP8's lower per-rank memory could pay back through `MBS=4`, `GA=4` before the reuse patch. It did not promote. Heap96, heap112, and heap128 all failed before step 1 on MORI static-heap allocations of about `1.0 GiB`; heap144 reached step 1 at only `1,593.38` tok/GPU/s and `80.68 TFLOPs/GPU`, then aborted before step 2 metrics with HSA out-of-resources and only `96 MiB` free while constructing/caching MORI backward dispatch/combine ops. Read: the failure was not the EP8 idea itself; it was hidden MORI workspace/op lifetime plus compact owner-VJP memory pressure blocking the MBS4 payoff.

W13 grouped recompute check: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_aiter_compact_w13gmm_smoke_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_aiter_compact_w13gmm_smoke_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) adds opt-in `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_COMPACT_RECOMPUTE_MODE=w13_gmm`, mirroring the Ascend grouped expert convention by concatenating W1/W3 gate-up transposed weights and recomputing gate/up with one grouped GMM. The 4xMI350 S4096/GBS128/MBS2 all-compressed two-step smoke completes finite, but step 2 is `3,899` tok/GPU/s and `197.41 TFLOPs/GPU` at `223.64 GiB`, `-5.06%` tok/GPU/s versus the retained step-2 `expert_loop` gate. Read: this validates the code path but rejects it as a throughput branch; the MoE track still needs fused compact owner-rank training backward, not another adapter-level grouped-GMM recompute variant.

Compact `aiter_compact` dX-first follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_aiter_compact_dxfirst_sync_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_aiter_compact_dxfirst_sync_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) validates `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_DX_RETURN_MODE=sync_dx_first` for the retained all-compressed MBS2 shape. The 2-step smoke passes, then the 6-step materialized run completes with steps 2-6 averaging `4,037.4` tok/GPU/s, `16,149.6` node tok/s, and `204.48 TFLOPs/GPU`, with peak logged memory `214.77 GiB`. That is only `+0.07%` tok/GPU/s versus the retained all-compressed candidate, while the late steps 4-6 average `3,968.67` tok/GPU/s, `-0.48%` versus retained. Read: the split is valid and can reduce peak logged memory by about `8.43 GiB`, but it is not a throughput promotion. Keep it as an opt-in diagnostic/lower-memory branch; the MoE path still needs fused compact grouped owner-rank training backward rather than sync-only scheduling.

MBS4 heap/VMM ladder: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mbs4_mori_heap_vmm_ladder_4x_s4096_gbs128_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mbs4_mori_heap_vmm_ladder_4x_s4096_gbs128_20260606.json) tests the retained all-compressed 12-layer shape at `MBS=4`, `GA=8`, `GBS=128`, no AC, checkpoint-free, expandable allocator, and `sync_dx_first`. Static MORI heap sizes `40G`, `48G`, `56G`, and `64G` all fail before step 1 on a `540,540,928` byte MORI allocation. The new launcher `CANARY_MORI_SHMEM_MODE=vmm_heap` pass-through gets past the fixed static-heap wall, but `96G` fails VMM VA allocation and `128G` fails with HSA out-of-resources / `0 MB` free while creating MORI dispatch/combine ops. Read: MBS4 is rejected for now and produced no materialized tok/s or TFLOPs/GPU. The retained 12-layer baseline remains MBS2 all-compressed H64/N64/D128; the next MoE work should reduce MORI op/workspace allocation and fused owner-rank backward memory rather than keep raising heap sizes.

MBS4 optimizer-memory follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_bf16opt_mbs4_fullac_heap32_failure_4x_s4096_gbs128_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_bf16opt_mbs4_fullac_heap32_failure_4x_s4096_gbs128_20260606.json) tests the same 12-layer all-compressed shape at `MBS=4`, `GA=8`, `GBS=128`, full activation checkpointing, heap32, expandable allocator, and `optimizer.implementation=fused_opt_states_bf16`. It reaches the first optimizer step but fails in the BF16 AdamW state pre-hook while allocating `exp_avg`: ranks 2 and 3 need `1024 MiB` with only `540-656 MiB` free. Read: BF16 optimizer states alone are not enough for MBS4. The Ascend reference uses optimizer-state-specific `swap_optimizer` / `virtual_optimizer`, not generic FSDP CPU offload; see [`changesets/torchtitan_optimizer_virtual_swap_mapping.md`](changesets/torchtitan_optimizer_virtual_swap_mapping.md). The AMD-equivalent memory path is a state-only AdamW virtual/swap port for DTensor shards, with `training.enable_cpu_offload` reserved as a fit-only diagnostic.

AMD swap optimizer MBS4 fit proof: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_swapopt_mbs4_fullac_fit_mori_4x_s4096_gbs128_step1_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_swapopt_mbs4_fullac_fit_mori_4x_s4096_gbs128_step1_20260606.json) adds the first portable TorchTitan `optimizer.implementation=swap_opt_states_cpu` run on the same `MBS=4`, `GA=8`, `GBS=128`, full-AC 4xMI350 shape, using the MORI overlay image and CPU-resident AdamW moments swapped in `16 MiB` chunks. It completes one optimizer step where the BF16 GPU-resident state path OOMed: loss `12.38876`, grad norm `19.375`, and logged memory `181.80 GiB`. Read: the fit problem is solved for this diagnostic shape, but throughput is not; the Python chunked update logs only `190` tok/GPU/s and `9.61 TFLOPs/GPU`, with rank-0 optimizer time about `65.56s`. The next performance rung would be a fused/pipelined C++ or HIP swap-update path, not this Python loop.
AMD swap optimizer full-param update follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_swapopt_torchparam_mbs4_fullac_fit_mori_4x_s4096_gbs128_step1_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_swapopt_torchparam_mbs4_fullac_fit_mori_4x_s4096_gbs128_step1_20260606.json) adds `TORCHTITAN_OPTIMIZER_SWAP_UPDATE_MODE=torch_param`, loading one local parameter's CPU-resident BF16 moments to device, updating the whole tensor with PyTorch AdamW tensor ops, and copying moments back. It preserves the MBS4 fit point at `181.80-181.83 GiB` and improves the one-step diagnostic from `190` to `245` tok/GPU/s (`9.61` to `12.43 TFLOPs/GPU`); rank-0 optimizer time drops from `65.56s` to `38.05s`. Read: this materializes a real optimizer swap improvement, but it is still a one-step fit/diagnostic path, not a sustained throughput baseline. The ROCm `torch._fused_adamw_` branch rejects BF16 parameters in this image, so the next serious rung is a HIP/C++ BF16 fused swap-update kernel or a ROCm mapped-memory allocator prototype inspired by `torch_npu.empty_with_swapped_memory`.
Pinned swap optimizer preflight: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_swap_optimizer_pinned_preflight_1xmi350_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_swap_optimizer_pinned_preflight_1xmi350_20260606.json) isolates one 64M-element BF16 parameter on one MI350. FP32 CPU moments now default to pinned `auto` and improve slightly versus unpinned (`19.47 ms` versus `19.82 ms` warm median), while the faster BF16/`param` diagnostic state path is `10.94 ms` pinned. Read: pinned CPU state is worth keeping, but the MBS4 full-run wall is Python per-parameter/chunk overhead, not this small transfer knob alone.

Foreach swap optimizer preflight: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_swap_optimizer_foreach_preflight_1xmi350_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_swap_optimizer_foreach_preflight_1xmi350_20260606.json) tests the next Python-level swap rung with 64M BF16 parameters split across 32 tensors. `foreach_param` is correct but not a promotion: `torch_param` warms at `13.68 ms`, while foreach batches of 4 and 8 warm at `14.15 ms` and `13.84 ms`, with peak memory rising from `0.291 GiB` to `0.417/0.584 GiB`. Read: keep `torch_param` as the best portable Python update path; the next optimizer-performance branch should be fused/pipelined HIP/C++ load-update-store or a ROCm mapped-memory allocator prototype, not more PyTorch foreach batching.

8xMI350 EP8 check: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_heap96_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_8x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_heap96_20260606.json) runs the same all-compressed 12-layer MBS2 shape at `FSDP8/EP8`, `GBS=128`, `GA=8`. Heap40 and heap64 failed before step 1 with MORI static-heap exhaustion; heap96 completed 6 steps but is rejected: steps 2-6 average only `2,857.8` tok/GPU/s, `22,862.4` node tok/s, and `144.69 TFLOPs/GPU`, with `130.61 GiB` peak logged memory. Read: 8x increases aggregate node tok/s versus 4x but loses `29.16%` per-GPU throughput versus the retained 4x candidate, so it is not a promotion path without fixing EP8 MORI allocation/skew and owner-VJP scaling.

8xMI350 MBS4 ladder: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_8x_mbs4_heap_ladder_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_8x_mbs4_heap_ladder_20260606.json) pushes MBS4 on the same 8x all-compressed shape. No candidate is promotable. No-AC heap96/112/128 fail before step 1 with MORI static-heap exhaustion; no-AC heap144 reaches only step 1 before sparse-MLA forward HSA exhaustion. Full-AC heap132 fails static heap, heap144 reaches step 2 (`2,819` tok/GPU/s, `142.74 TFLOPs/GPU`) then OOMs in compact MORI owner VJP, and heap140 reaches step 3 with steps 2-3 averaging `2,733` tok/GPU/s and `138.34 TFLOPs/GPU` before aborting in MORI backward-op creation during activation-checkpoint recompute. Lazy backward ops are worse at this shape, completing only step 1. Read: MBS4 is already slower than stable 8x MBS2 before stability, so the next 8x lever is lower MORI op/workspace pressure and lower compact owner-VJP transient memory, not larger batch or heap.

MORI owner-VJP scale-memory follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_scale_grad_chunking_preflight_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_scale_grad_chunking_preflight_20260606.json) adds bounded compact-row scaling for `dy_compact * topk_weight` under `CANARY_MORI_AITER_SCALE_CHUNK_ROWS`, replacing the full FP32 routed slab that requested `5.29 GiB` in the 8x MBS4 heap144 failure. Read: the old step-3 scale OOM is fixed, but MBS4 remains rejected because it is still below the stable 8x MBS2 anchor (`2,857.8` tok/GPU/s, `144.686` TFLOPs/GPU).

Current all-compressed profile: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_profile_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_profile_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) reruns the retained all-compressed MBS2 shape with additive, MORI, and shared-KV sidecars. It is diagnostic and not promoted: step 2 logs `3,888` tok/GPU/s, `15,552` node tok/s, `196.84 TFLOPs/GPU`, and `222.31 GiB` max logged memory, about `-3.60%` tokens versus the retained six-step average. The step-2 additive split is step wall `33.69s`, microbatch fwd/bwd `33.11s`, forward `7.00s`, loss `0.98s`, backward `19.69s`, and wrapper/residual `5.44s`. Same-rank subtraction attributes the backward wall to MORI named backward `~7.17s`, shared-KV sparse attention `~4.72s` (`~3.40s` C4 query, `~1.00s` C128 query, `~0.31s` sink), and an approximate `~7.80s` remainder. MORI detail keeps owner local VJP as the largest named branch (`~4.40s` mean, `4.96s` max), followed by `combine_dx` wait/skew (`~1.81s` mean, `2.48s` max); local VJP detail is led by wgrad, forward recompute, xgrad, and W2 dgrad/SwiGLU. Read: sparse attention work is real and materialized, but the current profile says the next optimization ladder must run in parallel across fused compact MoE owner backward, C4 dKV accumulation, and a narrower profile of the remaining dense/projection/FSDP/autograd backward bucket.

Dense-linear profile follow-up: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_dense_linear_profile_mori_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_allcompressed_h64n64d128_dense_linear_profile_mori_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) reruns the same shape with the MORI overlay image and `CANARY_PROFILE_DENSE_LINEAR_BACKWARD=true`. Shared-KV splits as `~2.33s` C4 query-recompute, `~0.69s` C128 query-recompute, and about `~0.22s` sink. Read: dense projections are real but not the shadow wall; the next attribution pass should scope FSDP/autograd/lifetime and any still-unscoped model backward work while MoE and C4 sparse attention continue in parallel.

dHidden dTopK reuse A/B: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_aiter_compact_ptgmm_dhidden_dtopk_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_aiter_compact_ptgmm_dhidden_dtopk_materialized_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) tests `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_DTOPK_MODE=dhidden` on the same retained MBS2 shape. Fused DW13 compact wgrad diagnostic: [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_compact_fused_dw13_wgrad_decision_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_compact_fused_dw13_wgrad_decision_20260606.json) tests `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_FUSED_DW13_WGRAD=true`, which concatenates compact `dgate` and `dup`, runs one grouped transpose-GMM for `dw13`, and splits it into `dw1/dw3`. Current-shape wrapper residual attribution: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_loss_lifetime_gap_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_loss_lifetime_gap_4x_s4096_gbs128_mbs2_20260606.json) parses the unique-sidecar additive trace above and ties the retained-candidate `5.405s` wrapper/residual to the earlier drop-original-loss lifetime probe. Previous guarded dense-fallback MBS2 batch-ladder candidate: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mbs2_heap_sweep_4x_s4096_gbs128_20260606.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_dsv4_flash12_mbs2_heap_sweep_4x_s4096_gbs128_20260606.json) completed 4 non-profiled steps at `MBS=2`, `GA=16`, `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=40G`, no AC, checkpoint-free.
