One-MI350 smokes pass against a PyTorch `index_add` oracle for `group_count=4`, `8`, and `16`: max diffs are `1.19e-7`, `5.96e-8`, and `2.98e-8`, with median event times `0.00736 ms`, `0.00792 ms`, and `0.00722 ms`; see [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_grouped_accum_tile_g4_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_grouped_accum_tile_g4_smoke_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_grouped_accum_tile_g8_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_grouped_accum_tile_g8_smoke_20260602.json), and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_grouped_accum_tile_g16_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_grouped_accum_tile_g16_smoke_20260602.json). This proves the no-global-partial `contrib -> LDS grouped reduce -> grouped write` contract on a tiny tile; the next real gate is expanding from K16 to the `32x256/D16` actual-LI route tile and beating the S512 scalar-local branches before S4096 timing.
- Compressed-dKV `32x256/D16` rocWMMA route-tile smoke: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_tile.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_tile.py) expands the grouped smoke to one token/selected route tile: for each token it computes selected-slot `K16xD16` contributions with rocWMMA, accumulates duplicate groups in an LDS table, and writes grouped D16 rows. The S512-like table run (`token_block=32`, `selected_block=256`, `group_count=128`) passes with max diff `1.91e-6`, median `0.902 ms`, and modeled `64x` grouped-write reduction; the S4096-like table-size run (`group_count=1024`) passes with max diff `3.58e-7`, median `0.937 ms`, and modeled `8x` reduction. See [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_tile_t32k256g128_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_tile_t32k256g128_smoke_20260602.json) and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_tile_t32k256g1024_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_tile_t32k256g1024_smoke_20260602.json). The read is mixed: the `32x256/D16` math/reduce contract and large LDS group table are valid, but a single CTA serializing all token/selected microsteps is not the production schedule. The next gate should split/parallelize the route tile across waves/CTAs or move to CK-Tile while preserving local grouped reduction; do not project the `0.9 ms` single-CTA timing directly to a full S512/S4096 layer.
- Compressed-dKV full-grid rocWMMA route pressure probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid.py) expands the same contribution body across the token/selected/D grid and compares raw selected-row global atomics, CTA-local grouped accumulation plus grouped global atomics, and a no-final-atomic partial emitter followed by `sum(dim=0)`. Small parity passes: [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_s64_g32_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_s64_g32_smoke_20260602.json) and the refreshed partial variant [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s64_g32_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s64_g32_smoke_20260602.json) match the PyTorch oracle, including grouped partial reduction, within `3.82e-6`; [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_s128_k256_g128_d512_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_s128_k256_g128_d512_smoke_20260602.json) validates the full D512 grid at max diff `1.10e-5` raw and `1.05e-5` grouped. The S512 timing-only rung is positive versus the rejected scalar local branch: grouped/partial emit both realize `64x` modeled write reduction and land at about `1.15 ms` versus raw atomic `1.43-1.45 ms`; see [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_s512_k256_g128_d512_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_s512_k256_g128_d512_timing_20260602.json) and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s512_k256_g128_d512_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s512_k256_g128_d512_timing_20260602.json). The compressed-group panel split branch is also rejected at target scale: the toy S64 panel run is parity-clean and faster (`0.112 ms` panel versus `0.130 ms` grouped), but S512 `group_panel=32` regresses to `2.00 ms` versus `1.15 ms` grouped with `4x` recompute, and S4096 `group_panel=128/256` lands at `66.95/33.70 ms` versus `21.26-21.32 ms` grouped and `9.92-9.96 ms` raw. See [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s64_g32_gp8_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s64_g32_gp8_smoke_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s512_k256_g128_gp32_d512_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s512_k256_g128_gp32_d512_timing_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s4096_k512_g1024_gp128_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s4096_k512_g1024_gp128_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json), and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s4096_k512_g1024_gp256_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_panel_s4096_k512_g1024_gp256_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json). The hard S4096 layer-2-style random-unique route is negative and now better localized: `32x256` tiles model `8.00x` write reduction but slow from `9.99 ms` raw to `21.31 ms` grouped; the partial emitter is still `20.51 ms` and the separate reduction is only `0.104 ms`. A direct-unique variant that removes local LDS atomics under the `K16` unique-route contract is correct on S64 (`max diff 2.86e-6`) and trims grouped overhead, but it only moves S4096 from `21.35 ms` grouped atomic to `19.22 ms`, still far slower than `9.96 ms` raw; see [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_direct_unique_s64_g32_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_direct_unique_s64_g32_smoke_20260602.json) and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_direct_unique_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_direct_unique_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json). A new `clustered_unique` route pattern calibrates the same kernel to the actual-LI active-list density envelope. The S64 clustered smoke passes with max diff `7.15e-7`; the target-shaped `topk512/cluster_width688` run models `23.81x` write reduction but still times `10.08 ms` raw, `20.98 ms` grouped, and `19.23 ms` grouped-direct; the average-valid proxy `topk384/cluster_width516` also models `23.81x` and scales to `7.14 ms` raw, `15.68 ms` grouped, and `14.79 ms` grouped-direct. See [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_clustered_unique_s64_k48_g128_cw80_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_clustered_unique_s64_k48_g128_cw80_smoke_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_clustered_unique_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t32k512_cw688_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_clustered_unique_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t32k512_cw688_timing_20260602.json), and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_clustered_unique_s4096_k384_g1024_d512_t32k384_cw516_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_clustered_unique_s4096_k384_g1024_d512_t32k384_cw516_timing_20260602.json). Coarser `64x512` tiles model `32x` write reduction but still take `20.77 ms` grouped; partial emit is `20.80 ms` and reduce is only `0.028 ms`. See [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t32k256_random_unique_timing_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t64k512_random_unique_timing_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_partial_s4096_k512_g1024_d512_t64k512_random_unique_timing_20260602.json), and the earlier grouped-atomic-only S4096 artifacts. This rejects a single-CTA dense LDS group table, local-atomic-only cleanup, no-final-atomic partial emission, actual-density route calibration, and recompute-per-panel group splitting as S4096 production schedules. The next branch should split the grouped reduction across waves/CTAs or use CK-Tile/rocPRIM-style segmented reduction so MFMA contribution math and local reduction both expose enough parallelism without recomputing the contribution tile per compressed-group panel.
- Compressed-dKV rocWMMA split-token follow-up: [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_split_sweep_summary_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_route_grid_split_sweep_summary_20260602.json) closes the simplest "more CTAs" branch for the full-grid route probe. On the actual-density clustered `S4096/topk512/cluster_width688` shape, shrinking `token_block` from `32` to `16` and `8` improves raw atomics from `10.08 -> 8.84 -> 8.43 ms`, but grouped atomic stays `20.98 -> 21.22 -> 21.27 ms`, grouped-direct stays `19.23 -> 19.48 -> 19.93 ms`, and no-final-atomic partial emit stays about `21.25 ms`. The separate partial reduction is tiny (`0.10-0.31 ms`), so the emitter/local-table body is the wall. This rejects token-block retuning of the dense LDS grouped kernel; the next reducer needs a sparse/segmented local topology that only touches active rows/lanes and must beat the new split raw-atomic floor of about `8.43 ms`.
- SASG ScatterAdd rocWMMA rewrite status: [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_persistent_tile_decision_20260603.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_persistent_tile_decision_20260603.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_persistent_tile_size_sweep_decision_20260603.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_persistent_tile_size_sweep_decision_20260603.json), [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_hash_tile_rewrite_decision_20260603.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_hash_tile_rewrite_decision_20260603.json), and [`run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_row_leader_tile_decision_20260603.json`](run_artifacts/compressed_dkv_rocwmma_row_leader_tile_decision_20260603.json) close the first direct implementation of `MFMA contribution math -> local grouped reduction -> reduced ScatterAdd`. The dense one-CTA persistent table is correct and positive at S128/S512 (`0.281/1.513 ms`, S512 beats the `3.08 ms` scalar-local gate), but S4096 is `132.95-136.08 ms`. Retuning `seq_chunk/selected_block` keeps S4096 flat at `130.5-136.1 ms` while modeled write reduction swings from `2.0x` to `23.8x`, proving the wall moved to the serialized producer/local-table body rather than final global writes. The sparse hash-table variant also passes S128/S512 (`0.321/1.538 ms`) but is `131.9 ms` at S4096; the K16 row-leader variant avoids LDS local atomics but still lands at `133.2 ms`. So the current answer to the Ascend-style overlap idea is: yes, this is the right ScatterAdd stage, but not with per-contribution LDS atomics or K16-local leader scans. The next branch must split MFMA producer work across many CTAs/waves and reduce compact touched-group partials with a real segmented reducer, without materializing a dense route/probability slab or losing the current `8.43-8.81 ms` sparse-atomic floor.
- Actual-LI query-major profile split: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_actual_li_query_recompute_profile.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_actual_li_query_recompute_profile.py) runs the existing Triton query-major backend profile modes on real TorchTitan LI routes. The S128 smoke [`run_artifacts/actual_li_query_recompute_profile_s128_layer2_h64n32_warm_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_query_recompute_profile_s128_layer2_h64n32_warm_20260602.json) passes dKV parity with max diff `0.0697` at BF16 tolerance. At the hard S4096 layer-2 shape [`run_artifacts/actual_li_query_recompute_profile_s4096_layer2_h64n64_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_query_recompute_profile_s4096_layer2_h64n64_20260602.json), H64/N64/D128 median timing is `1.974 ms` no-dKV, `2.795 ms` checksum-sink, and `11.081 ms` full atomic, so dKV dot math is only `~0.821 ms` while global dKV accumulation is `~8.286 ms`. Layer 3 [`run_artifacts/actual_li_query_recompute_profile_s4096_layer3_h64n32_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_query_recompute_profile_s4096_layer3_h64n32_20260602.json) is the easy contrast case: full is `1.067 ms` and global accumulation is only `~0.261 ms`.
- Ascend gap closure snapshot: [`run_artifacts/ascend_gap_closure_sparse_attention_moe_backward_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/ascend_gap_closure_sparse_attention_moe_backward_20260602.json) consolidates the current two remaining kernel gaps against the CANN AutoFuse reference. Sparse attention backward is now attributed to many-to-one compressed dKV atomic accumulation on both the retained route-slice probe and the real LI layer-2 route: actual-LI layer2 full/no-dKV/checksum-sink is `11.081/1.974/2.795 ms`, putting global dKV accumulation at `~8.286 ms`. The current query-major kernel cannot reach the D16 pressure-balanced plan through env knobs because it has four hard-coded D chunks and rejects `dim > 4 * block_d`; the next candidate is a separate or fused D16 compressed-dKV accumulator with `token_block=32`, `selected_block=512`, `head_block=64`, and `~23.8x` expected write reduction. Fixed-panel density and dynamic unique-group density are promising, but every external bridge tried so far is rejected. The production branch now has exact Triton active-group list packing at `0.848 ms` for the hard S4096 layer-2 route, and the backend decision record promotes a compile-proven gfx950 HIP/CK-Tile/rocPRIM segmented accumulator surface because TileLang is absent from the current image and the PyTorch HIP extension smoke plus scalar accumulator parity smokes pass. The scalar HIP body and no-atomic tile-partial variant are both rejected at S512, so the next kernel must be CK-Tile/MFMA-friendly rather than another scalar loop or dense partial slab. The dot-K follow-ups now separate the failure modes: dense active-group routing is rejected at S4096 (`47.26 ms`), while sparse direct atomics keep S4096 to `8.806 ms` but with actual write reduction `1.0x`, so they still land on the global dKV atomic wall. MoE training backward is also narrowed: MORI+AITER forward is integrated and fast enough, Triton SwiGLU reduces owner-rank VJP from `~7.5 ms` to `~6.4 ms`, but wgrad, xgrad/reduce, and the missing AITER/CK training-backward contract still need fused grouped training GEMM work.
- Actual-LI panelized BMM floor: [`run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s128_layer2_gp32_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s128_layer2_gp32_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer2_sc1024_gp128_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer2_sc1024_gp128_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer2_sc1024_gp512_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer2_sc1024_gp512_20260602.json), [`run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer2_sc1024_gp1024_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer2_sc1024_gp1024_20260602.json), and [`run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer3_sc1024_gp32_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/actual_li_panel_bmm_dkv_s4096_layer3_sc1024_gp32_20260602.json) test whether actual dynamic LI routes can be streamed through contiguous compressed-group BMM panels instead of materializing one full dense `[H,S,G]` route matrix. This rejects a PyTorch/launch-level panelized BMM bridge as the next layer-2 step. If we keep an MFMA dKV route, it needs a fused kernel that builds route weights and accumulates inside the tile without per-panel PyTorch scatter/BMM loops; otherwise stay with streaming sparse dKV/LI-compressor fusion work.

- Ascend TorchTitan-NPU source mapping: [`sources/references/torchtitan-npu-v0.2.2-dev/`](sources/references/torchtitan-npu-v0.2.2-dev/) is pinned at `a239d25ba71a6c2ab99e2ed57a9b2de7ac8ebdf5` and supplies the operator wrappers behind the recipe's `SparseAttnSharedkvGrad` and `SparseLightningIndexerGradKLLoss` sections. The AMD WIP now exposes an Ascend-style `sparse_attn_sharedkv(query, ori_kv, cmp_kv, cmp_sparse_indices, sinks, ...)` wrapper over the shared-KV backend. [`run_artifacts/sparse_attn_sharedkv_ascend_abi_s128_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/sparse_attn_sharedkv_ascend_abi_s128_mi350_20260601.json) passes MI350 BF16 parity against the legacy concatenated-bank ABI with output diff `0`, q/cmp/sink grad diff `0`, and ori-KV grad diff `1.49e-8`; [`run_artifacts/sparse_attn_sharedkv_ascend_abi_s4096_timing_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/sparse_attn_sharedkv_ascend_abi_s4096_timing_mi350_20260601.json) measures the same public wrapper at S4096 with `640` selected keys/query and `17.95 ms` fwd+bwd. The refreshed route-overhead verifier [`run_artifacts/sparse_attn_sharedkv_ascend_abi_s4096_route_overhead_queryrecompute_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/sparse_attn_sharedkv_ascend_abi_s4096_route_overhead_queryrecompute_20260602.json) keeps `query_recompute` with H64/N128 and shows exact public-vs-legacy parity plus only `0.189 ms` CUDA-event median overhead for the public route-split wrapper (`17.947 ms` public versus `17.758 ms` prebuilt concatenated-bank), so wrapper/index/cat overhead is not the shared-KV wall. The AMD WIP also ports the LI loss contract shape in [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/model.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/model.py): forward returns a dummy zero scalar, backward recomputes the selected sparse KL oracle, and gradients flow only to LI index tensors. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_deferred_li_kl_loss_cpu_s16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_deferred_li_kl_loss_cpu_s16_20260601.json) matches the direct oracle exactly on CPU; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_deferred_li_kl_loss_mi350_bf16_s128_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_deferred_li_kl_loss_mi350_bf16_s128_20260601.json) passes on MI350 BF16 with max grad diff `3.82e-6`; and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_public_abi_mi350_bf16_s128_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_public_abi_mi350_bf16_s128_20260601.json) verifies the public Ascend-style wrapper with Flash-shaped S128 tensors at max grad diff `1.91e-6`. The original public LI timing probe keeps the current limitation visible: S128 is `1.36 ms` median with `1.44 GiB` peak, S1024 is already `67.57 ms` median with `80.48 GiB` peak, S2048 OOMs on a `128 GiB` allocation, and S4096 OOMs on a `256 GiB` allocation. The WIP first added auto-chunked LI KL backward recompute to cap selected-main-K materialization: forced S128 `chunk_size=16` matches the direct oracle within `9.54e-7` and drops peak to `0.32 GiB`; S1024 auto-chunk passes at `78.25 ms` and `2.71 GiB`; S2048 passes at `4029 ms` and `2.84 GiB`; S4096 passes at `4280 ms` and `3.10 GiB`; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked16_s128_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked16_s128_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked_auto_s1024_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked_auto_s1024_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked_auto_s2048_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked_auto_s2048_mi350_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked_auto_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_lightning_indexer_grad_kl_loss_chunked_auto_s4096_mi350_20260601.json). [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/sparse_li_triton_backend.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/sparse_li_triton_backend.py) now exposes an opt-in `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_LI_KL_BACKEND=triton_tl_dot` backend over the public deferred wrapper: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_kl_triton_backend_public_abi_sharedkv_s128_mi350_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_kl_triton_backend_public_abi_sharedkv_s128_mi350_20260602.json) passes shared-KV S128 BF16 parity with max grad diff `9.54e-7`, and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_kl_triton_backend_public_abi_sharedkv_s4096_timing_mi350_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_kl_triton_backend_public_abi_sharedkv_s4096_timing_mi350_20260602.json) times S4096 at `4.17 ms` median and `0.64 GiB` peak. This removes the public LI-KL wrapper's multi-second S4096 chunked-PyTorch wall when selected, but it is still an unfused multi-kernel backend that must be fused into sparse MLA/compressor backward before final promotion.
- Sparse LI compact-logit Triton prototype: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_grad_triton.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_grad_triton.py) now checks a clamp-correct analytic backward for the `SparseLightningIndexerGradKLLoss` shape without materializing selected main-K. It materializes compact main logits and per-head LI logits, reduces LI logits explicitly, honors the `log(index_probs.clamp_min(1e-10))` reference derivative, and computes `d_query_index`, `d_key_index`, and `d_weights` with Triton atomics. MI350 parity passes at S32 FP32 with max grad diff about `1.5e-10`; Flash-shaped S128 BF16 passes with max grad diff `1.0e-6`, valid LI-logit diff `4.58e-5`, and `1.37 ms` median / `0.18 GiB` peak. Timing-only long-shape results are much better than the chunked PyTorch bridge but still not production: S1024 `21.60 ms` / `0.35 GiB`, S2048 `77.33 ms` / `1.09 GiB`, and S4096 `220.18 ms` / `2.18 GiB`; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s128_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s128_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s1024_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s1024_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s2048_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s2048_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s4096_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_triton_s4096_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json). The conclusion is that compact logits fix memory and validate the clamp-aware math, but the S4096 path needs an MFMA/CK-style fused schedule rather than scalar per-row dot loops.
- Sparse LI compact-GEMM floor: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact.py) tests the same clamp-aware compact-logit LI loss using prefix-selected `torch.bmm` as a library-GEMM floor. This is not a general dynamic-top-k implementation, but it isolates the scalar-dot issue. S128 BF16 passes oracle with max grad diff `8.52e-6` and `1.33 ms` median. Timing-only long shapes are S1024 `1.43 ms` / `0.68 GiB`, S2048 `3.28 ms` / `1.91 GiB`, and S4096 `5.82 ms` / `3.62 GiB`; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s128_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s128_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s1024_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s1024_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s2048_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s2048_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s4096_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_torch_compact_s4096_flashshape_mi350_20260601.json). This changes the LI conclusion: the math can live in the few-ms range on MI350 when expressed as compact GEMMs, so the production work should turn arbitrary LI top-k into MFMA-friendly tiled/gathered GEMM blocks rather than continue scalar rowwise Triton dots.
- Sparse LI dynamic-gather floor: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_grad_dynamic_gather.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_grad_dynamic_gather.py) measures the row-varying LI-index half only, using materialized selected `key_index` rows plus `torch.einsum`/autograd against a uniform target distribution. It intentionally excludes main-attention target-prob construction. For shifted dynamic indices, MI350 BF16 timing is S128 `1.12 ms`, S1024 `4.24 ms`, S2048 `14.94 ms`, and S4096 `17.43 ms` / `3.23 GiB`; prefix indices through the same materialized gather/einsum path are also S4096 `17.41 ms`, so the gap versus the compact-GEMM floor is the per-row selected-key materialization/per-token batched work, not just dynamic index disorder. See [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_dynamic_gather_shifted_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_dynamic_gather_shifted_s4096_mi350_20260601.json) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_dynamic_gather_prefix_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_grad_dynamic_gather_prefix_s4096_mi350_20260601.json). The production implication is narrower: do not materialize per-row selected `key_index` for long sequence; use an in-kernel gathered MFMA tile that keeps key rows in LDS/register tiles and accumulates dQ/dK/dW directly.
- Sparse LI gathered-`tl.dot` logits probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_logits_triton_dot.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_logits_triton_dot.py) tests the next production shape for LI index logits only: gather `key_index` rows inside a Triton `tl.dot` tile, apply ReLU plus LI weights, and reduce directly to `[B,S,K]` without writing `[B,S,K,D]` selected keys or `[B,S,H,K]` head logits. S128 shifted BF16 parity against the materialized PyTorch reference passes with max diff `0.607`. At S4096, retained `H16/K128/D64` timing is shifted `0.303 ms` and prefix `0.298 ms`, peak `0.106 GiB`, avoiding a `512 MiB` selected-key buffer; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_logits_triton_dot_shifted_s4096_h16k128d64_timing20_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_logits_triton_dot_shifted_s4096_h16k128d64_timing20_mi350_20260601.json) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_logits_triton_dot_prefix_s4096_h16k128d64_timing20_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_logits_triton_dot_prefix_s4096_h16k128d64_timing20_mi350_20260601.json). This is positive schedule evidence, not the full LI backward: target-prob construction, KL derivative, `dQ/dK/dW`, and attention/compressor integration still need the fused backward kernel.
- Sparse LI target-probability `tl.dot` producer: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_target_probs_triton_dot.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_target_probs_triton_dot.py) computes the main-attention target distribution `p` from `q_main + shared compressed_k + top_indices` with a gathered Triton dot tile, then reduces per-head softmax probabilities directly to `[B,S,K]`. It does not write selected main-K or `[B,S,H,K]` logits/probabilities. S128 shifted BF16 parity passes with max diff `5.96e-8`; S4096 shifted parity passes with max diff `2.98e-8` and median `0.969 ms` / `0.374 GiB` peak, while the timing-only pass is `0.929 ms` / `0.282 GiB`. The reference path would materialize `2.0 GiB` selected main-K plus two `0.5 GiB` per-head score/probability tensors. See [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_target_probs_dot_shifted_s4096_check_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_target_probs_dot_shifted_s4096_check_mi350_20260601.json) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_target_probs_dot_shifted_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_target_probs_dot_shifted_s4096_mi350_20260601.json).
- Sparse LI gathered-`tl.dot` backward-gradient probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_index_backward_triton_dot.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_index_backward_triton_dot.py) extends the same no-selected-buffer schedule to the LI index-gradient slice. Given upstream `d_index_logits`, it recomputes gathered LI head logits inside Triton dot tiles and writes `d_index_q`, `d_index_k`, and LI weight gradients without selected `[B,S,K,D]` or `[B,S,H,K]` workspaces. S128 shifted BF16 parity passes at retained `H64/K64/D64` with max diffs `dQ=0.124`, `dK=5.50` versus `dK` norm `2991`, and `dW=0.486`. At S4096 shifted, the original `H64/K64/D64` point was `7.03-7.09 ms` full, split as `q+w 3.29 ms` and `dK 3.83-3.89 ms`, with `0.34 GiB` peak and a `512 MiB` selected-key buffer avoided. The 2026-06-01 tile sweep now retains `H64/K512/D128` with `dot-block-d=64`: full `3.20 ms`, `q+w 0.59 ms`, and `dK 2.71 ms`; `H64/K512/D128` with `dot-block-d=128` regresses to `4.76 ms`, `H32/K512/D128` regresses to `5.71 ms`, and `H128/K512/D128` exceeds shared memory. See [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_index_bwd_tldot_s4096_h64k512d128dot64_full_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_index_bwd_tldot_s4096_h64k512d128dot64_full_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_index_bwd_tldot_s4096_h64k512d128dot64_qw_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_index_bwd_tldot_s4096_h64k512d128dot64_qw_mi350_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_index_bwd_tldot_s4096_h64k512d128dot64_k_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_index_bwd_tldot_s4096_h64k512d128dot64_k_mi350_20260601.json). This is a useful backward slice, but still not the full LI loss: the separately proven target-probability producer and clamp-aware KL derivative must feed `d_index_logits`, then all slices have to fuse with sparse MLA/compressor backward. The remaining LI-gradient hotspot is still dK accumulation.
- Sparse LI KL-derivative probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_kl_derivative.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_kl_derivative.py) isolates the clamp-aware `target_probs + index_logits -> d_index_logits` step. S128 parity passes with max diff `1.82e-12`; S4096 parity passes with max diff `2.84e-14`. The warmed S4096 median is only `0.057 ms` with `0.049 GiB` peak, so this derivative is not a meaningful bottleneck once target probabilities and LI logits exist. See [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_kl_derivative_s4096_check_timing_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_kl_derivative_s4096_check_timing_mi350_20260601.json). The remaining LI work is fused composition: target-prob producer plus KL derivative plus LI `dQ/dK/dW`, integrated with sparse MLA/compressor backward instead of run as separate diagnostic kernels.
- Sparse LI full-pipeline `tl.dot` floor: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_full_pipeline_tl_dot.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_li_full_pipeline_tl_dot.py) composes the no-selected-buffer target-probs producer, LI index-logit producer, clamp-aware KL derivative, and LI `dQ/dK/dW` gradient tile as separate Triton calls. S128 shifted BF16 parity passes end-to-end with target diff `5.96e-8`, index-logit diff `0.430`, `d_index_logits` diff `3.03e-7`, and gradient diffs under `9e-6`. At S4096 shifted, the original unfused full pipeline was `8.31 ms` median with `0.78 GiB` peak; stage medians were target_probs `0.927 ms`, index_logits `0.292 ms`, KL derivative `0.052 ms`, and LI gradients `7.07 ms`. With the retained `H64/K512/D128` LI-gradient tile, the S128 parity gate still passes and the S4096 unfused full pipeline drops to `4.49 ms` median with the same `0.78 GiB` peak; stage medians are target_probs `0.954 ms`, index_logits `0.297 ms`, KL derivative `0.053 ms`, and LI gradients `3.18 ms`. See [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_full_pipeline_tl_dot_shifted_s128_bwd_h64k512d128dot64_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_full_pipeline_tl_dot_shifted_s128_bwd_h64k512d128dot64_mi350_20260601.json) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_full_pipeline_tl_dot_shifted_s4096_bwd_h64k512d128dot64_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_li_full_pipeline_tl_dot_shifted_s4096_bwd_h64k512d128dot64_mi350_20260601.json). This confirms the old LI bridge's seconds/OOM behavior is gone in the diagnostic floor, but the production path still has to fuse this floor into the sparse MLA/compressor backward and avoid launching it as a separate side pipeline.
- Fused sparse MLA/LI implementation contract: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_li_kernel_contract_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_li_kernel_contract_20260601.json), generated by [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/plan_torchtitan_sparse_mla_li_kernel.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/plan_torchtitan_sparse_mla_li_kernel.py), pins the real TorchTitan Flash compressed-layer boundary for `B=1`, `S=4096`, `H=64`, `Dq=Dv=512`. It distinguishes the old `1a` attention microbench as a forward/perf anchor rather than a drop-in training path. For `compress_ratio=4`, the materialized selected K/V state would be `640` keys/query and about `320 GiB` BF16; for `compress_ratio=128`, it would be `160` keys/query and about `80 GiB` BF16. The target kernel must therefore keep the `manual_stream` row-stat/output save contract while fusing dynamic LI top-k gather, online softmax/value accumulation, backward recomputation, and scatter-add gradients for `dQ/dK/dV/dCompressedK/dCompressedV`.
- Fused sparse MLA backend hook: [`changesets/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_backend_hook.md`](changesets/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_backend_hook.md) adds an explicit `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_PYTORCH_SPARSE_MLA_BACKWARD_MODE=fused` mode to the TorchTitan WIP. It requires `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_SPARSE_MLA_KERNEL_MODULE` to expose `sparse_mla(q, k, v, compressed_k, compressed_v, local_indices, csa_indices, invalid, scale) -> Tensor` with autograd support; it deliberately does not silently fall back to `manual_stream`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_backend_missing_abi_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_backend_missing_abi_20260601.json) validates that the missing-backend state fails fast in the TorchTitan ROCm image. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_reference_backend_abi_s16_cpu_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_reference_backend_abi_s16_cpu_20260601.json) validates the positive import/call/autograd ABI path using the non-production `torchtitan.models.deepseek_v4.sparse_mla_reference_backend`, which delegates to `manual_stream`. This makes the next production kernel pluggable and measurable through the existing mode parity gate, while keeping current `fused` status honest: ABI hook present, reference shim proven, real fused backend pending.
- Experimental Triton-forward sparse MLA backend: [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/sparse_mla_triton_forward_backend.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/sparse_mla_triton_forward_backend.py) is the first kernel-backed fused ABI candidate in this experiment. It runs a Triton forward kernel and recomputes `manual_stream` in backward, so it is useful for bring-up but not yet the production S4096 fused fwd+bwd kernel. The backend accepts `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_TRITON_SPARSE_MLA_BLOCK_V` for value tiles and `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_TRITON_SPARSE_MLA_BLOCK_KEYS` for selected-key chunks. The earlier S32/S64 full-value-tile checks pass BF16 parity, with the best S32 timing point at `BLOCK_V=512`: `6.91 ms` candidate versus `7.33 ms` `manual_stream` in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_backend_parity_s32_blockv512_timing20_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_backend_parity_s32_blockv512_timing20_mi350_bf16_20260601.json). The chunked selected-key path now extends the fused ABI candidate beyond the old one-shot key-vector limit: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s128_blockk128_blockv512_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s128_blockk128_blockv512_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) passes at `S=128`, `selected_keys=160`; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s512_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s512_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) passes with the sparse guard disabled at `S=512`, `selected_keys=256`; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s1024_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s1024_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) passes at `S=1024`, `selected_keys=384`; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s2048_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s2048_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) passes at `S=2048`, `selected_keys=640`; and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s4096_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_parity_s4096_blockk128_blockv512_sparse_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) passes at `S=4096`, `selected_keys=640`, max output diff `0.00390625`, max input-grad diff `3.73e-9`, max param-grad diff `5.96e-8`, and no nonfinite diffs. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_preflight_s4096_s4096cap_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_triton_forward_chunked_preflight_s4096_s4096cap_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) records `MAX_PROMOTED_SEQ_LEN=4096` and correctly rejects production promotion because it is forward-only Triton bring-up, uses reference backward, and is not marked long-sequence-capable.
- Forward-only sparse MLA timing probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward.py) measures the attention forward path with gradients enabled by default, reports both CUDA-event and wall-clock samples, compares against the `3.6 ms` S4096 attention-forward anchor, and keeps correctness separate from fwd+bwd parity. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_probe_cpu_smoke_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_probe_cpu_smoke_20260601.json) passed inside the TorchTitan image on CPU at `S=16`, comparing `manual_stream` to the fused reference backend with exact output match and sparse path active. The S4096 MI350 timing is now measured in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_s4096_timing_summary_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_s4096_timing_summary_20260601.json): the correctness/timing anchor at `BLOCK_KEYS=128`, `BLOCK_V=512`, grad-enabled training forward passed against `manual_stream` with max output diff `0.00390625`, but took `98.75 ms` CUDA-event mean, `27.43x` slower than the `3.6 ms` target. No-grad at the same tile shape was essentially identical at `98.71 ms`, so the gap is in the current kernel/body rather than autograd bookkeeping. The quick no-grad sweep found `BLOCK_KEYS=64`, `BLOCK_V=512` best at `88.04 ms`, still `24.46x` off target; smaller value tiles were worse (`120.12 ms` at `V=128`, `142.59 ms` at `V=256`). The follow-up rocprofv3 summary in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_s4096_rocprof_kernel_summary_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_s4096_rocprof_kernel_summary_20260601.json) attributes `158.996/176.410 ms` of profiled GPU kernel time across two forwards to `_sparse_mla_forward_kernel` itself (`90.1%`), while projection GEMMs total only `4.263 ms` (`2.4%`). A subsequent tile retune in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_s4096_blockd_sweep_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_forward_s4096_blockd_sweep_20260601.json) adds `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_TRITON_SPARSE_MLA_BLOCK_D` and promotes the best observed defaults to `BLOCK_KEYS=64`, `BLOCK_D=128`, `BLOCK_V=512`: default S4096 no-grad correctness passes against `manual_stream` at max diff `0.00390625`, and the clean default training-graph forward timing is `84.55 ms`, still `23.49x` off the `3.6 ms` target. A standalone direct-backend synthetic probe on `do-sonle-kernel` removes TorchTitan import overhead and confirms the same schedule bottleneck: S64 combined-source and split-source both pass BF16 parity at max diff `0.00390625`, but at S4096 the combined-source kernel is `74.66 ms` with a training graph and `74.67 ms` no-grad, while the split-source variant regresses to `86.96 ms`; see [`run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_default_s4096_synthetic_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_default_s4096_synthetic_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_default_s4096_synthetic_nograd_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_default_s4096_synthetic_nograd_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_split_sources_s4096_synthetic_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_split_sources_s4096_synthetic_20260601.json). The selected-key sweep in [`run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_selected_key_sweep_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/kernel_node_sparse_mla_selected_key_sweep_20260601.json) shows the rowwise schedule is almost linear in compressed selected keys: CSA-only `128/256/384/512` keys measure `17.98/35.76/53.28/70.49 ms`. This keeps the combined-source default and reinforces that the larger lever remains a different sparse MLA/LI kernel schedule with multi-query MFMA-friendly QK/PV tiles, query/key reuse, and a production backward path.
- Shared latent-KV sparse MLA forward probe: [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/sparse_mla_shared_kv_triton_forward_backend.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/deepseek_v4/sparse_mla_shared_kv_triton_forward_backend.py) is the corrected DeepSeek-V4 sparse MLA naming for the reference-style shared latent-KV schedule. It exposes `sparse_mla_shared_kv(q, kv, attn_sink, indices, scale)`, separate from the older per-head `sparse_mla(...)` fused ABI. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_preflight_s4096_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_preflight_s4096_20260601.json) shows MI350 BF16 S64 correctness and backward smoke passed with max output diff `0.015625`, nonzero `q/kv/attn_sink` gradients, and isolated S4096 Flash-shape grad-enabled forward timing at `1.66 ms` median / `1.67 ms` mean for `H=64`, `D=512`, `selected=640`, `BLOCK_H=16`, `BLOCK_N=128`. [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary.py) now measures the next boundary: TorchTitan-shape `q/wkv_a/RoPE/LightningIndexer/compression/shared-KV sparse MLA/wo` without `wkv_b` per-head K/V expansion. The S64 MI350 backward smoke passes with nonzero input and sink gradients in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_s64_smoke_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_s64_smoke_20260601.json), and the S4096 boundary forward in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_s4096_timing_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_s4096_timing_20260601.json) reports output `[1,4096,4096]`, `640` selected keys/query, `kv_bank [1,5120,512]`, `4.83 ms` CUDA-event median, and `2.87 GiB` peak allocation. The backend now replaces autograd-reference backward with explicit PyTorch softmax/score/value/sink/scatter math: CPU parity in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_cpu_smoke_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_cpu_smoke_20260601.json) matches reference gradients within `1e-9`, MI350 BF16 parity in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s64_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s64_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) has max `dQ/dKV/dSink` diffs `5.96e-8` / `8.58e-6` / `1.22e-7`, and refreshed S4096 grad-enabled forward timing in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s4096_forward_timing_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s4096_forward_timing_20260601.json) is `1.71 ms` median. The preflight now also records saved tensors and fwd+bwd timing: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s128_savedstate_bwdtiming_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s128_savedstate_bwdtiming_20260601.json) passes MI350 BF16 parity at `S=128` with `selected_state_saved=false`, max `dKV` diff `8.11e-6`, `0.0316 GiB` saved tensors, and `0.926 ms` fwd+bwd median; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s4096_bwdtiming_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_explicit_backward_s4096_bwdtiming_20260601.json) records diagnostic explicit-PyTorch fwd+bwd at `S=4096`, `640` selected keys/query, `45.63 ms` median, and `32.48 GiB` peak allocation. [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/profile_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/profile_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward.py) then attributes that wall: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_attr_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_attr_s4096_mi350_20260601.json) shows `scatter_grad_kv` at `21.34 ms` median, `47.8%` of the component median sum, followed by selected-KV gather `3.17 ms`, selected-score dKV math `2.98 ms`, selected-gradient add `2.72 ms`, selected-value dKV math `2.55 ms`, score recompute `2.42 ms`, dQ `2.28 ms`, and dO.V `2.23 ms`. The same evidence records why it is still not production-promotable: backward is still explicit PyTorch scatter math rather than a fused Triton/HIP kernel, the real TorchTitan shared-KV model path still needs full pretraining-image validation, and LightningIndexer/compressor backward are not fused. The memory-shape comparison remains the important direction signal: the current per-head materialized selected K/V would be `320.0 GiB` BF16 at S4096, while a shared latent one-bank materialization would be `2.5 GiB` and the target output plus two row stats is about `0.252 GiB`.
- Shared latent-KV dKV scatter follow-up: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter.py) checks dKV scatter replacements before writing the fused output-row backward kernel. The PyTorch-only pass kept flat `index_add` best at S128 (`0.328 ms`) and split local/compressed `index_add` best at S4096 (`20.27 ms` versus `21.21 ms` flat); see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_variants_s128_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_variants_s128_mi350_20260601.json) and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_variants_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_variants_s4096_mi350_20260601.json). The newer Triton atomic scatter probe adds a correctness-filtered ranking: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_triton_atomic_flatgrid_s128_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_triton_atomic_flatgrid_s128_mi350_20260601.json) finds S128 correct atomic scatter at `0.080 ms`, and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_triton_atomic_correct_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_scatter_triton_atomic_correct_s4096_mi350_20260601.json) finds S4096 correct atomic scatter at `4.17 ms` (`bm4/bd128` or `bm8/bd64`) while rejecting the faster `bm4/bd32` raw point because it fails parity. The backend auto path now uses Triton atomic scatter on CUDA and keeps PyTorch fallback otherwise: S128 parity plus no-selected-state saved tensors pass at `0.672 ms` fwd+bwd median in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_triton_atomic_s128_savedstate_bwdtiming_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_triton_atomic_s128_savedstate_bwdtiming_20260601.json), and S4096 diagnostic fwd+bwd drops to `27.84 ms` median / `27.71 GiB` peak in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_triton_atomic_s4096_bwdtiming_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_triton_atomic_s4096_bwdtiming_20260601.json). The post-atomic component profile in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_attr_s4096_triton_atomic_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_attr_s4096_triton_atomic_mi350_20260601.json) has component median sum `27.05 ms` and wall median `27.37 ms`: scatter is still largest at `4.40 ms` but only `16.3%`, followed by selected-KV gather `3.16 ms`, selected-gradient score/value/add pieces around `2.6-2.9 ms`, and score/value/dQ pieces around `2.1-2.2 ms`. This moves the measured bottleneck past raw dKV scatter but is still a mixed explicit PyTorch/Triton bridge, not the production fused sparse MLA/LI backward.
- Shared latent-KV backward fusion probes: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dq.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dq.py) isolates a Triton dQ recompute kernel using the same tiled shared-KV schedule as forward. It passes MI350 BF16 parity at S128 and S4096 with max dQ diff `0.015625`; at S4096 it cuts the PyTorch dQ reference chain from `12.10 ms` to `2.27 ms` and peak memory from `10.48 GiB` to `1.60 GiB`; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dq_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dq_s4096_mi350_20260601.json). The companion dKV experiment fuses selected-gradient construction with atomic scatter from materialized `probs` and `grad_logits`, but this simple fusion is a negative result: the default S4096 fused line is `14.67 ms`, the best quick tile seen is `14.32 ms`, and the whole component profile is slower than the current PyTorch GEMM selected-gradient plus Triton atomic scatter bridge despite lower peak memory; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_attr_s4096_fused_selected_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_attr_s4096_fused_selected_mi350_20260601.json). The forward optimization mechanism transfers cleanly to dQ, but not to dKV's many-to-one shared-KV scatter.
- Shared latent-KV no-materialized dKV recompute probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dkv.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dkv.py) recomputes QK, dO.V, probabilities, and grad logits inside a Triton tile, then atomic-adds directly into the shared latent KV gradient. S128 and S4096 pass with BF16-level tolerance (`max_abs_diff` about `0.045-0.048`, small versus dKV norm). The first S4096 tile (`m16/h16/d64`) cuts peak memory from `29.40 GiB` for the PyTorch dKV reference chain to `0.86 GiB`, but is slow at `70.22 ms`; the first sweep found `m16/h32/d128` at `19.98 ms`, and the wider follow-up finds the best retained diagnostic tile at `m16/h64/d512`, `16.36 ms`, with the same `0.86 GiB` peak memory; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dkv_recompute_s4096_m16h64d512_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dkv_recompute_s4096_m16h64d512_mi350_20260601.json). [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined.py) then tested a combined dQ+dKV recompute tile. It passes S4096 parity, but is a negative schedule: `84.56 ms` combined versus `18.40 ms` for separate dQ plus tuned dKV at the same `m16/h64/d512` tile; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_s4096_m16h64d512_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_s4096_m16h64d512_mi350_20260601.json). [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dkv_structured.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dkv_structured.py) tests a structured local-window plus prefix-CSA inverse-route reduction that writes per-key partials and reduces without hot-path atomics; it is much more accurate (`S4096` max diff about `5e-5`) but performance-negative. The prior best is `140.67 ms` at `block_s=4` with a `1.25 GiB` partial buffer, and a fresh larger-block/lower-scratch sweep records `432-483 ms`; see [`run_artifacts/structured_dkv_inverse_route_sweep_20260601/summary.json`](run_artifacts/structured_dkv_inverse_route_sweep_20260601/summary.json). The next production design should keep dQ query-major and keep dKV query-key reuse; simply removing atomics by switching to key-major scratch reduction loses too much reuse and memory bandwidth.
- Shared latent-KV query-major combined backward probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/benchmark_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined.py) now also tests `sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_dq_dkv_query_recompute`, a diagnostic Triton kernel that keeps dQ accumulation query-major and atomically accumulates only dKV. At S128 Flash dimensions it passes and improves combined timing to `0.469 ms` versus `0.763 ms` for the old key-major combined line and `0.742 ms` for separate dQ+dKV. At S4096, default H16/N128 is still slow (`54.89 ms`), but setting `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_TRITON_SPARSE_MLA_SHAREDKV_BLOCK_H=64` gives a retained S4096 H64/N128 median of `14.46 ms` across three samples, with max dQ diff `0.01315`, max dKV diff `0.04513`, and `1.36 GiB` peak allocation; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n128_s4096_timing3_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n128_s4096_timing3_mi350_20260601.json). A refreshed five-sample tile check on the current backend keeps the same conclusion: raw query-major H64/N64 is best but only slightly faster at `14.36 ms`, H64/N128 is `14.53 ms`, H64/N32 regresses to `18.72 ms`, and H32/N64 regresses to `36.65 ms`; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n64_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n64_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n128_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n128_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n32_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h64n32_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h32n64_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_combined_query_h32n64_s4096_timing5_current_mi350_20260601.json). A clean route-slice rerun at H64/N64 then attributes the raw slice: full local128+compressed512 is `14.39 ms`, local128-only is `3.83 ms`, and compressed512-only is `11.02 ms`; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_query_h64n64_route_full_s4096_timing5_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_query_h64n64_route_full_s4096_timing5_mi350_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_query_h64n64_route_local128_only_s4096_timing5_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_query_h64n64_route_local128_only_s4096_timing5_mi350_20260601.json), and [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_query_h64n64_route_compressed512_only_s4096_timing5_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_backward_query_h64n64_route_compressed512_only_s4096_timing5_mi350_20260601.json). The focused compressed-only tile sweep in [`run_artifacts/shared_kv_compressed_tile_sweep_20260601/summary.json`](run_artifacts/shared_kv_compressed_tile_sweep_20260601/summary.json) keeps H64/N64 at `10.997 ms`; no smaller head tile or larger key tile improves it. The backend now wires this as an opt-in autograd bridge with `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_SPARSE_MLA_SHAREDKV_BACKWARD_MODE=query_recompute`; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_query_autograd_s4096_bwdtiming_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_shared_kv_query_autograd_s4096_bwdtiming_mi350_20260601.json) passes S128 gradient parity and no-selected-state checks, then measures S4096 `sparse_mla_shared_kv(...).backward()` fwd+bwd at `17.73 ms` median with `3.17 GiB` peak. This is still diagnostic: LI/compressor backward and the full TorchTitan layer path are not fused, and the route-slice plus tile-sweep results say the next single-GPU attention cut should focus on compressed top-k dKV/scatter/dynamic selected-group reuse.
- Shared latent-KV TorchTitan-shape boundary fwd+bwd: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary.py) now has a backward timing loop. With the query-major shared-KV backward mode, S128 passes with nonzero input/sink gradients and `2.36 ms` fwd+bwd. At S4096 layer 2, the boundary `q/wkv_a/RoPE/LightningIndexer/compression/shared-KV sparse MLA/wo` reports forward `4.31 ms`, fwd+bwd `23.22 ms`, `640` selected keys/query, and `3.70 GiB` peak; see [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_query_bwd_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_query_bwd_s4096_mi350_20260601.json). A fresh attribution run in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_query_attribution_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_query_attribution_s4096_mi350_20260601.json) measures the same boundary at `23.36 ms` fwd+bwd, with the raw shared-KV autograd slice at `17.84 ms`, output projection fwd+bwd at `3.32 ms`, and only `~2.20 ms` left for q/wkv_a/RoPE/LI/compression overhead under this decomposition. A boundary-level H64/N64 tile check is slower at `23.92 ms`, so H64/N128 remains retained. A warmed forward stage profile in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_query_stage_warm_s4096_mi350_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_shared_kv_attention_boundary_query_stage_warm_s4096_mi350_20260601.json) attributes about `1.23 ms` to LightningIndexer top-k, `1.18 ms` to shared-KV sparse MLA forward, `0.85 ms` to q projection/RoPE, `0.81 ms` to output projection, `0.26 ms` to compression/index construction, and `0.13 ms` to shared-KV projection/RoPE. This is an attention-boundary result, not the full layer: MoE, residual/RMSNorm boundaries, LI auxiliary-loss backward, and compressor backward still need integration.
- Sparse MLA backward-mode parity gate: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/compare_torchtitan_sparse_mla_modes.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/compare_torchtitan_sparse_mla_modes.py) compares two TorchTitan sparse-MLA modes with identical layer weights and input, accepts per-mode kernel modules for `fused` candidates, and can also record a small fwd+bwd timing plus peak allocated memory snapshot. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_mode_parity_s16_cpu_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_mode_parity_s16_cpu_20260601.json) validates the harness inside `onenexus/nexus-titan:rocm722-pytorch-nightly` on layer 2 at `S=16`, where `manual_stream` matches `manual_split` with max output diff `7.15e-7`, max input-grad diff `1.31e-10`, and max parameter-grad diff `8.15e-10`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_reference_backend_parity_s16_cpu_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_reference_backend_parity_s16_cpu_20260601.json) then proves `fused` plus the reference backend matches `manual_stream` exactly at `S=16`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_reference_backend_parity_s32_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_fused_reference_backend_parity_s32_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) extends that positive ABI parity gate to MI350 BF16 at `S=32`, with max output and input-gradient diff `0.0` and max parameter-gradient diff `5.96e-8`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_mode_parity_s128_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_mode_parity_s128_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) remains the larger MI350 manual-stream memory reference; at `S=128`, `manual_stream` matches `manual_split` within BF16 tolerance and lowers peak allocated memory from `14.16 GiB` to `5.11 GiB`, but is slower (`47.09 ms` versus `38.65 ms` for this single-iteration harness). Use these gates before promoting a real fused sparse MLA/LI backend.
- Sparse MLA production backend preflight: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/preflight_torchtitan_sparse_mla_backend.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/preflight_torchtitan_sparse_mla_backend.py) now requires a fused candidate to self-identify as production, backward-capable, long-sequence-capable, and selected-state-free before it can be treated as the `S=4096` path. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_reference_backend_preflight_s4096_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_reference_backend_preflight_s4096_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) records the reference backend correctly failing production preflight on MI350 while still passing the small ABI smoke under `--expect-not-promotable`; the same production-required check exits nonzero without that diagnostic flag. Layer 2 at `S=4096` would materialize `640` selected keys/query and `320.0 GiB` BF16 selected K/V if implemented naively, so the next backend must declare and demonstrate `MATERIALIZES_SELECTED_STATE=False`, `SUPPORTS_LONG_SEQUENCE=True`, and `IS_PRODUCTION_BACKEND=True`.
- Sparse MLA saved-state verifier: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/verify_torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/verify_torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state.py) uses PyTorch saved-tensor hooks to prove whether a backend saves materialized selected K/V or attention probabilities across forward/backward. The negative control [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state_manual_s16_cpu_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state_manual_s16_cpu_20260601.json) catches the old `manual` path saving two full selected K/V tensors shaped `[1,16,20,64,512]` plus probabilities `[1,64,16,20]`. The fused reference backend passes the no-selected-state gate on CPU and on MI350 BF16: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state_fused_reference_s32_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state_fused_reference_s32_mi350_bf16_20260601.json) records `selected_state_saved=false`, `row_stat=2`, `attention_activation=4`, and `selected_keys=40` at `S=32`. The Triton-forward backend also passes this gate in [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state_triton_forward_s32_mi350_bf16_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_sparse_mla_saved_state_triton_forward_s32_mi350_bf16_20260601.json): `selected_state_saved=false`, `row_stat=2`, `attention_activation=7`, `selected_keys=40`. These remain saved-state contract checks, not production fused-kernel performance claims.
- Sparse-LI S512 failure narrowing: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_sparse_li_s512_1xmi350_noac_nofsdp_noaux_noguard_failure_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_sparse_li_s512_1xmi350_noac_nofsdp_noaux_noguard_failure_20260601.json) shows the unguarded `S=512` sparse path still faults during `loss.backward()` with single-rank FSDP skipped, LI aux loss disabled, and the selected-state guard disabled. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_sparse_li_s512_layer3only_1xmi350_noac_nofsdp_noaux_failure_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_sparse_li_s512_layer3only_1xmi350_noac_nofsdp_noaux_failure_20260601.json) then forces layer 2 dense while allowing only layer 3 under the `4.5B` selected-state threshold, and still faults in `loss.backward()`. That makes the current crash a materialized sparse attention backward problem rather than Primus, multi-rank EP, activation checkpointing, FSDP post-backward, LI aux-loss gradients, or only the layer-2 `compress_ratio=4` shape.
- Manual sparse-MLA backward bridge: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s512_manual_sparse_backward_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s512_manual_sparse_backward_20260601.json) replaces the old autograd-through-materialized-selected-state backward with an explicit PyTorch backward bridge. The bridge passed remote CPU smoke, MI350 compressed-layer probes at `S=128` and `S=256`, 1xMI350 `S=512` layer-3-only sparse, 1xMI350 `S=512` all-sparse with and without FSDP, and 4x/8xMI350 all-sparse checkpoint-free steps. The no-aux 4x run logged `loss=12.35096`, `grad_norm=10.1875`, `~399-400 tok/s`, `5.31-5.32` TFLOPs/GPU, `0.23%` MFU. With LI aux loss enabled at the default coefficient, the 4x no-activation-checkpoint run logged `loss=12.15306`, `grad_norm=10.0625`, `~397-398` tok/s, and the 4x full activation-checkpoint run logged `loss=12.31200`, `grad_norm=10.4375`, `~357-358` tok/s, `148.96 GiB` memory. The 8x full activation-checkpoint run at `S=512`, `GBS=128`, `FSDP=8`, `EP=8` logged `loss=12.21498`, `grad_norm=10.0000`, `~249-250` tok/s, `3.31-3.32` TFLOPs/GPU, `0.14%` MFU, and clean process-group teardown. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s512_manual_split_sparse_backward_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s512_manual_split_sparse_backward_20260601.json) adds `TORCHTITAN_DSV4_PYTORCH_SPARSE_MLA_BACKWARD_MODE=manual_split`, which splits local-window and LI-compressed branches instead of concatenating one combined selected K/V state. Container parity against `manual` passed for output and all differentiable inputs; 1xMI350 `S=512` passed with `loss=12.23117`; 4xMI350 `S=512`, `GBS=64`, `FSDP=4`, `EP=4`, no activation checkpointing passed on visible GPUs `2,3,4,5` with `loss=12.23311`, `grad_norm=10.5000`, `75.66 GiB` memory, and `536-538` tok/s. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s512_manual_recompute_sparse_backward_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s512_manual_recompute_sparse_backward_20260601.json) adds `manual_recompute`, which saves original Q/K/V, compressed K/V, sparse indices, and masks, then recomputes selected K/V and probabilities in backward. It matched `manual_split` exactly in container parity and passed 4xMI350 `S=512`, `GBS=64`, `FSDP=4`, `EP=4`, no activation checkpointing on visible GPUs `4,5,6,7` with `loss=12.18545`, `grad_norm=10.2500`, `75.66 GiB` memory, and `529` tok/s. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s128_manual_stream_sparse_backward_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_s128_manual_stream_sparse_backward_20260601.json) adds `manual_stream`, which streams selected local and LI-compressed keys in chunks, saves row max/sum plus output, and avoids full selected K/V/probability tensors in the forward save contract. It matched `manual_split` in container parity with max output diff `2.38e-7`, and passed 1xMI350 `S=128` training on visible GPU `2` with `loss=12.19987`, `grad_norm=17.6250`, `207.14 GiB` memory, and `11` tok/s. Prefer `manual_split` for short-sequence throughput; use `manual_stream` to debug the no-full-selected-state contract while the next production fix remains a fused sparse MLA/LI kernel.
- Direct 4xMI350 training evidence: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_4xmi350_canary_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_4xmi350_canary_20260601.json). The two-step checkpointed run completed with finite loss and gradients: step 1 `loss=12.25273`, `tps~2,985-2,994` tok/GPU/s, `mfu~18.0%`; step 2 `loss=9.27922`. After deleting generated `step-1` and partial `step-3` checkpoints while preserving `step-2`, the resume run loaded `step-2` in about `16.1s`, started at step 3, logged `loss=15.53901`, `tps~1,961-1,964` tok/GPU/s, saved `checkpoint/step-3`, completed training, and destroyed process groups.
- Direct dedicated-EP and checkpoint-free evidence: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_4x_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_4x_20260601.json) shows the selected direct TorchTitan runtime reports `fsdp_group_is_ep_group=false` on all four ranks with FSDP all-reduce and EP all-to-all passing. - Direct 8xMI350 evidence: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_8x_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_8x_20260601.json) shows the direct runtime reports `fsdp_group_is_ep_group=false` on all eight ranks, with FSDP all-reduce sum `28.0` and EP all-to-all receiving `[0..7]` on each rank.
