- MORI config guard evidence: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_config_guard_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_config_guard_20260601.json) records the direct TorchTitan config parse for both `CANARY_MOE_COMM_BACKEND=standard` and `mori`. The standard path selects `AllToAllTokenDispatcher.Config`; the MORI switch selects `MoriEPTokenDispatcher.Config` but remains guarded for EP>1 until the autograd-safe MORI dispatch/combine and score-gradient path are implemented.
- MORI EP overlap reference: [`run_artifacts/mori_ep_overlap_reference_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_ep_overlap_reference_20260601.json) records the `ROCm/mori` snapshot and the current standalone 8-GPU tile-ready probe. MORI provides AMD EP dispatch/combine plus split send/recv hooks, and the remote tile-ready probe passed with `ready_wait_failures=0`, but TorchTitan training still needs an autograd-safe Mori dispatcher and a grouped-GEMM output path that writes MORI's registered combine buffer before this can replace the PyTorch all-to-all baseline.
- MORI + AITER MoE forward floor: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor.py) now measures the SGLang-style forward sequence on 8xMI350: MORI dispatch, local AITER `fused_moe`, MORI combine. The DSv4-shaped BF16 run with `4096` tokens/rank, hidden `4096`, intermediate `2048`, `256` experts, EP8, and top-k `6` reports `3.10 ms` rank-median e2e with random top-k fanout and `2.62 ms` with locality-friendly balanced top-k; see [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_dsv4_t4096_h4096_i2048_e256_top6_random_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_dsv4_t4096_h4096_i2048_e256_top6_random_20260601.json), [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_dsv4_t4096_h4096_i2048_e256_top6_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_dsv4_t4096_h4096_i2048_e256_top6_20260601.json), and the small smoke [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_smoke_t64_h1024_i128_e64_top2_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_smoke_t64_h1024_i128_e64_top2_20260601.json). The TorchTitan-to-AITER parity probe [`run_artifacts/aiter_torchtitan_moe_forward_parity_contrast_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/aiter_torchtitan_moe_forward_parity_contrast_20260601.json) identifies the valid weight contract: `w13 = cat([TorchTitan w1 gate, TorchTitan w3 up])`, AITER `shuffle_weight(layout=(16,16))` for both `w13` and `w2`, and `gate_mode="separated"`. With that valid preshuffled contract, the 8x random-top-k forward floor is still `3.109 ms` rank-median e2e in [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_dsv4_t4096_h4096_i2048_e256_top6_random_preshuffled_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_floor_dsv4_t4096_h4096_i2048_e256_top6_random_preshuffled_20260601.json). This makes the forward adapter worth porting because the current fixed-router integrated forward MoE attribution is `9.66 ms`. The autograd probe [`run_artifacts/aiter_fused_moe_autograd_smoke_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/aiter_fused_moe_autograd_smoke_20260601.json) shows AITER `fused_moe` is not training-autograd-usable as-is: PyTorch warns no autograd kernel is registered and gradients for hidden states, `w1`, `w2`, and `topk_weight` remain `None`. The new custom-autograd bridge [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_aiter_moe_forward_custom_backward.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_aiter_moe_forward_custom_backward.py) proves the local expert VJP wiring for an AITER-forward adapter: the small smoke [`run_artifacts/aiter_moe_forward_custom_backward_smoke_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/aiter_moe_forward_custom_backward_smoke_20260601.json) matches reference gradients exactly after a `0.03125` BF16 forward max diff, and the Flash-dimension smoke [`run_artifacts/aiter_moe_forward_custom_backward_flashdim_smoke_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/aiter_moe_forward_custom_backward_flashdim_smoke_20260601.json) passes at hidden `4096`, intermediate `2048`, top-k `6` with forward max diff `3.81e-6` and exact gradients. This is a training-semantics bridge only; its backward is slow PyTorch recompute, not the final fused MoE backward.
- MORI + AITER forward semantic parity: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_mori_aiter_moe_forward_parity.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_mori_aiter_moe_forward_parity.py) compares actual 8-rank MORI dispatch, local AITER fused MoE, and MORI combine against a direct TorchTitan-style global-weight reference for each rank's original tokens. The balanced smoke [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_parity_smoke_t64_h1024_i128_e64_top2_balanced_recvfix_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_parity_smoke_t64_h1024_i128_e64_top2_balanced_recvfix_20260601.json) passes all ranks with max abs diff `0.0625`, max rank mean abs diff `0.00327`, and receive counts `[64,64,64,64,64,64,64,64]`. The random-fanout smoke [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_parity_smoke_t64_h1024_i128_e64_top2_random_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_forward_parity_smoke_t64_h1024_i128_e64_top2_random_20260601.json) also passes all ranks with max abs diff `0.0625`, max rank mean abs diff `0.00311`, and uneven receive counts `[113,132,125,120,126,127,116,119]`. This upgrades the MORI/AITER evidence from speed plus finiteness to forward routing semantics; the production backward wrapper is still pending.
- EP-routed MoE backward contract: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_ep_routed_moe_backward_contract.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_ep_routed_moe_backward_contract.py) defines the training VJP target for the MORI+AITER wrapper without using MORI or AITER kernels. The 4xMI350 random-routed smoke [`run_artifacts/ep_routed_moe_backward_contract_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/ep_routed_moe_backward_contract_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260601.json) passes with `all_ranks_pass=true` and `max_abs_diff_across_ranks=0.0`, comparing full global TorchTitan-style autograd against a route-decomposed VJP for local `dX`, `dTopkWeight`, local dW contribution, and all-reduced owner-shard `dW1_gate/dW3_up/dW2_down`. This pins the backward semantics for combine backward, expert backward, and dispatch backward before replacing the current all-to-all MoE path.
- MORI + AITER autograd bridge: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_mori_aiter_moe_autograd_bridge.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_mori_aiter_moe_autograd_bridge.py) wraps the actual MORI dispatch, local AITER fused MoE, and MORI combine forward in a custom autograd shell. Backward is still a slow PyTorch reference: it all-gathers local expert shards, recomputes the global routed SwiGLU VJP for each rank's original tokens, all-reduces expert-weight gradients, and returns local owner-shard gradients. The 4xMI350 smoke [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_autograd_bridge_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_autograd_bridge_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260601.json) passes with `all_ranks_pass=true`, max forward diff `3.81e-6`, and max grad diff `0.0`. The 8xMI350 smoke [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_autograd_bridge_8x_smoke_t8_h128_i64_e32_top2_random_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_moe_autograd_bridge_8x_smoke_t8_h128_i64_e32_top2_random_20260601.json) also passes with max forward diff `1.91e-6` and max grad diff `0.0`. This proves the borrowed forward can be made training-shaped; it is not yet a fused backward performance path.
- MORI + AITER routed-backward probe: the same autograd bridge now has an opt-in `--backward-mode routed` probe that uses separate MORI handles for saved-activation routing, combine-backward `grad_output` routing, and FP32 `dTopkWeight` combine. [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_autograd_bridge_routed_aligned_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_autograd_bridge_routed_aligned_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260602.json) passes on 4xMI350 with max forward diff `3.81e-6`, max gradient diff `3.81e-6`, and `6.06 ms` rank-median fwd+bwd for the tiny probe shape. The paired reference-regression artifact [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_autograd_bridge_reference_regression_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_autograd_bridge_reference_regression_4x_smoke_t16_h128_i64_e16_top2_random_20260602.json) passes at `10.83 ms`. Two negative artifacts record important MORI API lessons: one handle cannot be reused for back-to-back dispatches without count skew, and independent handles require row alignment by `get_dispatch_src_token_pos()`. This is still a probe, not the production fused MoE backward.
- TorchTitan MORI+AITER routed-backward integration: [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/common/mori_aiter_moe.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/common/mori_aiter_moe.py) now keeps reference backward as the default and adds `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_BACKWARD_MODE=routed` for MORI-routed `grad_output`, `dX`, and `dTopkWeight` around the local owned-expert PyTorch VJP. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_backward_integrated_4x_s128_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_backward_integrated_4x_s128_20260602.json) records local `py_compile`, launcher `bash -n`, `check-source`, remote `check-config`, and three 4xMI350 train smokes on GPUs `4,5,6,7`: `S=128/GBS=4` LI-aux-off checkpoint-free, `S=128/GBS=64` LI-aux-on checkpoint-free, and the same `GBS=64` shape with full activation checkpointing. All three completed with finite loss/grad norm and clean process-group teardown. This is production-code integration movement, not performance evidence; the owned-expert VJP is still PyTorch and must be replaced by fused MoE backward kernels.
- Owned-expert VJP EP-shape backend probe: [`tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_owned_expert_vjp_ep_shape.py`](tools/dsv4_runtime_probe/probe_owned_expert_vjp_ep_shape.py) models the local owner-rank VJP behind MORI routed backward at the real 8x EP shape: `32768` source tokens, `32` local experts, `24695` local expert assignments, mean `771.7` rows/expert, and only `1.057x` local max padding. The tiny correctness smoke [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep_shape_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep_shape_smoke_20260602.json) shows AITER compact GMM/TGMM matches the padded torch VJP for `dX`, `dW1`, `dW2`, `dW3`, and `dTopk`. The full EP8-shape timing [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_shape_ptgmm_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_shape_ptgmm_20260602.json) shows padded torch remains faster than current AITER compact GMM/TGMM: `7.57 ms` full local VJP versus `10.32 ms` with `ptgmm`; [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_shape_nptgmm_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_shape_nptgmm_20260602.json) improves AITER slightly to `10.19 ms` but still loses. The detail refresh [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_shape_detail_ptgmm_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_shape_detail_ptgmm_20260602.json) keeps padded torch full VJP at `7.51 ms` and splits the local wall: forward recompute `2.79 ms`, dgrad+SwiGLU `1.78 ms`, wgrad `2.08 ms`, xgrad+reduce `1.74 ms`, with reduce-only `0.64 ms`, dTopk `0.59 ms`, and backward SwiGLU `1.18 ms`. So the owner-rank MoE gap is still local expert training math and elementwise fusion, not MORI dispatch/combine or token reduce alone. The TorchTitan bridge now exposes that padded owner-rank VJP as `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_LOCAL_VJP_MODE=padded` under routed backward; [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_padded_vjp_integrated_4x_s128_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_padded_vjp_integrated_4x_s128_20260602.json) passes 4xMI350 `S=128` train smokes for `GBS=4` LI-aux-off and `GBS=64` LI-aux-on, both checkpoint-free with finite loss/grad norm and clean process-group teardown. The next MoE backward lever is productionizing/fusing the padded owner-rank training-GEMM/SwiGLU schedule or building a CK/TileLang grouped-training-GEMM path that beats the `7.51 ms` owner-rank baseline.
- Owner-expert VJP saved-intermediate gate: [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_saved_activation_triton_swiglu_20260604.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_saved_activation_triton_swiglu_20260604.json) and [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_saved_activation_decision_20260604.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_saved_activation_decision_20260604.json) quantify the next MoE backward branch at the same EP8 owner-rank shape. Preallocating VJP buffers alone is not the lever (`6.64 ms`), and fused W13 is similar (`6.59 ms`), but saving `gate/up/hidden` drops the modeled owner VJP to `5.50 ms`, while saving `gate/up/hidden` plus compact expert output for `dTopkWeight` reaches `4.96 ms` with correctness checks passing for `dx`, `dw1`, `dw3`, `dw2`, and `dtopk`. The memory cost is `0.30 GiB` for `gate/up/hidden` or `0.49 GiB` with compact output for this owner-rank/layer shape. This promotes an opt-in TorchTitan saved-intermediate or AITER/CK training-backward adapter branch, but it is not yet an e2e TFLOPs promotion because the current AITER fused forward does not expose these tensors.
- Triton SwiGLU fusion update for the owner-rank VJP probe: [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_triton_swiglu_detail_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_triton_swiglu_detail_20260602.json) adds an opt-in `--triton-swiglu` path that keeps the padded grouped GEMM schedule but fuses SwiGLU forward/backward. Full EP8-shape parity passes for `dX`, `dW1`, `dW2`, `dW3`, and `dTopkWeight`; the full local VJP improves from `7.50 ms` to `6.43 ms`, dgrad+SwiGLU from `1.79 ms` to `0.70 ms`, backward SwiGLU from `1.19 ms` to `0.125 ms`, and forward SwiGLU from `0.247 ms` to `0.095 ms`. This is a useful Ascend-AutoFuse-style vector-fusion win, but wgrad is still about `2.24 ms`, xgrad+reduce about `1.60 ms`, and reduce-only about `0.63 ms`, so the next MoE training-backward lever remains fused/production GEMM scheduling rather than another dispatch/combine-only change.
- Saved-activation owner-rank VJP probe: [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_saved_activation_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_saved_activation_20260602.json), refreshed by [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_stage1_saved_activation_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_stage1_saved_activation_20260602.json) and the AITER API contract [`run_artifacts/aiter_fused_moe_saved_intermediate_contract_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/aiter_fused_moe_saved_intermediate_contract_20260602.json), tests whether the MoE backward gap can be closed by retaining forward expert activations instead of recomputing them under activation checkpointing. Parity passes for the retained Triton-SwiGLU VJP and saved-state variants. Same-run EP8 local VJP timing is `7.73 ms` padded torch, `6.58 ms` Triton-SwiGLU recompute, `5.39 ms` when saving ideal `gate/up/hidden` (`0.299 GiB`), and `4.77 ms` when also saving compact expert output for `dTopkWeight` (`0.487 GiB`). But the current public AITER `fused_moe` forward returns only final output; its two-stage path can expose post-SwiGLU stage1 hidden, not the `gate/up` tensors needed for backward SwiGLU. The AITER-compatible partial save is therefore much weaker: stage1 hidden alone is `6.59 ms` (`0.100 GiB`), and stage1 hidden plus unweighted compact output would be `5.86 ms` (`0.288 GiB`) if that output were exposed. This narrows the MoE ladder: either change the AITER/CK forward-backward contract to expose or recompute the right training intermediates inside a fused backward, or keep treating ideal saved activations as an upper bound while productionizing grouped wgrad/xgrad GEMM scheduling.
- Packed-W13 owner-rank VJP probe: [`run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_fused_w13_triton_swiglu_strided_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/owned_expert_vjp_ep8_fused_w13_triton_swiglu_strided_20260602.json) fixes the probe's Triton SwiGLU helper to handle the strided gate/up views created by `gate_up.split(...)`, then times a packed `w13 = cat(w1, w3)` path at the same EP8 owner-rank shape. Parity passes for `dX`, `dW1`, `dW2`, `dW3`, and `dTopkWeight`. Same-run timing is only a marginal full-VJP improvement, `6.596 ms` Triton-SwiGLU padded to `6.497 ms` fused W13, while aggregate wgrad regresses `2.023 ms` to `2.135 ms`. Do not promote packed W13 into the TorchTitan routed-backward bridge; keep it as a layout-contract probe for future CK/TileLang grouped training GEMM work.
- TorchTitan Triton SwiGLU VJP integration: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_triton_swiglu_vjp_4x_s128_smoke_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_triton_swiglu_vjp_4x_s128_smoke_20260602.json) adds the opt-in `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_LOCAL_VJP_SWIGLU_BACKEND=triton` path inside `mori_aiter_moe.py` and forwards it through the direct canary launcher as `CANARY_MORI_AITER_LOCAL_VJP_SWIGLU_BACKEND`. The default remains `torch`. A 4xMI350 `S=128`, `GBS=4`, LI-aux-off train smoke with MORI routed backward, padded owner-rank VJP, and Triton SwiGLU completed one step with finite loss `12.14935`, grad norm `12.0625`, memory `73.79 GiB`, and clean teardown across all four ranks. This proves the vector-fusion win can be carried into the production TorchTitan bridge; it is still tiny integration evidence, not long-sequence throughput.
- Triton SwiGLU VJP target-shape pass: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_triton_swiglu_vjp_4x_s4096_gbs64_acfull_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_triton_swiglu_vjp_4x_s4096_gbs64_acfull_20260602.json) promotes the earlier preflight [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_triton_swiglu_vjp_s4096_preflight_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_triton_swiglu_vjp_s4096_preflight_20260602.json) to an actual two-step normalized 4x target slice: `S=4096`, `GBS=64`, `FSDP=4`, `EP=4`, full activation checkpointing, MORI routed padded VJP, `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=32G`, and `mori_aiter_local_vjp_swiglu_backend=triton`. The run moves loss `12.14107 -> 9.05285`, reports step 1 `2,042-2,046` tok/GPU/s and step 2 `2,882` tok/GPU/s (`22.74s` structured step time), peaks at `240.70 GiB`, and destroys all process groups cleanly. This is guarded dense-fallback systems evidence, not final sparse-MLA/LI evidence, and the offline MoE-backward decision is unchanged: the earlier direct Triton xgrad+reduce and simple Triton W2-dgrad+SwiGLU probes are correct but much slower than padded torch at S4096, so the next MoE lever should be CK/TileLang-style grouped training GEMM or another MFMA-efficient owner-rank wgrad/xgrad backend.
- MORI+AITER routed padded VJP S512 extension: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_padded_vjp_s512_4x8x_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_padded_vjp_s512_4x8x_20260602.json) moves the same training-shaped bridge beyond S128. The 4xMI350 `S=512`, `GBS=64`, checkpoint-free run on GPUs `4,5,6,7` passes two steps with step 2 loss `10.94040`, grad norm `19.75`, memory `90.71-98.63 GiB`, and `1,376` tok/GPU/s (`5,504` tok/node/s). The first 8xMI350 `S=512`, `GBS=128` run failed before step 1 on MORI static SHMEM heap exhaustion; the launcher now exposes `CANARY_MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE`, and rerunning with `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=32G` passes two steps with step 2 loss `10.45562`, grad norm `19.75`, memory `51.45 GiB`, and `1,583` tok/GPU/s (`12,664` tok/node/s). This is still short-sequence, checkpoint-free evidence, but it proves EP8/FSDP8 routed+padded MORI training works once MORI heap sizing is explicit.
- MORI+AITER routed padded VJP long-sequence threshold: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_padded_vjp_longseq_threshold_4x_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_padded_vjp_longseq_threshold_4x_20260602.json) extends the same bridge with full activation checkpointing on the 4xMI350 target slice (`FSDP=4`, `EP=4`, `GBS=64`, `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=32G`). `S=1024` passes two steps with step 2 loss `9.93446`, grad norm `20.75`, memory `97.87-127.60 GiB`, and `2,934` tok/GPU/s. `S=2048` passes two steps with step 2 loss `10.14578`, grad norm `21.375`, memory `124.34-192.76 GiB`, and `4,144` tok/GPU/s. The first `S=4096` target attempt failed before the first step metric with GPU memory access faults in routed MoE backward, surfacing at `mori_aiter_moe.py:436` after `op.dispatch`; the cache-fix artifact below supersedes that initial failure.
- S4096 MORI routed-backward cache fix and 4x target pass: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_backward_op_cache_fix_s4096_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_backward_op_cache_fix_s4096_20260602.json) adds a distinct `backward_x` MORI op role and makes `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_OP_CACHE_MODE=backward` the safe default, meaning forward ops stay cached but backward ops are rebuilt per forward/backward call. The cached-backward A/B (`cache_mode=default`) fails with explicit receive-count skew (`x=21108-29161`, `grad=10595-15610`), while the safe default passes `S=4096`, `GBS=4`, two full-AC steps and the normalized 4x target slice `S=4096`, `GBS=64`, `FSDP=4`, `EP=4`, full activation checkpointing. The retained two-step target run moves loss `12.21879 -> 9.32217`, reports step 1 `2,440-2,445` tok/GPU/s and step 2 `3,226` tok/GPU/s, with memory peaking at `250.55 GiB` and two ranks reporting allocation retries. This meets the normalized 4x throughput target in the guarded systems path, but it is not final sparse-MLA/LightningIndexer evidence because compressed attention still falls back above the sparse sequence threshold and MoE backward still uses the padded PyTorch owner-rank VJP.
- MORI+AITER 8x target-shape pass: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_8x_s4096_gbs128_acfull_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_8x_s4096_gbs128_acfull_20260602.json) carries the same safe-default routed padded bridge to the intended 8x shape: `S=4096`, `GBS=128`, `FSDP=8`, `EP=8`, full activation checkpointing, checkpoint disabled, `MORI_SHMEM_HEAP_SIZE=32G`, and `TORCHTITAN_MORI_AITER_OP_CACHE_MODE=backward`. The two-step run passes with clean process-group teardown and loss movement `12.30504 -> 8.90129`. Step 1 is below target at `1,910-1,913` tok/GPU/s (`34.26-34.31s` implied step time), while step 2 exceeds the normalized target at `2,645` tok/GPU/s, `21,160` tok/node/s, and `24.78s` implied step time. Memory peaks at `248.68 GiB`, and four CUDA allocation retry warnings are recorded. This is the first 8x DeepSeek-V4 Flash MORI+AITER target-shape canary with real learned routing and loss movement; it remains guarded dense-fallback systems evidence until fused sparse MLA/LI and fused MoE backward replace the current fallbacks.
- S4096 MORI routed-backward reuse localization: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_padded_vjp_s4096_reuse_fault_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_routed_padded_vjp_s4096_reuse_fault_20260602.json) is retained as the pre-fix fault localization. It showed the standalone S4096/EP4 routed payload and a one-step TorchTitan `S=4096`, `GBS=4` full-AC run could pass, while cached repeated production use faulted on the second accumulation microstep or second train step. The follow-up artifact above narrows that to backward MORI op caching rather than raw S4096 payload size, static heap size, or activation checkpointing.
- TorchTitan MORI+AITER WIP bridge: [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/common/mori_aiter_moe.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/common/mori_aiter_moe.py) now exposes the borrowed forward behind `comm_backend=mori` plus `TORCHTITAN_EXPERIMENTAL_MORI_AITER_MOE=1`. [`sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/common/moe.py`](sources/wip/torchtitan/torchtitan/models/common/moe.py) routes `GroupedExperts` into that bridge only when the MORI dispatcher is selected and EP is wired; otherwise the guarded dispatcher still fails closed. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_bridge_wip_static_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_bridge_wip_static_20260601.json) records local `py_compile`, ROCm-container import, and direct TorchTitan `check-config` with `MoriEPTokenDispatcher.Config`, `score_before_experts=False`, `sqrtsoftplus`, and Flash-layer compress ratios `[0,0,4,128]`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_overlay_image_build_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_overlay_image_build_20260601.json) records the derived `onenexus/nexus-titan:rocm722-pytorch-nightly-mori` image, which layers MORI commit `5dd02d6815e9113381a72f6de6b22034fc09b5a3` onto the internal NexusTitan ROCm 7.2.2 TorchTitan image. [`run_artifacts/mori_aiter_autograd_bridge_overlay_4x_smoke_20260601_v2.json`](run_artifacts/mori_aiter_autograd_bridge_overlay_4x_smoke_20260601_v2.json) proves the overlay's standalone 4x bridge with max forward diff `3.81e-6` and max grad diff `0.0`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs4_noaux_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs4_noaux_20260602.json) is the first integrated TorchTitan train-step pass with MORI dispatch, AITER fused-MoE forward, MORI combine, FSDP4/EP4, `S=128`, `GBS=4`, and LI aux disabled. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs64_liaux_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs64_liaux_20260602.json) then passes the normal `GBS=64` accumulation shape with default LI aux enabled: loss `12.24433`, grad norm `9.5625`, memory `136.32 GiB`, clean process-group teardown, and no checkpoint directory. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs64_liaux_acfull_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs64_liaux_acfull_20260602.json) passes the same shape with full activation checkpointing: loss `12.25618`, grad norm `9.5`, memory `132.27 GiB`, and clean teardown. [`changesets/torchtitan_checkpoint_inactive_adam_state.md`](changesets/torchtitan_checkpoint_inactive_adam_state.md) then fixes full-state checkpoint resume for branch-inactive trainable parameters by materializing missing Adam state before save. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs64_liaux_acfull_checkpoint_resume_adamstate_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_direct_dsv4_mori_aiter_overlay_4x_s128_gbs64_liaux_acfull_checkpoint_resume_adamstate_20260602.json) proves the 4xMI350 `S=128`, `GBS=64`, full-AC MORI+AITER bridge saves a full `156G` checkpoint, resumes from it in `16.67-16.72s`, starts at step 2, completes with loss `11.86221` and grad norm `19.375`, saves `checkpoint/step-2`, and destroys process groups cleanly. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_persistent_jit_cache_20260602.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_mori_aiter_persistent_jit_cache_20260602.json) adds persistent image-keyed MORI/AITER JIT cache evidence: the warm 4x `S=128`, `GBS=4` run compiled 3 AITER modules and 2 MORI kernels, while the reuse run completed with 0 AITER build starts and 0 MORI compile lines. This is production-code integration movement, not final performance evidence; default backward remains reference recompute, the opt-in routed backward is tracked above, and cold-cache timings are still non-performance evidence.
- TorchTitan proxy runtime evidence: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_canary_runtime.yaml`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_canary_runtime.yaml). The checkpointed save/resume run completed steps 1-3 with full-state checkpoints, and the checkpoint-free `GBS=128` perf smoke reported clean-step throughput around `7.0k` tokens/GPU/s on the DeepSeek-V3 16B proxy. Treat this as distributed-systems evidence only.
- FSDP/EP process-group probe evidence: [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_4x_20260531.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_4x_20260531.json) showed the unpatched proxy runtime shared the FSDP and EP `ProcessGroup`. [`run_artifacts/torchtitan_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_4x_dedicated_ep_20260531.json`](run_artifacts/torchtitan_fsdp_ep_pg_probe_4x_dedicated_ep_20260531.json) showed the temporary proxy EP DeviceMesh patch flipped the 4x slice to `fsdp_group_is_ep_group=false`. The direct TorchTitan WIP now carries the equivalent EP backend override in `ParallelDims`.
- The issue roadmap records a H200/B200 Docker image, a 4-layer Flash smoke command, and an 8-node H200 Flash 284B full-train command. Treat these as NVIDIA reference shapes, not AMD rerun commands.
- Existing AMD Primus pretraining baselines in this repo are Qwen-family topology and runtime proofs only. This experiment now targets a direct TorchTitan 4x/8xMI350 DSv4 canary, with Primus removed from the real execution path. Remaining promotion work is replacing the guarded materializing sparse fallback with a fused sparse MLA/indexer, training-safe MORI overlap, checkpoint footprint management for additional save/resume runs, and final-path checkpoint-free throughput.

## Next Checkpoint

1. Keep future multi-MI350 raw logs, checkpoints, traces, and large outputs under `/scratch/sonle5/dsv4_pretrain_canary_20260527/`. The former `/local/data/sonle5/dsv4_pretrain_canary_20260527` payload was migrated off root storage on 2026-06-01 and replaced with a symlink to `/scratch`; see [`run_artifacts/storage_migration_scratch_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/storage_migration_scratch_20260601.json). The live follow-up check in [`run_artifacts/storage_root_cleanup_check_20260601.json`](run_artifacts/storage_root_cleanup_check_20260601.json) confirms `/` is healthy at `621G/2.0T` used and `/scratch` has `37T` free after moving `2.6G` of inactive DSv4 work dirs to `/scratch`; the remaining large root-backed HF cache is currently bind-mounted by an active SGLang container and should be migrated only during a stop/restart window.
2. Replace the manual PyTorch sparse-MLA backward bridge with the fused sparse MLA/LightningIndexer kernel. Current evidence: 4x `S=256` sparse-LI passes with nonzero LI gradients; old autograd materialized `S=512` sparse selected-state backward faults; the `manual` bridge makes all-sparse `S=512` pass on 1x, 4x, and 8xMI350 with LI aux loss and full activation checkpointing; the newer `manual_split` bridge removes the combined selected-K/V cat and improves short-sequence 4x no-AC memory/throughput; the diagnostic `manual_recompute` bridge proves saved-state-only recompute does not reduce the observed S512 peak; the diagnostic `manual_stream` bridge validates row-stats/output saved-state semantics without full selected K/V/prob saves but is far too slow as PyTorch. The next attention lever is replacing the Python streaming loops with a fused sparse MLA/LI kernel. The default selected-state guard remains useful for stable dense-fallback systems runs.
3. Replace the bounded TorchTitan PyTorch sparse MLA/indexer fallback with the DSv4 fused sparse MLA/LightningIndexer kernel path so compressed layers can run at target `GBS=64/128` and `S=4096` without materializing selected-KV tensors. The current shared-KV + LI Triton path now passes one-GPU layer smokes, a 4x `GBS=4` integration step, safe-auto two-step 4x `GBS=64`, and safe-auto two-step 8x `GBS=128` target-shape runs after making Triton atomic dKV scatter opt-in. It remains prototype backward evidence, not final performance; the next attention lever is hardening/fusing the dKV scatter path rather than restoring unsafe atomic scatter as default.
4. Replace the current PyTorch all-to-all EP path with a training-safe MORI overlap path: the WIP now has a guarded TorchTitan entrypoint for MORI dispatch, AITER fused-MoE forward, and MORI combine under `TORCHTITAN_EXPERIMENTAL_MORI_AITER_MOE=1`, following the measured SGLang-style `3.10 ms` random-top-k floor. The integrated 4x TorchTitan bridge now passes `S=128`, `GBS=64`, default LI aux, full activation checkpointing, full-state checkpoint/resume with reference backward, image-keyed persistent MORI/AITER JIT cache reuse, and sparse shared-KV `S=4096`, `GBS=64` two-step training with the safe scatter default. The retained standard-EP top-8 wait-split profile now shows combine-side `dX` return wait (`256.20 ms` rank-max) separately from real weighted scatter (`178.17 ms`), so the remaining MoE step is replacing the padded owner-rank PyTorch VJP with fused/batched helper-owner backward and MORI-native backward routing/overlap, not a scatter-only wrapper.
5. Run and profile `flash_12layer_ceiling_probe` at `S=4096`, `GBS=128`, MBS tuned, `TP=PP=CP=1`, `FSDP=4`, `EP=4`, AdamW, and the first-12-layer recipe compress-ratio mix `(1,1,4,128,4,128,4,128,4,128,4,128)`, encoded locally as `[0,0,4,128,4,128,4,128,4,128,4,128]`. Promotion requires late-step or multi-step averages for tok/GPU/s, node tok/s, TFLOPs/GPU under that model accounting, peak memory, and a profile-ranked MoE/MORI plus sparse-MLA bottleneck breakdown.
6. Keep the AdamW optimizer path checkpointable and distributed-safe; revisit mixed Muon/AdamW after the canary is stable.
